ParetoSlider: Diffusion Models Post-Training for Continuous Reward Control
Authors: Shelly Golan, Michael Finkelson, Ariel Bereslavsky, Yotam Nitzan, Or Patashnik
First: 2026-04-22T17:44:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T17:44:56+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://shelley-golan.github.io/ParetoSlider-webpage/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) post-training has become the standard for aligning generative models with human preferences, yet most methods rely on a single scalar reward. When multiple criteria matter, the prevailing practice of ``early scalarization'' collapses rewards into a fixed weighted sum. This commits the model to a single trade-off point at training time, providing no inference-time control over inherently conflicting goals -- such as prompt adherence versus source fidelity in image editing. We introduce ParetoSlider, a multi-objective RL (MORL) framework that trains a single diffusion model to approximate the entire Pareto front. By training the model with continuously varying preference weights as a conditioning signal, we enable users to navigate optimal trade-offs at inference time without retraining or maintaining multiple checkpoints. We evaluate ParetoSlider across three state-of-the-art flow-matching backbones: SD3.5, FluxKontext, and LTX-2. Our single preference-conditioned model matches or exceeds the performance of baselines trained separately for fixed reward trade-offs, while uniquely providing fine-grained control over competing generative goals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ParetoSlider：扩散模型后训练实现连续奖励控制
强化学习后训练已成为将生成模型与人类偏好对齐的标准方法，但大多数方法依赖于单一标量奖励。当多个标准至关重要时，常见的“早期标量化”做法会将奖励合并为固定的加权和。这使模型在训练时承诺单一权衡点，无法在推理时控制固有冲突的目标——例如图像编辑中的提示遵循度与源保真度。我们提出ParetoSlider，一种多目标强化学习框架，通过训练单个扩散模型来近似整个帕累托前沿。通过将连续变化的偏好权重作为条件信号训练模型，用户无需重新训练或维护多个检查点，即可在推理时导航最优权衡。我们在三个最先进的流匹配骨干网络（SD3.5、FluxKontext和LTX-2）上评估了ParetoSlider。我们单一的偏好条件模型在固定奖励权衡的基线上达到或超越其性能，同时独特地提供了对竞争性生成目标的精细控制。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces ParetoSlider, a multi-objective reinforcement learning framework designed to address the limitation of traditional RL post-training that collapses multiple criteria into a single fixed reward, thereby lacking inference-time control over conflicting goals like prompt adherence versus source fidelity in image editing. The method trains a single diffusion model with continuously varying preference weights as a conditioning signal, enabling it to approximate the entire Pareto front and allowing users to navigate optimal trade-offs at inference without retraining. Evaluated on three state-of-the-art flow-matching backbones—SD3.5, FluxKontext, and LTX-2—the single preference-conditioned model matches or exceeds baselines trained separately for fixed trade-offs while uniquely offering fine-grained control over competing generative objectives.
该论文提出了ParetoSlider，一个多目标强化学习框架，旨在解决传统RL后训练将多个标准压缩为单一固定奖励、从而在推理时无法控制冲突目标（如图像编辑中的提示遵循度与源保真度）的局限。该方法通过将连续变化的偏好权重作为条件信号训练单个扩散模型，使其逼近整个帕累托前沿，用户无需重新训练或维护多个检查点即可在推理时导航最优权衡。在SD3.5、FluxKontext和LTX-2三个最先进的流匹配骨干网络上的评估表明，该单一偏好条件模型在性能上匹配或超过为固定权衡单独训练的基线，同时独特地提供了对竞争性生成目标的细粒度控制。
Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yunke Ao, Le Chen, Bruce D. Lee, Assefa S. Wahd, Aline Czarnobai, Philipp Fürnstahl, Bernhard Schölkopf, Andreas Krause
First: 2026-04-20T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T17:00:06+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures; Project page and code available at https://bounded-ratio-rl.github.io/brrl/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has become the predominant algorithm for on-policy reinforcement learning due to its scalability and empirical robustness across domains. However, there is a significant disconnect between the underlying foundations of trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in PPO. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. We formulate a novel regularized and constrained policy optimization problem and derive its analytical optimal solution. We prove that this solution ensures monotonic performance improvement. To handle parameterized policy classes, we develop a policy optimization algorithm called Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) that minimizes an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and the analytic optimal solution from BRRL. We further establish a lower bound on the expected performance of the resulting policy in terms of the BPO loss function. Notably, our framework also provides a new theoretical lens to interpret the success of the PPO loss, and connects trust region policy optimization and the Cross-Entropy Method (CEM). We additionally extend BPO to Group-relative BPO (GBPO) for LLM fine-tuning. Empirical evaluations of BPO across MuJoCo, Atari, and complex IsaacLab environments (e.g., Humanoid locomotion), and of GBPO for LLM fine-tuning tasks, demonstrate that BPO and GBPO generally match or outperform PPO and GRPO in stability and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有界比率强化学习
近端策略优化（PPO）因其跨领域的可扩展性和经验鲁棒性，已成为在线策略强化学习的主流算法。然而，信任区域方法的基本原理与PPO中使用的启发式裁剪目标之间存在显著脱节。本文通过引入有界比率强化学习（BRRL）框架来弥合这一差距。我们提出了一种新颖的正则化且受约束的策略优化问题，并推导出其解析最优解。我们证明该解能确保单调性能提升。为了处理参数化策略类，我们开发了一种名为有界策略优化（BPO）的策略优化算法，该算法最小化策略与BRRL解析最优解之间的优势加权散度。我们进一步建立了所得策略期望性能的下界，该下界以BPO损失函数表示。值得注意的是，我们的框架还为解释PPO损失的成功提供了新的理论视角，并连接了信任区域策略优化和交叉熵方法（CEM）。此外，我们将BPO扩展为面向LLM微调的组相对BPO（GBPO）。在MuJoCo、Atari和复杂IsaacLab环境（如人形机器人运动）中对BPO进行的经验评估，以及在LLM微调任务中对GBPO进行的评估表明，BPO和GBPO在稳定性和最终性能上通常匹配或优于PPO和GRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework to address the theoretical gap between trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective in Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). The authors formulate a regularized and constrained policy optimization problem, derive its analytical optimal solution with proven monotonic performance improvement, and develop the Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) algorithm that minimizes an advantage-weighted divergence from this solution. Empirical results across MuJoCo, Atari, and IsaacLab environments, along with a Group-relative BPO (GBPO) extension for LLM fine-tuning, show that BPO and GBPO generally match or outperform PPO and GRPO in stability and final performance.
该论文提出了有界比率强化学习（BRRL）框架，以弥合信任区域方法与PPO中启发式裁剪目标之间的理论差距。作者构建了一个正则化且带约束的策略优化问题，推导出其解析最优解并证明了单调性能改进，进而开发了有界策略优化（BPO）算法，该算法最小化策略与BRRL解析最优解之间的优势加权散度。在MuJoCo、Atari和IsaacLab环境中的实证结果，以及针对大语言模型微调的组相对BPO（GBPO）扩展表明，BPO和GBPO在稳定性和最终性能上通常达到或超过PPO和GRPO。
V-tableR1: Process-Supervised Multimodal Table Reasoning with Critic-Guided Policy Optimization
Authors: Yubo Jiang, Yitong An, Xin Yang, Abudukelimu Wuerkaixi, Xuxin Cheng, Fengying Xie, Zhiguo Jiang, Cao Liu, Ke Zeng, Haopeng Zhang
First: 2026-04-22T16:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T16:44:33+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 4 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce V-tableR1, a process-supervised reinforcement learning framework that elicits rigorous, verifiable reasoning from multimodal large language models (MLLMs). Current MLLMs trained solely on final outcomes often treat visual reasoning as a black box, relying on superficial pattern matching rather than performing rigorous multi-step inference. While Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards could enforce transparent reasoning trajectories, extending it to visual domains remains severely hindered by the ambiguity of grounding abstract logic into continuous pixel space. We solve this by leveraging the deterministic grid structure of tables as an ideal visual testbed. V-tableR1 employs a specialized critic VLM to provide dense, step-level feedback on the explicit visual chain-of-thought generated by a policy VLM. To optimize this system, we propose Process-Guided Direct Alignment Policy Optimization (PGPO), a novel RL algorithm integrating process rewards, decoupled policy constraints, and length-aware dynamic sampling. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that V-tableR1 explicitly penalizes visual hallucinations and shortcut guessing. By fundamentally shifting multimodal inference from black-box pattern matching to verifiable logical derivation, V-tableR1 4B establishes state-of-the-art accuracy among open-source models on complex tabular benchmarks, outperforming models up to 18x its size and improving over its SFT baseline
中文标题/摘要
标题：V-tableR1：基于过程监督的多模态表格推理与评论引导策略优化
我们提出V-tableR1，一种过程监督的强化学习框架，能够从多模态大语言模型中激发严谨、可验证的推理能力。当前仅基于最终结果训练的多模态大语言模型往往将视觉推理视为黑箱，依赖浅层模式匹配而非执行严谨的多步推理。尽管可验证奖励的强化学习能够强制透明推理轨迹，但将其扩展到视觉领域仍因抽象逻辑在连续像素空间中的模糊性而严重受阻。我们通过利用表格的确定性网格结构作为理想视觉测试平台来解决这一问题。V-tableR1采用专门的评论视觉语言模型，为策略视觉语言模型生成的显式视觉思维链提供密集的步骤级反馈。为优化该系统，我们提出过程引导直接对齐策略优化，一种融合过程奖励、解耦策略约束和长度感知动态采样的新型强化学习算法。大量评估表明，V-tableR1明确惩罚视觉幻觉和捷径猜测。通过从根本上将多模态推理从黑箱模式匹配转变为可验证的逻辑推导，V-tableR1 4B在复杂表格基准测试中建立了开源模型的最先进准确率，性能超越其18倍大小的模型，并优于其监督微调基线。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces V-tableR1, a process-supervised reinforcement learning framework designed to improve multimodal table reasoning in large language models. The motivation stems from the observation that current models rely on superficial pattern matching rather than rigorous multi-step inference, as they are trained only on final outcomes. To address this, V-tableR1 uses a critic VLM to provide step-level feedback on the visual chain-of-thought generated by a policy VLM, leveraging the deterministic grid structure of tables. The method incorporates a novel algorithm, Process-Guided Direct Alignment Policy Optimization (PGPO), which integrates process rewards, decoupled policy constraints, and length-aware dynamic sampling. Experimental results show that V-tableR1 explicitly penalizes visual hallucinations and shortcut guessing, achieving state-of-the-art accuracy among open-source models on complex tabular benchmarks, outperforming models up to 18 times its size and improving over its SFT baseline.
该论文介绍了V-tableR1，一个过程监督的强化学习框架，旨在提升多模态大语言模型在表格推理中的表现。其动机在于当前模型仅基于最终结果训练，依赖浅层模式匹配而非严谨的多步推理。为解决此问题，V-tableR1利用表格的确定性网格结构，通过一个批评者视觉语言模型对策略视觉语言模型生成的显式视觉思维链提供密集的步骤级反馈。方法中提出了新型算法PGPO，整合了过程奖励、解耦策略约束和长度感知动态采样。实验结果表明，V-tableR1明确惩罚了视觉幻觉和捷径猜测，在复杂表格基准测试中达到了开源模型的最先进准确率，超越了体积大18倍的模型，并优于其监督微调基线。
Semantic Interaction Information mediates compositional generalization in latent space
Authors: John Schwarcz
First: 2026-03-28T04:46:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T16:36:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Are there still barriers to generalization once all relevant variables are known? We address this question via a framework that casts compositional generalization as a variational inference problem over latent variables with parametric interactions. To explore this, we develop the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) where observations are generated jointly by multiple latent variables, yet feedback is provided for only a single goal variable. This setting allows us to define Semantic Interaction Information (SII): a metric measuring the contribution of latent variable interactions to task performance. Using SII, we analyze Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs) provided with these interactions, finding that SII explains the accuracy gap between Echo State and Fully Trained networks. Our analysis also uncovers a theoretically predicted failure mode where confidence decouples from accuracy, suggesting that utilizing interactions between relevant variables is a non-trivial capability. We then address a harder regime where the interactions must be learned by an embedding model. Learning how latent variables interact requires accurate inference, yet accurate inference depends on knowing those interactions. The Cognitive Gridworld reveals this circular dependence as a core challenge for continual meta-learning. We approach this dilemma via Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), a JEPA-style architecture that disentangles these processes: variable inference and variable embeddings are learned by separate modules through Reinforcement Learning and self-supervised learning, respectively. Lastly, we demonstrate that RCCs facilitate compositional generalization to novel combinations of relevant variables. Together, these results establish a grounded setting for evaluating goal-directed generalist agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语义交互信息介导潜在空间中的组合泛化
一旦所有相关变量已知，泛化是否仍存在障碍？我们通过一个框架来探讨这一问题，该框架将组合泛化视为一个关于具有参数交互的潜在变量的变分推断问题。为此，我们开发了认知网格世界（Cognitive Gridworld），这是一个静态的部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），其中观测由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单个目标变量提供。这种设置使我们能够定义语义交互信息（SII）：一种衡量潜在变量交互对任务性能贡献的指标。利用SII，我们分析了提供这些交互的循环神经网络（RNN），发现SII解释了回声状态网络与完全训练网络之间的准确率差距。我们的分析还揭示了一种理论上预测的失败模式，即置信度与准确率脱钩，这表明利用相关变量之间的交互是一种非平凡的能力。 随后，我们处理了一个更困难的场景，其中交互必须由嵌入模型学习。学习潜在变量如何交互需要准确的推断，而准确的推断又依赖于了解这些交互。认知网格世界揭示了这种循环依赖是持续元学习的核心挑战。我们通过表示分类链（RCCs）来解决这一困境，这是一种JEPA风格的架构，它将这些过程解耦：变量推断和变量嵌入分别通过强化学习和自监督学习由不同模块学习。最后，我们证明了RCCs能够促进对相关变量新组合的组合泛化。这些结果共同为评估目标导向的通用智能体建立了一个基础性场景。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether compositional generalization remains challenging even when all relevant variables are known, proposing a framework that treats it as variational inference over latent variables with parametric interactions. To study this, the authors introduce the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary POMDP where observations are generated by multiple latent variables but feedback is given only for a single goal variable, and define Semantic Interaction Information (SII) to measure the contribution of latent variable interactions to task performance. Experiments with Recurrent Neural Networks show that SII explains the accuracy gap between Echo State and Fully Trained networks, and reveal a failure mode where confidence decouples from accuracy, indicating that utilizing variable interactions is non-trivial. To address the harder regime where interactions must be learned, the authors propose Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), a JEPA-style architecture that separates variable inference and embedding learning via Reinforcement Learning and self-supervised learning, demonstrating that RCCs enable compositional generalization to novel combinations of relevant variables.
该论文探讨了即使所有相关变量已知，组合泛化是否仍然存在障碍，提出了一个将组合泛化视为潜在变量参数化交互的变分推理框架。为此，作者设计了认知网格世界，一个静态的部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，其中观测由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单一目标变量，并定义了语义交互信息来量化潜在变量交互对任务性能的贡献。使用循环神经网络的实验表明，语义交互信息解释了回声状态网络与全训练网络之间的准确率差距，并揭示了一种置信度与准确率脱节的失败模式，表明利用变量交互是一项非平凡的能力。针对需要学习交互的更难场景，作者提出了表示分类链，一种基于JEPA的架构，通过强化学习和自监督学习分别解耦变量推理和嵌入学习，实验证明表示分类链能够促进对相关变量新组合的组合泛化。
Near-Future Policy Optimization
Authors: Chuanyu Qin, Chenxu Yang, Qingyi Si, Naibin Gu, Dingyu Yao, Zheng Lin, Peng Fu, Nan Duan, Jiaqi Wang
First: 2026-04-22T16:20:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T16:20:41+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a core post-training recipe. Introducing suitable off-policy trajectories into on-policy exploration accelerates RLVR convergence and raises the performance ceiling, yet finding a source of such trajectories remains the key challenge. Existing mixed-policy methods either import trajectories from external teachers (high-quality but distributionally far) or replay past training trajectories (close but capped in quality), and neither simultaneously satisfies the strong enough (higher $Q$ , more new knowledge to learn) and close enough (lower $V$ , more readily absorbed) conditions required to maximize the effective learning signal $\mathcal{S} = Q/V$. We propose \textbf{N}ear-Future \textbf{P}olicy \textbf{O}ptimization (\textbf{NPO}), a simple mixed-policy scheme that learns from a policy's own near-future self: a later checkpoint from the same training run is a natural source of auxiliary trajectories that is both stronger than the current policy and closer than any external source, directly balancing trajectory quality against variance cost. We validate NPO through two manual interventions, early-stage bootstrapping and late-stage plateau breakthrough, and further propose \textbf{AutoNPO},an adaptive variant that automatically triggers interventions from online training signals and selects the guide checkpoint that maximizes $S$. On Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct with GRPO, NPO improves average performance from 57.88 to 62.84, and AutoNPO pushes it to 63.15, raising the final performance ceiling while accelerating convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：近未来策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为核心的后训练方法。将合适的离策略轨迹引入在策略探索中，可加速RLVR收敛并提升性能上限，但寻找此类轨迹的来源仍是关键挑战。现有的混合策略方法要么从外部教师导入轨迹（质量高但分布差异大），要么重放过去的训练轨迹（分布接近但质量受限），两者均无法同时满足最大化有效学习信号S = Q/V所需的足够强（更高的Q，更多可学习的新知识）和足够接近（更低的V，更易吸收）的条件。我们提出近未来策略优化（NPO），一种简单的混合策略方案，从策略自身的近未来自我中学习：同一训练过程中较晚的检查点是一种自然的辅助轨迹来源，它既比当前策略更强，又比任何外部来源更接近，直接平衡了轨迹质量与方差成本。我们通过两种人工干预（早期启动引导和后期平台期突破）验证了NPO，并进一步提出AutoNPO，一种自适应变体，可从在线训练信号中自动触发干预，并选择最大化S的引导检查点。在基于GRPO的Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct上，NPO将平均性能从57.88提升至62.84，AutoNPO进一步将其推至63.15，在加速收敛的同时提高了最终性能上限。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of accelerating reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) by introducing suitable off-policy trajectories into on-policy exploration, where existing mixed-policy methods fail to balance trajectory quality and distributional closeness. The authors propose Near-Future Policy Optimization (NPO), a simple scheme that uses a later checkpoint from the same training run as a source of auxiliary trajectories, which is both stronger than the current policy and closer than any external source, maximizing the effective learning signal S = Q/V. They also introduce AutoNPO, an adaptive variant that automatically triggers interventions based on online training signals. Experiments on Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct with GRPO show that NPO improves average performance from 57.88 to 62.84, and AutoNPO further pushes it to 63.15, raising the final performance ceiling while accelerating convergence.
该论文针对在基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）中，通过引入合适的离策略轨迹来加速在线策略探索的挑战，指出现有的混合策略方法无法同时满足轨迹质量和分布接近性的要求。作者提出了近未来策略优化（NPO），一种简单的混合策略方案，利用同一训练过程中较晚的检查点作为辅助轨迹来源，该轨迹既比当前策略更强，又比任何外部来源更接近，从而最大化有效学习信号 S = Q/V。他们还提出了自适应变体 AutoNPO，可根据在线训练信号自动触发干预。在 Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct 模型上使用 GRPO 的实验表明，NPO 将平均性能从 57.88 提升至 62.84，而 AutoNPO 进一步将其提升至 63.15，在提高最终性能上限的同时加速了收敛。
Cyber Defense Benchmark: Agentic Threat Hunting Evaluation for LLMs in SecOps
Authors: Alankrit Chona, Igor Kozlov, Ambuj Kumar
First: 2026-04-21T14:53:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T16:03:07+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 3 figures, 5 tables. Complete benchmark and hunt traces available on request
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce the Cyber Defense Benchmark, a benchmark for measuring how well large language model (LLM) agents perform the core SOC analyst task of threat hunting: given a database of raw Windows event logs with no guided questions or hints, identify the exact timestamps of malicious events. The benchmark wraps 106 real attack procedures from the OTRF Security-Datasets corpus - spanning 86 MITRE ATT&CK sub-techniques across 12 tactics - into a Gymnasium reinforcement-learning environment. Each episode presents the agent with an in-memory SQLite database of 75,000-135,000 log records produced by a deterministic campaign simulator that time-shifts and entity-obfuscates the raw recordings. The agent must iteratively submit SQL queries to discover malicious event timestamps and explicitly flag them, scored CTF-style against Sigma-rule-derived ground truth. Evaluating five frontier models - Claude Opus 4.6, GPT-5, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Kimi K2.5, and Gemini 3 Flash - on 26 campaigns covering 105 of 106 procedures, we find that all models fail dramatically: the best model (Claude Opus 4.6) submits correct flags for only 3.8% of malicious events on average, and no run across any model ever finds all flags. We define a passing score as >= 50% recall on every ATT&CK tactic - the minimum bar for unsupervised SOC deployment. No model passes: the leader clears this bar on 5 of 13 tactics and the remaining four on zero. These results suggest that current LLMs are poorly suited for open-ended, evidence-driven threat hunting despite strong performance on curated Q&A security benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：网络防御基准：面向安全运营中心的大语言模型代理威胁狩猎评估
我们提出网络防御基准，用于衡量大语言模型代理在执行核心SOC分析师任务——威胁狩猎时的表现：给定一个包含原始Windows事件日志的数据库，无引导问题或提示，需识别恶意事件的确切时间戳。该基准将OTRF安全数据集语料库中的106个真实攻击流程（涵盖MITRE ATT&CK中12种战术下的86种子技术）封装为Gymnasium强化学习环境。每个回合向代理提供一个内存SQLite数据库，包含75,000-135,000条日志记录，由确定性战役模拟器生成，对原始记录进行时间偏移和实体混淆。代理需迭代提交SQL查询以发现恶意事件时间戳并明确标记，按CTF风格根据Sigma规则导出的真实结果评分。评估五个前沿模型（Claude Opus 4.6、GPT-5、Gemini 3.1 Pro、Kimi K2.5和Gemini 3 Flash）在覆盖105/106个流程的26个战役上的表现，我们发现所有模型均表现糟糕：最佳模型（Claude Opus 4.6）平均仅正确标记3.8%的恶意事件，且任何模型的任何运行均未找到所有标记。我们将通过分数定义为每个ATT&CK战术的召回率≥50%——无监督SOC部署的最低门槛。无模型通过：领先者在13个战术中的5个上达到此门槛，其余四个模型在零个战术上达标。这些结果表明，尽管在精心策划的问答安全基准上表现强劲，当前大语言模型仍不适合开放式、证据驱动的威胁狩猎。

MGDA-Decoupled: Geometry-Aware Multi-Objective Optimisation for DPO-based LLM Alignment
Authors: Andor Vári-Kakas, Ji Won Park, Natasa Tagasovska
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-22T15:33:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T15:33:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the Algorithmic Fairness Across Alignment Procedures and Agentic Systems Workshop at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) to desirable human values requires balancing multiple, potentially conflicting objectives such as helpfulness, truthfulness, and harmlessness, which presents a multi-objective optimisation challenge. Most alignment pipelines rely on a fixed scalarisation of these objectives, which can introduce procedural unfairness by systematically under-weighting harder-to-optimise or minority objectives. To promote more equitable trade-offs, we introduce MGDA-Decoupled, a geometry-based multi-objective optimisation algorithm that finds a shared descent direction while explicitly accounting for each objective's convergence dynamics. In contrast to prior methods that depend on reinforcement learning (e.g., GAPO) or explicit reward models (e.g., MODPO), our approach operates entirely within the lightweight Direct Preference Optimisation (DPO) paradigm. Experiments on the UltraFeedback dataset show that geometry-aware methods -- and MGDA-Decoupled in particular -- achieve the highest win rates against golden responses, both overall and per objective.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MGDA-Decoupled：基于几何感知的多目标优化方法用于DPO大语言模型对齐
将大语言模型与理想的人类价值观对齐需要在多个可能相互冲突的目标（如有用性、真实性和无害性）之间取得平衡，这构成了一个多目标优化挑战。大多数对齐流程依赖这些目标的固定标量化，可能通过系统性地低估较难优化或少数目标而引入程序不公平性。为促进更公平的权衡，我们提出MGDA-Decoupled，一种基于几何的多目标优化算法，在明确考虑每个目标收敛动态的同时寻找共享下降方向。与依赖强化学习（如GAPO）或显式奖励模型（如MODPO）的先前方法不同，我们的方法完全在轻量级直接偏好优化（DPO）范式内运行。在UltraFeedback数据集上的实验表明，几何感知方法——尤其是MGDA-Decoupled——在整体和每个目标上均实现了对黄金响应的最高胜率。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning large language models (LLMs) with multiple conflicting human values, such as helpfulness and harmlessness, where traditional fixed scalarisation methods introduce procedural unfairness by under-weighting harder objectives. To solve this, the authors propose MGDA-Decoupled, a geometry-aware multi-objective optimisation algorithm that operates within the Direct Preference Optimisation (DPO) paradigm, finding a shared descent direction while accounting for each objective's convergence dynamics without requiring reinforcement learning or explicit reward models. Experiments on the UltraFeedback dataset demonstrate that MGDA-Decoupled achieves the highest win rates against golden responses, both overall and per objective, outperforming prior methods like GAPO and MODPO.
该论文针对大语言模型（LLM）对齐中多个冲突的人类价值观（如有用性和无害性）的挑战，指出传统固定标量化方法因系统性低估难以优化或少数目标而引入程序不公平性。为此，作者提出MGDA-Decoupled，一种基于几何的多目标优化算法，在轻量级直接偏好优化（DPO）范式内运作，通过考虑每个目标的收敛动态来寻找共享下降方向，无需依赖强化学习或显式奖励模型。在UltraFeedback数据集上的实验表明，MGDA-Decoupled在整体和每个目标上均取得了对黄金响应的最高胜率，优于GAPO和MODPO等先前方法。
GRPO-VPS: Enhancing Group Relative Policy Optimization with Verifiable Process Supervision for Effective Reasoning
Authors: Jingyi Wang, Lei Zhu, Tengjin Weng, Song-Li Wu, Haochen Tan, Jierun Chen, Chaofan Tao, Haoli Bai, Lu Hou, Lifeng Shang, Xiao-Ping Zhang
First: 2026-04-22T15:08:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T15:08:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has advanced the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) by leveraging direct outcome verification instead of learned reward models. Building on this paradigm, Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) eliminates the need for critic models but suffers from indiscriminate credit assignment for intermediate steps, which limits its ability to identify effective reasoning strategies and incurs overthinking. In this work, we introduce a model-free and verifiable process supervision via probing the model's belief in the correct answer throughout its reasoning trajectory. By segmenting the generation into discrete steps and tracking the conditional probability of the correct answer appended at each segment boundary, we efficiently compute interpretable segment-wise progress measurements to refine GRPO's trajectory-level feedback. This approach enables more targeted and sample-efficient policy updates, while avoiding the need for intermediate supervision derived from costly Monte Carlo rollouts or auxiliary models. Experiments on mathematical and general-domain benchmarks show consistent gains over GRPO across diverse models: up to 2.6-point accuracy improvements and 13.7% reasoning-length reductions on math tasks, and up to 2.4 points and 4% on general-domain tasks, demonstrating strong generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GRPO-VPS：通过可验证过程监督增强组相对策略优化以实现有效推理
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通过利用直接结果验证而非学习奖励模型，提升了大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力。在此范式基础上，组相对策略优化（GRPO）消除了对评论家模型的需求，但存在对中间步骤的盲目信用分配问题，这限制了其识别有效推理策略的能力并导致过度思考。在本工作中，我们通过探测模型在推理轨迹中对正确答案的信念，引入了一种无模型且可验证的过程监督方法。通过将生成过程分割为离散步骤，并追踪每个分割边界处附加正确答案的条件概率，我们高效计算了可解释的逐段进度度量，以优化GRPO的轨迹级反馈。该方法实现了更具针对性和样本高效的策略更新，同时避免了从昂贵的蒙特卡洛展开或辅助模型中获取中间监督的需求。在数学和通用领域基准测试上的实验表明，与GRPO相比，该方法在不同模型上均取得了一致提升：数学任务上准确率提升高达2.6个百分点，推理长度减少13.7%；通用领域任务上准确率提升高达2.4个百分点，推理长度减少4%，展现了强大的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) in reinforcement learning for large language models, which suffers from indiscriminate credit assignment for intermediate reasoning steps, leading to overthinking and ineffective strategy identification. The authors propose GRPO-VPS, a method that introduces model-free and verifiable process supervision by probing the model's belief in the correct answer throughout its reasoning trajectory, segmenting generation into discrete steps and tracking conditional probabilities to compute segment-wise progress measurements. Experiments on mathematical and general-domain benchmarks show consistent improvements over GRPO, with up to 2.6-point accuracy gains and 13.7% reduction in reasoning length on math tasks, and up to 2.4 points and 4% on general-domain tasks, demonstrating strong generalization without requiring costly Monte Carlo rollouts or auxiliary models.
该论文针对组相对策略优化（GRPO）在大型语言模型强化学习中存在的中间步骤信用分配不明确、导致过度思考及策略识别效率低下的问题，提出了一种名为GRPO-VPS的方法。该方法通过在整个推理轨迹中探测模型对正确答案的信念，将生成过程分割为离散步骤并追踪各步骤边界处正确答案的条件概率，从而计算可解释的逐段进度度量，以优化GRPO的轨迹级反馈。在数学和通用领域基准上的实验表明，该方法相比GRPO持续提升性能：数学任务上准确率最高提升2.6个百分点，推理长度减少13.7%；通用领域任务上准确率提升2.4个百分点，推理长度减少4%，且无需昂贵的蒙特卡洛展开或辅助模型，展现了强大的泛化能力。
Occupancy Reward Shaping: Improving Credit Assignment for Offline Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Aravind Venugopal, Jiayu Chen, Xudong Wu, Chongyi Zheng, Benjamin Eysenbach, Jeff Schneider
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-22T14:41:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T14:41:56+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
The temporal lag between actions and their long-term consequences makes credit assignment a challenge when learning goal-directed behaviors from data. Generative world models capture the distribution of future states an agent may visit, indicating that they have captured temporal information. How can that temporal information be extracted to perform credit assignment? In this paper, we formalize how the temporal information stored in world models encodes the underlying geometry of the world. Leveraging optimal transport, we extract this geometry from a learned model of the occupancy measure into a reward function that captures goal-reaching information. Our resulting method, Occupancy Reward Shaping, largely mitigates the problem of credit assignment in sparse reward settings. ORS provably does not alter the optimal policy, yet empirically improves performance by 2.2x across 13 diverse long-horizon locomotion and manipulation tasks. Moreover, we demonstrate the effectiveness of ORS in the real world for controlling nuclear fusion on 3 Tokamak control tasks. Code: https://github.com/aravindvenu7/occupancy_reward_shaping; Website: https://aravindvenu7.github.io/website/ors/
中文标题/摘要
标题：占用奖励塑形：改进离线目标条件强化学习中的信用分配
动作与其长期后果之间的时间滞后使得从数据中学习目标导向行为时，信用分配成为一项挑战。生成式世界模型捕捉了智能体可能访问的未来状态分布，表明它们已捕获时间信息。如何提取这些时间信息以进行信用分配？在本文中，我们形式化了世界模型中存储的时间信息如何编码世界的底层几何结构。利用最优传输，我们从学习到的占用度量模型中提取这种几何结构，转化为捕捉目标到达信息的奖励函数。由此产生的方法——占用奖励塑形，在很大程度上缓解了稀疏奖励设置中的信用分配问题。ORS可证明不改变最优策略，但在13个不同的长时程运动与操作任务中，经验上性能提升了2.2倍。此外，我们在3个托卡马克控制任务上展示了ORS在现实世界中控制核聚变的有效性。 代码：https://github.com/aravindvenu7/occupancy_reward_shaping；网站：https://aravindvenu7.github.io/website/ors/
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the credit assignment problem in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning, where actions and their long-term consequences are temporally separated. The authors propose Occupancy Reward Shaping (ORS), a method that extracts temporal information from generative world models by leveraging optimal transport to derive a reward function from the learned occupancy measure, which captures the geometry of the world and goal-reaching information. ORS provably preserves the optimal policy while significantly improving performance, achieving a 2.2x improvement across 13 diverse long-horizon locomotion and manipulation tasks, and demonstrating effectiveness in real-world nuclear fusion control on 3 Tokamak tasks.
该论文针对离线目标条件强化学习中的信用分配问题，即动作与其长期后果之间存在时间延迟。作者提出了占用奖励塑形方法，通过最优传输从生成式世界模型中提取时间信息，基于学习到的占用度量推导出捕捉世界几何结构和目标达成信息的奖励函数。该方法在理论上不改变最优策略，同时显著提升性能，在13个多样化的长时域运动与操作任务中实现了2.2倍的性能提升，并在3个托卡马克核聚变控制任务中展示了实际有效性。
CodeRL+: Improving Code Generation via Reinforcement with Execution Semantics Alignment
Authors: Xue Jiang, Yihong Dong, Mengyang Liu, Hongyi Deng, Tian Wang, Yongding Tao, Rongyu Cao, Binhua Li, Zhi Jin, Wenpin Jiao, Fei Huang, Yongbin Li, Ge Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-10-21T09:48:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T14:35:52+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at code generation by learning from vast code corpora, a fundamental semantic gap remains between their training on textual patterns and the goal of functional correctness, which is governed by formal execution semantics. Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) approaches attempt to bridge this gap using outcome rewards from executing test cases. However, solely relying on binary pass/fail signals is inefficient for establishing a well-aligned connection between the textual representation of code and its execution semantics, especially for subtle logical errors within the code. In this paper, we propose CodeRL+, a novel approach that integrates execution semantics alignment into the RLVR training pipeline for code generation. CodeRL+ enables the model to infer variable-level execution trajectory, providing a direct learning signal of execution semantics. CodeRL+ can construct execution semantics alignment directly using existing on-policy rollouts and integrates seamlessly with various RL algorithms. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CodeRL+ outperforms post-training baselines (including RLVR and Distillation), achieving a 4.6% average relative improvement in pass@1. CodeRL+ generalizes effectively to other coding tasks, yielding 15.5% and 4.4% higher accuracy on code-reasoning and test-output-generation benchmarks, respectively. CodeRL+ shows strong applicability across diverse RL algorithms and LLMs. Furthermore, probe analyses provide compelling evidence that CodeRL+ strengthens the alignment between code's textual representations and its underlying execution semantics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CodeRL+：通过执行语义对齐的强化学习改进代码生成
尽管大型语言模型（LLM）通过从海量代码语料库中学习在代码生成方面表现出色，但其基于文本模式的训练与由形式化执行语义所决定的功能正确性目标之间仍存在根本性的语义鸿沟。基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法尝试通过执行测试用例的结果奖励来弥合这一差距。然而，仅依赖二元通过/失败信号难以在代码的文本表示与其执行语义之间建立良好对齐的联系，尤其是针对代码中细微的逻辑错误。本文提出CodeRL+，一种将执行语义对齐集成到代码生成的RLVR训练流程中的新方法。CodeRL+使模型能够推断变量级执行轨迹，提供执行语义的直接学习信号。该方法可直接利用现有的策略内采样构建执行语义对齐，并能无缝集成多种强化学习算法。大量实验表明，CodeRL+优于包括RLVR和蒸馏在内的后训练基线，在pass@1指标上平均相对提升4.6%。CodeRL+能有效泛化至其他编码任务，在代码推理和测试输出生成基准上分别取得15.5%和4.4%的准确率提升。该方法在多种强化学习算法和LLM上展现出强适用性。此外，探针分析提供了有力证据，证明CodeRL+增强了代码文本表示与其底层执行语义之间的对齐。
Summary / 总结
CodeRL+ addresses the semantic gap between LLMs' text-based training and the need for functionally correct code by enhancing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). The method integrates execution semantics alignment, enabling the model to infer variable-level execution trajectories from on-policy rollouts to provide direct learning signals. Experiments show CodeRL+ outperforms post-training baselines with a 4.6% average relative improvement in pass@1, achieves 15.5% and 4.4% higher accuracy on code-reasoning and test-output-generation benchmarks, and generalizes effectively across diverse RL algorithms and LLMs, with probe analyses confirming strengthened alignment between code text and execution semantics.
CodeRL+旨在弥合大型语言模型基于文本训练与代码功能正确性之间的语义鸿沟，通过增强基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法。该方法引入执行语义对齐，利用策略采样中的变量级执行轨迹提供直接学习信号。实验表明，CodeRL+在pass@1上平均相对提升4.6%，优于后训练基线（包括RLVR和蒸馏），在代码推理和测试输出生成基准上分别提高15.5%和4.4%的准确率，并有效泛化至多种强化学习算法和语言模型，探针分析证实了代码文本与执行语义之间对齐的增强。
Self-Guided Plan Extraction for Instruction-Following Tasks with Goal-Conditional Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zoya Volovikova, Nikita Sorokin, Dmitriy Lukashevskiy, Aleksandr Panov, Alexey Skrynnik
First: 2026-04-22T14:19:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T14:19:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce SuperIgor, a framework for instruction-following tasks. Unlike prior methods that rely on predefined subtasks, SuperIgor enables a language model to generate and refine high-level plans through a self-learning mechanism, reducing the need for manual dataset annotation. Our approach involves iterative co-training: an RL agent is trained to follow the generated plans, while the language model adapts and modifies these plans based on RL feedback and preferences. This creates a feedback loop where both the agent and the planner improve jointly. We validate our framework in environments with rich dynamics and stochasticity. Results show that SuperIgor agents adhere to instructions more strictly than baseline methods, while also demonstrating strong generalization to previously unseen instructions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向指令跟随任务的自主规划提取与目标条件强化学习
我们提出SuperIgor框架，用于指令跟随任务。与依赖预定义子任务的先前方法不同，SuperIgor通过自学习机制使语言模型能够生成并优化高层规划，减少人工数据集标注需求。我们的方法采用迭代协同训练：强化学习智能体被训练以遵循生成的规划，而语言模型则基于强化学习反馈和偏好调整修改这些规划。这形成了智能体与规划器共同改进的反馈循环。我们在具有丰富动态性和随机性的环境中验证了该框架。结果表明，SuperIgor智能体比基线方法更严格地遵循指令，同时对未见指令展现出强大的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SuperIgor, a framework for instruction-following tasks that addresses the limitation of prior methods requiring predefined subtasks. The motivation is to reduce manual dataset annotation by enabling a language model to autonomously generate and refine high-level plans through a self-learning mechanism. The method employs iterative co-training where a reinforcement learning agent learns to follow generated plans, and the language model adapts these plans based on RL feedback and preferences, creating a joint improvement loop. Experimental results in dynamic and stochastic environments demonstrate that SuperIgor agents adhere to instructions more strictly than baseline methods and exhibit strong generalization to unseen instructions.
该论文提出了SuperIgor框架，用于处理指令跟随任务，旨在解决先前方法依赖预定义子任务的局限性。其动机是通过自学习机制让语言模型自主生成并优化高层计划，从而减少人工数据集标注的需求。方法采用迭代协同训练：强化学习智能体学习执行生成的计划，而语言模型则根据强化学习的反馈和偏好调整计划，形成共同改进的反馈循环。在动态和随机环境中的实验结果表明，SuperIgor智能体比基线方法更严格地遵循指令，并对未见过的指令展现出强大的泛化能力。
A Hierarchical MARL-Based Approach for Coordinated Retail P2P Trading and Wholesale Market Participation of DERs
Authors: Patrick Wilk, Ethan Cantor, Yikui Liu, Jie Li
First: 2026-04-22T14:02:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T14:02:56+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 6 figures, 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The ongoing shift towards decentralization of the electric energy sector, driven by the growing electrification across end-use sectors, and widespread adoption of distributed energy resources (DERs), necessitates their active participation in the electricity markets to support grid operations. Furthermore, with bi-directional energy and communication flows becoming standard, intelligent, easy-to-deploy, resource-conservative demand-side participation is expected to play a critical role in securing power grid operational flexibility and market efficiency. This work proposes a market engagement framework that leverages a hierarchical multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MARL) approach to enable individual prosumers to participate in peer-to-peer retail auctions and further aggregate these intelligent prosumers to facilitate effective DER participation in wholesale markets. Ultimately, a Stackelberg game is proposed to coordinate this hierarchical MARL-based DER market participation framework toward enhanced market performance.

标题：基于分层多智能体强化学习的分布式能源协调零售点对点交易与批发市场参与方法
随着终端用电领域电气化程度不断提高以及分布式能源的广泛普及，电力行业正持续向去中心化方向转型，这要求分布式能源积极参与电力市场以支撑电网运行。此外，随着双向能量流与信息流成为常态，智能、易部署、资源节约的需求侧参与将在保障电网运行灵活性和市场效率方面发挥关键作用。本文提出一种市场参与框架，利用分层多智能体深度强化学习方法，使个体产消者能够参与点对点零售拍卖，并进一步聚合这些智能产消者，促进分布式能源有效参与批发市场。最终，通过斯塔克尔伯格博弈协调该基于分层多智能体强化学习的分布式能源市场参与框架，以提升市场绩效。

Motivated by the need for decentralized energy resources to actively participate in electricity markets for grid support, this paper proposes a hierarchical multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MARL) framework that enables individual prosumers to engage in peer-to-peer retail auctions while aggregating them for wholesale market participation. The method employs a Stackelberg game to coordinate the hierarchical MARL-based market engagement, optimizing both retail and wholesale interactions. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed approach effectively enhances market performance, achieving improved operational flexibility and economic efficiency compared to baseline methods.

IVY-FAKE: A Unified Explainable Framework and Benchmark for Image and Video AIGC Detection
Authors: Changjiang Jiang, Wenhui Dong, Zhonghao Zhang, Fengchang Yu, Wei Peng, Xinbin Yuan, Yifei Bi, Ming Zhao, Zian Zhou, Chenyang Si, Caifeng Shan
First: 2025-06-01T12:20:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T13:06:23+00:00
Comments: 30 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid development of Artificial Intelligence Generated Content (AIGC) techniques has enabled the creation of high-quality synthetic content, but it also raises significant security concerns. Current detection methods face two major limitations: (1) the lack of multidimensional explainable datasets for generated images and videos. Existing open-source datasets (e.g., WildFake, GenVideo) rely on oversimplified binary annotations, which restrict the explainability and trustworthiness of trained detectors. (2) Prior MLLM-based forgery detectors (e.g., FakeVLM) exhibit insufficiently fine-grained interpretability in their step-by-step reasoning, which hinders reliable localization and explanation. To address these challenges, we introduce Ivy-Fake, the first large-scale multimodal benchmark for explainable AIGC detection. It consists of over 106K richly annotated training samples (images and videos) and 5,000 manually verified evaluation examples, sourced from multiple generative models and real world datasets through a carefully designed pipeline to ensure both diversity and quality. Furthermore, we propose Ivy-xDetector, a reinforcement learning model based on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), capable of producing explainable reasoning chains and achieving robust performance across multiple synthetic content detection benchmarks. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of our dataset and confirm the effectiveness of our approach. Notably, our method improves performance on GenImage from 86.88% to 96.32%, surpassing prior state-of-the-art methods by a clear margin.

标题：IVY-FAKE：面向图像与视频AIGC检测的统一可解释框架与基准
人工智能生成内容（AIGC）技术的快速发展使得高质量合成内容的创作成为可能，但也引发了重大的安全隐患。当前检测方法面临两大局限：（1）缺乏针对生成图像与视频的多维可解释数据集。现有开源数据集（如WildFake、GenVideo）依赖过于简化的二元标注，限制了训练检测器的可解释性与可信度。（2）基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的伪造检测器（如FakeVLM）在逐步推理过程中表现出细粒度可解释性不足，阻碍了可靠的定位与解释。为应对这些挑战，我们提出Ivy-Fake——首个面向可解释AIGC检测的大规模多模态基准。该基准包含超过10.6万条丰富标注的训练样本（图像与视频）及5000个经人工验证的评估示例，数据源自多种生成模型与真实世界数据集，并通过精心设计的流程确保多样性与质量。此外，我们提出Ivy-xDetector——一种基于组相对策略优化（GRPO）的强化学习模型，能够生成可解释的推理链，并在多个合成内容检测基准上实现稳健性能。大量实验证明了我们数据集的优越性及方法的有效性。值得注意的是，我们的方法将GenImage上的性能从86.88%提升至96.32%，显著超越了先前的最优方法。

Temporal Difference Calibration in Sequential Tasks: Application to Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Shelly Francis-Meretzki, Mirco Mutti, Yaniv Romano, Aviv Tamar
First: 2026-04-22T11:58:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T11:58:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in vision-language-action (VLA) models for robotics have highlighted the importance of reliable uncertainty quantification in sequential tasks. However, assessing and improving calibration in such settings remains mostly unexplored, especially when only partial trajectories are observed. In this work, we formulate sequential calibration for episodic tasks, where task-success confidence is produced along an episode, while success is determined at the end of it. We introduce a sequential extension of the Brier score and show that, for binary outcomes, its risk minimizer coincides with the VLA policy's value function. This connection bridges uncertainty calibration and reinforcement learning, enabling the use of temporal-difference (TD) value estimation as a principled calibration mechanism over time. We empirically show that TD calibration improves performance relative to the state-of-the-art on simulated and real-robot data. Interestingly, we show that when calibrated using TD, the VLA's single-step action probabilities can yield competitive uncertainty estimates, in contrast to recent findings that employed different calibration techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时序差分校准在序列任务中的应用：面向视觉-语言-动作模型
近期机器人领域视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型的进展凸显了序列任务中可靠不确定性量化的重要性。然而，在此类场景下评估与改进校准性能仍鲜有探索，尤其当仅能观测到部分轨迹时。本研究针对情节性任务提出序列校准方法——任务成功置信度在情节过程中逐步生成，而成功结果在情节结束时判定。我们引入Brier分数的序列扩展形式，并证明在二元结果下其风险最小化器与VLA策略的价值函数一致。这一关联架起了不确定性校准与强化学习之间的桥梁，使得时序差分（TD）价值估计可作为随时间演化的原则性校准机制。实验表明，在仿真与真实机器人数据上，TD校准相较现有最优方法能提升性能。值得注意的是，我们发现经TD校准后，VLA的单步动作概率可产生具有竞争力的不确定性估计，这与近期采用不同校准技术的研究结论形成对比。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the underexplored problem of uncertainty calibration in sequential tasks for vision-language-action (VLA) models in robotics, where task-success confidence must be produced throughout an episode but success is only known at the end. The authors formulate sequential calibration for episodic tasks, extend the Brier score to the sequential setting, and prove that its risk minimizer equals the VLA policy's value function, bridging calibration with reinforcement learning. 该论文针对机器人视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在序列任务中的不确定性校准这一未被充分探索的问题展开研究，其中任务成功置信度需在回合过程中生成，但成功与否仅在回合结束时确定。作者为回合任务制定了序列校准框架，将Brier分数扩展到序列场景，并证明其风险最小化器等价于VLA策略的价值函数，从而将校准与强化学习联系起来。他们提出使用时序差分（TD）价值估计作为原则性的校准机制，并在模拟和真实机器人数据上实验证明，TD校准优于现有最先进方法，同时有趣地发现，当使用TD校准时，VLA的单步动作概率能产生具有竞争力的不确定性估计，这与先前采用不同校准技术的研究结论相反。
WebGen-R1: Incentivizing Large Language Models to Generate Functional and Aesthetic Websites with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Juyong Jiang, Chenglin Cai, Chansung Park, Jiasi Shen, Sunghun Kim, Jianguo Li, Yue Wang
First: 2026-04-22T10:04:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T10:04:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at function-level code generation, project-level tasks such as generating functional and visually aesthetic multi-page websites remain highly challenging. Existing works are often limited to single-page static websites, while agentic frameworks typically rely on multi-turn execution with proprietary models, leading to substantial token costs, high latency, and brittle integration. Training a small LLM end-to-end with reinforcement learning (RL) is a promising alternative, yet it faces a critical bottleneck in designing reliable and computationally feasible rewards for website generation. Unlike single-file coding tasks that can be verified by unit tests, website generation requires evaluating inherently subjective aesthetics, cross-page interactions, and functional correctness. To this end, we propose WebGen-R1, an end-to-end RL framework tailored for project-level website generation. We first introduce a scaffold-driven structured generation paradigm that constrains the large open-ended action space and preserves architectural integrity. We then design a novel cascaded multimodal reward that seamlessly couples structural guarantees with execution-grounded functional feedback and vision-based aesthetic supervision. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our WebGen-R1 substantially transforms a 7B base model from generating nearly nonfunctional websites into producing deployable, aesthetically aligned multi-page websites. Remarkably, our WebGen-R1 not only consistently outperforms heavily scaled open-source models (up to 72B), but also rivals the state-of-the-art DeepSeek-R1 (671B) in functional success, while substantially exceeding it in valid rendering and aesthetic alignment. These results position WebGen-R1 as a viable path for scaling small open models from function-level code generation to project-level web application generation.
Summary / 总结
Large language models struggle with project-level website generation due to the need for functional correctness and aesthetic quality across multiple pages. WebGen-R1 addresses this by introducing a reinforcement learning framework with a scaffold-driven generation paradigm to constrain the action space and a cascaded multimodal reward that combines structural, functional, and aesthetic feedback. Experiments show that a 7B model trained with WebGen-R1 outperforms larger open-source models up to 72B and rivals DeepSeek-R1 (671B) in functional success while exceeding it in rendering and aesthetic alignment.
大型语言模型在项目级网站生成中面临功能正确性和多页面美观性的挑战。WebGen-R1提出了一种强化学习框架，通过脚手架驱动的生成范式约束动作空间，并设计级联多模态奖励机制，结合结构、功能和美学反馈。实验表明，使用WebGen-R1训练的7B模型在功能成功率上超越高达72B的开源模型，与DeepSeek-R1（671B）相当，并在有效渲染和美学对齐上显著领先。
Distributional Value Estimation Without Target Networks for Robust Quality-Diversity
Authors: Behrad Koohy, Jamie Bayne
First: 2026-04-22T09:31:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T09:31:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted as Full Paper at GECCO'26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms excel at discovering diverse repertoires of skills, but are hindered by poor sample efficiency and often require tens of millions of environment steps to solve complex locomotion tasks. Recent advances in Reinforcement Learning (RL) have shown that high Update-to-Data (UTD) ratios accelerate Actor-Critic learning. While effective, standard high-UTD algorithms typically utilise target networks to stabilise training. This requirement introduces a significant computational bottleneck, rendering them impractical for resource-intensive Quality-Diversity (QD) tasks where sample efficiency and rapid population adaptation are critical. In this paper, we introduce QDHUAC, a sample-efficient, target-free and distributional QD-RL algorithm that provides dense and low-variance gradient signals, which enables high-UTD training for Dominated Novelty Search whilst requiring an order of magnitude fewer environment steps. We demonstrate that our method enables stable training at high UTD ratios, achieving competitive coverage and fitness on high-dimensional Brax environments with an order of magnitude fewer samples than baselines. Our results suggest that combining target-free distributional critics with dominance-based selection is a key enabler for the next generation of sample-efficient evolutionary RL algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需目标网络的分布价值估计以实现鲁棒的质量-多样性
质量-多样性（QD）算法在发现多样化技能库方面表现出色，但受限于样本效率低下，通常需要数千万环境步才能解决复杂的运动任务。强化学习（RL）的最新进展表明，高更新-数据比（UTD）能加速演员-评论家学习。然而，标准的高UTD算法通常利用目标网络来稳定训练，这引入了显著的计算瓶颈，使其在样本效率和快速种群适应至关重要的资源密集型质量-多样性（QD）任务中不实用。本文提出QDHUAC，一种样本高效、无目标且分布式的QD-RL算法，提供密集且低方差的梯度信号，从而在主导新颖性搜索中实现高UTD训练，同时所需环境步数减少一个数量级。我们证明，该方法能在高UTD比率下实现稳定训练，在高维Brax环境中以比基线少一个数量级的样本达到竞争性的覆盖率和适应度。结果表明，将无目标分布评论家与基于主导性的选择相结合，是下一代样本高效进化RL算法的关键推动因素。

Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms are effective at discovering diverse skills but suffer from poor sample efficiency, often requiring tens of millions of environment steps for complex tasks. By providing dense and low-variance gradient signals for Dominated Novelty Search, QDHUAC achieves competitive coverage and fitness on high-dimensional Brax environments with an order of magnitude fewer samples than baselines, demonstrating stable training at high UTD ratios.

Scalable Quantum Reinforcement Learning on NISQ Devices with Dynamic-Circuit Qubit Reuse and Grover Optimization
Authors: Thet Htar Su, Shaswot Shresthamali, Masaaki Kondo
First: 2025-09-19T14:11:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T09:27:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A scalable and resource-efficient quantum reinforcement learning framework is presented that eliminates the linear qubit-scaling barrier in multi-step quantum Markov decision processes (QMDPs). The proposed framework integrates a QMDP formulation, dynamic-circuit execution, and Grover-based amplitude amplification into a unified quantum-native architecture. Environment dynamics are encoded entirely within quantum Hilbert space, enabling coherent superposition over state-action sequences and a direct quantum agent-environment interface without intermediate quantum-to-classical conversion. The central contribution is a dynamic execution model for multi-step QMDPs that employs mid-circuit measurement and reset to recycle a fixed physical quantum register across sequential interactions. This approach preserves trajectory fidelity relative to a static unrolled QMDP, generating identical state-action sequences while reducing the physical qubit requirement from 7xT to a constant 7, independent of the interaction horizon T. Thus, the qubit complexity of multi-step QMDPs is transformed from O(T) to O(1) while maintaining functional equivalence at the level of trajectory generation. Trajectory returns are evaluated via quantum arithmetic, and high-return trajectories are marked and amplified using amplitude amplification to increase their sampling probability. Simulations confirm preservation of trajectory fidelity with a 66% qubit reduction compared to a static design. Experimental execution on an IBM Heron-class processor demonstrates feasibility on noisy intermediate-scale quantum hardware, establishing a scalable and resource-efficient foundation for large-scale quantum-native reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动态电路量子比特复用与Grover优化的NISQ设备可扩展量子强化学习
提出了一种可扩展且资源高效的量子强化学习框架，消除了多步量子马尔可夫决策过程（QMDP）中的线性量子比特扩展障碍。该框架将QMDP公式、动态电路执行和基于Grover的幅度放大整合为统一的量子原生架构。环境动态完全编码在量子希尔伯特空间中，实现了状态-动作序列的相干叠加，以及无需中间量子-经典转换的直接量子智能体-环境接口。核心贡献在于多步QMDP的动态执行模型，该模型利用中间电路测量和重置，在连续交互中回收固定的物理量子寄存器。该方法相对于静态展开的QMDP保持了轨迹保真度，生成相同的状态-动作序列，同时将物理量子比特需求从7×T降低到常数7，与交互时间步T无关。因此，多步QMDP的量子比特复杂度从O(T)转变为O(1)，同时在轨迹生成层面保持功能等价性。通过量子算术评估轨迹回报，并利用幅度放大标记和放大高回报轨迹以增加其采样概率。仿真证实，与静态设计相比，轨迹保真度得以保持，量子比特减少66%。在IBM Heron级处理器上的实验执行证明了其在含噪中等规模量子硬件上的可行性，为大规模量子原生强化学习建立了可扩展且资源高效的基础。

Simulations show a 66% qubit reduction compared to static designs, and experimental execution on an IBM Heron-class processor confirms feasibility on noisy intermediate-scale quantum hardware.
本文提出了一种可扩展的量子强化学习框架，解决了多步量子马尔可夫决策过程（QMDP）中线性量子比特扩展的瓶颈。该方法整合了QMDP公式、动态电路执行和基于Grover的振幅放大，将环境动态完全编码在量子希尔伯特空间中，避免了量子到经典的转换。通过使用中间电路测量和重置来回收固定的7量子比特寄存器，该方法在保持轨迹保真度的同时，将量子比特复杂度从O(T)降低到O(1)。模拟显示相比静态设计减少了66%的量子比特，在IBM Heron级处理器上的实验执行验证了其在含噪中等规模量子硬件上的可行性。
LiteResearcher: A Scalable Agentic RL Training Framework for Deep Research Agent
Authors: Wanli Li, Bince Qu, Bo Pan, Jianyu Zhang, Zheng Liu, Pan Zhang, Wei Chen, Bo Zhang
First: 2026-04-20T08:11:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T09:13:22+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful training paradigm for LLM-based agents. However, scaling agentic RL for deep research remains constrained by two coupled challenges: hand-crafted synthetic data fails to elicit genuine real-world search capabilities, and real-world search dependency during RL training introduces instability and prohibitive cost, which limits the scalability of Agentic RL. LiteResearcher is a training framework that makes Agentic RL scalable: by constructing a lite virtual world that mirrors real-world search dynamics, we enable a continuously improving training recipe that empowers a tiny search agent to outperform large-scale open-source and commercial models (e.g., Tongyi DeepResearch and Claude-4.5 Sonnet). Specifically, on common benchmarks such as GAIA and Xbench, our LiteResearcher-4B achieves open-source state-of-the-art results of 71.3% and 78.0% respectively, demonstrating that scalable RL training is a key enabler for Deep Research Agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LiteResearcher：面向深度研究智能体的可扩展强化学习训练框架
强化学习已成为基于大语言模型智能体的强大训练范式。然而，将智能体强化学习扩展到深度研究领域仍受限于两个相互耦合的挑战：手工制作的合成数据无法激发真实的搜索能力，而强化学习训练过程中对真实搜索的依赖则引入了不稳定性和高昂成本，限制了智能体强化学习的可扩展性。LiteResearcher是一个使智能体强化学习具备可扩展性的训练框架：通过构建一个模拟真实搜索动态的轻量虚拟世界，我们实现了持续改进的训练方案，使一个微型搜索智能体能够超越大规模开源和商业模型（如通义千问DeepResearch和Claude-4.5 Sonnet）。具体而言，在GAIA和Xbench等常见基准测试中，我们的LiteResearcher-4B分别取得了71.3%和78.0%的开源最优结果，证明了可扩展的强化学习训练是深度研究智能体的关键推动因素。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LiteResearcher, a scalable agentic reinforcement learning (RL) training framework designed to address the challenges of training deep research agents. The motivation stems from the limitations of existing methods, which rely on hand-crafted synthetic data that fails to capture real-world search behaviors and suffer from instability and high costs when using real-world search during RL training. The method constructs a lite virtual world that mirrors real-world search dynamics, enabling a continuously improving training recipe. Experimental results show that LiteResearcher-4B achieves state-of-the-art open-source performance on GAIA and Xbench benchmarks, with scores of 71.3% and 78.0% respectively, outperforming larger models like Tongyi DeepResearch and Claude-4.5 Sonnet.

CARLA-Air: Fly Drones Inside a CARLA World -- A Unified Infrastructure for Air-Ground Embodied Intelligence
Authors: Tianle Zeng, Yanci Wen, Hong Zhang
First: 2026-03-30T04:49:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T08:50:07+00:00
Comments: Prebuilt binaries, project page, full source code, and community discussion group are all available at: https://github.com/louiszengCN/CarlaAir
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The convergence of low-altitude economies, embodied intelligence, and air-ground cooperative systems creates growing demand for simulation infrastructure capable of jointly modeling aerial and ground agents within a single physically coherent environment. Existing open-source platforms remain domain-segregated: driving simulators lack aerial dynamics, while multirotor simulators lack realistic ground scenes. Bridge-based co-simulation introduces synchronization overhead and cannot guarantee strict spatial-temporal consistency. We present CARLA-Air, an open-source infrastructure that unifies high-fidelity urban driving and physics-accurate multirotor flight within a single Unreal Engine process. The platform preserves both CARLA and AirSim native Python APIs and ROS 2 interfaces, enabling zero-modification code reuse. Within a shared physics tick and rendering pipeline, CARLA-Air delivers photorealistic environments with rule-compliant traffic, socially-aware pedestrians, and aerodynamically consistent UAV dynamics, synchronously capturing up to 18 sensor modalities across all platforms at each tick. The platform supports representative air-ground embodied intelligence workloads spanning cooperation, embodied navigation and vision-language action, multi-modal perception and dataset construction, and reinforcement-learning-based policy training. An extensible asset pipeline allows integration of custom robot platforms into the shared world. By inheriting AirSim's aerial capabilities -- whose upstream development has been archived -- CARLA-Air ensures this widely adopted flight stack continues to evolve within a modern infrastructure. Released with prebuilt binaries and full source: https://github.com/louiszengCN/CarlaAir

PromptEcho: Annotation-Free Reward from Vision-Language Models for Text-to-Image Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jinlong Liu, Wanggui He, Peng Zhang, Mushui Liu, Hao Jiang, Pipei Huang
First: 2026-04-14T12:21:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T08:05:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) can improve the prompt following capability of text-to-image (T2I) models, yet obtaining high-quality reward signals remains challenging: CLIP Score is too coarse-grained, while VLM-based reward models (e.g., RewardDance) require costly human-annotated preference data and additional fine-tuning. We propose PromptEcho, a reward construction method that requires \emph{no} annotation and \emph{no} reward model training. Given a generated image and a guiding query, PromptEcho computes the token-level cross-entropy loss of a frozen VLM with the original prompt as the label, directly extracting the image-text alignment knowledge encoded during VLM pretraining. The reward is deterministic, computationally efficient, and improves automatically as stronger open-source VLMs become available. For evaluation, we develop DenseAlignBench, a benchmark of concept-rich dense captions for rigorously testing prompt following capability. Experimental results on two state-of-the-art T2I models (Z-Image and QwenImage-2512) demonstrate that PromptEcho achieves substantial improvements on DenseAlignBench (+26.8pp / +16.2pp net win rate), along with consistent gains on GenEval, DPG-Bench, and TIIFBench without any task-specific training. Ablation studies confirm that PromptEcho comprehensively outperforms inference-based scoring with the same VLM, and that reward quality scales with VLM size. We will open-source the trained models and the DenseAlignBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PromptEcho：面向文本到图像强化学习的视觉语言模型免标注奖励方法
强化学习可提升文本到图像（T2I）模型的提示遵循能力，但获取高质量奖励信号仍具挑战：CLIP分数过于粗粒度，而基于VLM的奖励模型（如RewardDance）需要昂贵的人工标注偏好数据和额外微调。我们提出PromptEcho，一种无需标注且无需奖励模型训练的奖励构建方法。给定生成图像和引导查询，PromptEcho以原始提示为标签，计算冻结VLM的token级交叉熵损失，直接提取VLM预训练中编码的图像-文本对齐知识。该奖励具有确定性、计算高效性，并随更强开源VLM的出现自动提升。为评估，我们构建了DenseAlignBench——一个富含概念密集描述的基准测试，用于严格检验提示遵循能力。在两个最先进T2I模型（Z-Image和QwenImage-2512）上的实验表明，PromptEcho在DenseAlignBench上取得显著提升（净胜率+26.8pp/+16.2pp），并在GenEval、DPG-Bench和TIIFBench上获得一致增益，无需任何任务特定训练。消融研究证实，PromptEcho在使用相同VLM时全面优于基于推理的评分方法，且奖励质量随VLM规模扩大而提升。我们将开源训练模型和DenseAlignBench。
Summary / 总结
PromptEcho addresses the challenge of obtaining high-quality reward signals for reinforcement learning in text-to-image generation, where existing methods like CLIP Score are too coarse and VLM-based reward models require costly human annotations. The method computes token-level cross-entropy loss from a frozen vision-language model using the original prompt as a label, extracting alignment knowledge without any annotation or reward model training. Experiments on two state-of-the-art T2I models show that PromptEcho achieves substantial improvements on the proposed DenseAlignBench benchmark with net win rate gains of +26.8pp and +16.2pp, along with consistent improvements on GenEval, DPG-Bench, and TIIFBench, while ablation studies confirm that reward quality scales with VLM size.
PromptEcho旨在解决文本到图像生成中强化学习所需高质量奖励信号的获取难题，现有方法如CLIP Score过于粗糙，而基于VLM的奖励模型需要昂贵的人工标注数据。该方法利用冻结的视觉语言模型，以原始提示为标签计算词级交叉熵损失，无需任何标注或奖励模型训练即可直接提取图像-文本对齐知识。在两个最先进的T2I模型上的实验表明，PromptEcho在提出的DenseAlignBench基准上取得了显著改进，净胜率分别提升26.8和16.2个百分点，同时在GenEval、DPG-Bench和TIIFBench上均有一致提升，消融研究证实奖励质量随VLM规模扩大而提升。
From Competition to Synergy: Unlocking Reinforcement Learning for Subject-Driven Image Generation
Authors: Ziwei Huang, Ying Shu, Hao Fang, Quanyu Long, Wenya Wang, Qiushi Guo, Tiezheng Ge, Leilei Gan
First: 2025-10-21T03:32:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T07:39:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Subject-driven image generation models face a fundamental trade-off between identity preservation (fidelity) and prompt adherence (editability). While online reinforcement learning (RL), specifically GPRO, offers a promising solution, we find that a naive application of GRPO leads to competitive degradation, as the simple linear aggregation of rewards with static weights causes conflicting gradient signals and a misalignment with the temporal dynamics of the diffusion process. To overcome these limitations, we propose Customized-GRPO, a novel framework featuring two key innovations: (i) Synergy-Aware Reward Shaping (SARS), a non-linear mechanism that explicitly penalizes conflicted reward signals and amplifies synergistic ones, providing a sharper and more decisive gradient. (ii) Time-Aware Dynamic Weighting (TDW), which aligns the optimization pressure with the model's temporal dynamics by prioritizing prompt-following in the early, identity preservation in the later. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms naive GRPO baselines, successfully mitigating competitive degradation. Our model achieves a superior balance, generating images that both preserve key identity features and accurately adhere to complex textual prompts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从竞争到协同：解锁强化学习用于主题驱动图像生成
主题驱动图像生成模型在身份保持（保真度）与提示遵循（可编辑性）之间面临根本性权衡。虽然在线强化学习（特别是GPRO）提供了有前景的解决方案，但我们发现，简单应用GRPO会导致竞争性退化，因为静态权重的线性奖励聚合会产生冲突的梯度信号，并与扩散过程的时间动态不匹配。为克服这些限制，我们提出Customized-GRPO，一种包含两项关键创新的新框架：(i) 协同感知奖励塑造（SARS），一种非线性机制，明确惩罚冲突奖励信号并放大协同信号，提供更清晰、更果断的梯度。(ii) 时间感知动态加权（TDW），通过早期优先提示遵循、后期优先身份保持，使优化压力与模型的时间动态对齐。大量实验表明，我们的方法显著优于朴素GRPO基线，成功缓解了竞争性退化。我们的模型实现了卓越的平衡，生成的图像既保留了关键身份特征，又准确遵循了复杂文本提示。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the trade-off between identity preservation and prompt adherence in subject-driven image generation, where naive application of online reinforcement learning (GRPO) leads to competitive degradation due to conflicting gradient signals from static reward aggregation. The authors propose Customized-GRPO, which introduces Synergy-Aware Reward Shaping (SARS) to penalize conflicted rewards and amplify synergistic ones, and Time-Aware Dynamic Weighting (TDW) to align optimization with diffusion temporal dynamics. Experiments show that Customized-GRPO significantly outperforms naive GRPO baselines, achieving a superior balance between preserving key identity features and accurately following complex textual prompts.
该论文针对主题驱动图像生成中身份保持与提示遵循之间的权衡问题，发现直接应用在线强化学习（GRPO）因静态奖励聚合导致梯度冲突和扩散过程时间动态不匹配，从而引发竞争性退化。作者提出Customized-GRPO框架，包含两个关键创新：协同感知奖励塑形（SARS）通过非线性机制惩罚冲突奖励并放大协同信号，以及时间感知动态加权（TDW）将优化压力与模型时间动态对齐。实验表明，该方法显著优于原始GRPO基线，在保持关键身份特征和准确遵循复杂文本提示之间实现了更优平衡。
RADS: Reinforcement Learning-Based Sample Selection Improves Transfer Learning in Low-resource and Imbalanced Clinical Settings
Authors: Wei Han, David Martinez, Anna Khanina, Lawrence Cavedon, Karin Verspoor
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-22T07:05:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T07:05:25+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A common strategy in transfer learning is few shot fine-tuning, but its success is highly dependent on the quality of samples selected as training examples. Active learning methods such as uncertainty sampling and diversity sampling can select useful samples. However, under extremely low-resource and class-imbalanced conditions, they often favor outliers rather than truly informative samples, resulting in degraded performance. In this paper, we introduce RADS (Reinforcement Adaptive Domain Sampling), a robust sample selection strategy using reinforcement learning (RL) to identify the most informative samples. Experimental evaluations on several real world clinical datasets show our sample selection strategy enhances model transferability while maintaining robust performance under extreme class imbalance compared to traditional methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RADS：基于强化学习的样本选择方法提升低资源与不平衡临床场景下的迁移学习效果
迁移学习中一种常见策略是少样本微调，但其成功高度依赖于所选训练样本的质量。主动学习方法（如不确定性采样和多样性采样）能够选择有用样本，但在极端低资源和类别不平衡条件下，这些方法往往偏向于异常值而非真正信息丰富的样本，导致性能下降。本文提出RADS（强化自适应领域采样），一种使用强化学习（RL）识别最具信息量样本的鲁棒样本选择策略。在多个真实临床数据集上的实验评估表明，与传统方法相比，我们的样本选择策略在极端类别不平衡下增强了模型的可迁移性，同时保持了鲁棒性能。
Summary / 总结
RADS addresses the challenge of sample selection in few-shot fine-tuning for transfer learning, particularly under low-resource and class-imbalanced clinical settings where traditional active learning methods often select outliers over informative samples. The method employs a reinforcement learning framework to adaptively identify the most informative samples for training. Experimental results on real-world clinical datasets demonstrate that RADS enhances model transferability and maintains robust performance under extreme class imbalance, outperforming conventional sample selection strategies.
RADS针对迁移学习中小样本微调时的样本选择问题，尤其是在资源匮乏和类别不平衡的临床场景下，传统主动学习方法常倾向于选择异常值而非真正有信息的样本。该方法利用强化学习框架自适应地识别最具信息量的训练样本。在多个真实临床数据集上的实验表明，RADS在极端类别不平衡条件下提升了模型的可迁移性并保持了稳健性能，优于传统的样本选择策略。
Thinking While Listening: Fast-Slow Recurrence for Long-Horizon Sequential Modeling
Authors: Shota Takashiro, Masanori Koyama, Takeru Miyato, Yusuke Iwasawa, Yutaka Matsuo, Kohei Hayashi
First: 2026-04-02T03:45:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T06:02:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We extend the recent latent recurrent modeling to sequential input streams. By interleaving fast, recurrent latent updates with self-organizational ability between slow observation updates, our method facilitates the learning of stable internal structures that evolve alongside the input. This mechanism allows the model to maintain coherent and clustered representations over long horizons, improving out-of-distribution generalization in reinforcement learning and algorithmic tasks compared to sequential baselines such as LSTM, state space models, and Transformer variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：边听边想：面向长程序列建模的快慢递归机制
我们将近期提出的潜在递归建模方法扩展到连续输入流。通过在慢速观测更新之间交错进行具有自组织能力的快速递归潜在更新，我们的方法促进了与输入同步演化的稳定内部结构的学习。该机制使模型能够在长程范围内保持连贯且聚类化的表征，相较于LSTM、状态空间模型和Transformer变体等序列基线方法，在强化学习和算法任务中提升了分布外泛化能力。

Experimental results demonstrate that this approach maintains coherent and clustered representations over long sequences, achieving improved out-of-distribution generalization in reinforcement learning and algorithmic tasks compared to baselines including LSTM, state space models, and Transformer variants.
该论文提出了一种用于长程序列建模的新型循环架构，通过将快速的潜在状态更新与缓慢的观测更新交替进行。该方法扩展了潜在循环建模，在更新之间引入自组织能力，使模型能够学习随输入演化的稳定内部结构。实验结果表明，该方法能在长序列上保持连贯且聚类良好的表征，在强化学习和算法任务中相比LSTM、状态空间模型和Transformer变体等基线方法，实现了更好的分布外泛化性能。
Issues with Value-Based Multi-objective Reinforcement Learning: Value Function Interference and Overestimation Sensitivity
Authors: Peter Vamplew, Ethan, Watkins, Cameron Foale, Richard Dazeley
First: 2024-02-09T09:28:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T05:23:45+00:00
Comments: This updates our previous pre-print to add extended discussion of value-function interference as well as new material illustrating the interaction between Q-value overestimation and non-linear utility
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) algorithms extend conventional reinforcement learning (RL) to the more general case of problems with multiple, conflicting objectives, represented by vector-valued rewards. Widely-used scalar RL methods such as Q-learning can be modified to handle multiple objectives by (1) learning vector-valued value functions, and (2) performing action selection using a scalarisation or ordering operator which reflects the user's preferences with respect to the different objectives. This paper investigates two previously unreported issues which can hinder the performance of value-based MORL algorithms when applied in conjunction with a non-linear utility function -- value function interference, and sensitivity to overestimation. We illustrate the nature of these phenomena on simple multi-objective MDPs using a tabular implementation of multiobjective Q-learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于价值的多目标强化学习中的问题：价值函数干扰与过估计敏感性
多目标强化学习算法将传统强化学习扩展到更一般的情况，即处理具有多个冲突目标的问题，这些目标由向量值奖励表示。广泛使用的标量强化学习方法（如Q学习）可以通过以下方式修改以处理多个目标：（1）学习向量值价值函数，（2）使用反映用户对不同目标偏好的标量化或排序算子执行动作选择。本文研究了两个先前未报道的问题，这些问题在将基于价值的多目标强化学习算法与非线性效用函数结合应用时可能阻碍其性能——价值函数干扰和对过估计的敏感性。我们通过使用表格形式的多目标Q学习在简单的多目标MDP上说明了这些现象的本质。
Summary / 总结
This paper identifies two previously unreported issues in value-based multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) when combined with non-linear utility functions: value function interference and sensitivity to overestimation. The authors extend conventional Q-learning to handle vector-valued rewards by learning vector-valued value functions and using scalarisation or ordering operators for action selection. Through tabular implementations of multi-objective Q-learning on simple multi-objective MDPs, they demonstrate how these phenomena degrade performance, with value function interference causing conflicting updates and overestimation sensitivity amplifying errors under non-linear utility. The study highlights critical challenges that must be addressed for robust MORL algorithms.
本文揭示了基于价值的多目标强化学习（MORL）在结合非线性效用函数时存在的两个先前未报告的问题：价值函数干扰和对过高估计的敏感性。作者通过学习向量值价值函数并使用标量化或排序算子进行动作选择，将传统Q学习扩展到处理向量值奖励的通用情况。通过在简单多目标MDP上使用表格形式的多目标Q学习实现，他们展示了这些现象如何降低性能：价值函数干扰导致冲突更新，而过估计敏感性在非线性效用下放大误差。该研究强调了开发稳健MORL算法必须解决的关键挑战。
Lever: Inference-Time Policy Reuse under Support Constraints
Authors: Ihor Vitenki, Noha Ibrahim, Sihem Amer-Yahia
First: 2026-04-22T04:28:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T04:28:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) policies are typically trained for fixed objectives, making reuse difficult when task requirements change. We study inference-time policy reuse: given a library of pre-trained policies and a new composite objective, can a high-quality policy be constructed entirely offline, without additional environment interaction? We introduce lever (Leveraging Efficient Vector Embeddings for Reusable policies), an end-to-end framework that retrieves relevant policies, evaluates them using behavioral embeddings, and composes new policies via offline Q-value composition. We focus on the support-limited regime, where no value propagation is possible, and show that the effectiveness of reuse depends critically on the coverage of available transitions. To balance performance and computational cost, lever proposes composition strategies that control the exploration of candidate policies. Experiments in deterministic GridWorld environments show that inference-time composition can match, and in some cases exceed, training-from-scratch performance while providing substantial speedups. At the same time, performance degrades when long-horizon dependencies require value propagation, highlighting a fundamental limitation of offline reuse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：杠杆：支持约束下的推理时策略复用
强化学习策略通常针对固定目标进行训练，当任务需求变化时难以复用。我们研究推理时策略复用：给定预训练策略库和新的复合目标，能否完全离线构建高质量策略，无需额外环境交互？我们提出Lever（可复用策略的高效向量嵌入利用框架），这是一个端到端框架，通过行为嵌入检索相关策略、评估策略，并通过离线Q值组合构建新策略。我们聚焦于支持受限场景（无法进行值传播），并证明复用效果关键取决于可用转移的覆盖范围。为平衡性能与计算成本，Lever提出控制候选策略探索的组合策略。在确定性网格世界环境中的实验表明，推理时组合可匹配甚至超越从头训练的性能，同时提供显著加速。然而，当长程依赖需要值传播时性能下降，揭示了离线复用的根本局限性。

Temporally Extended Mixture-of-Experts Models
Authors: Zeyu Shen, Peter Henderson
First: 2026-04-22T03:50:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T03:50:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts models, now popular for scaling capacity at fixed inference speed, switch experts at nearly every token. Once a model outgrows available GPU memory, this churn can render optimizations like offloading and pre-fetching ineffective. We make the case that the options framework in reinforcement learning is a perfect match to tackle this problem, and argue for temporally extended mixture-of-experts layers. Building on the option-critic framework with deliberation costs, we add a controller to each layer that learns when to switch expert sets and which to load. By applying this to gpt-oss-20b with low-rank adapters and a self-distillation reward, our method reduces switch rates from over 50% to below 5% while retaining up to 90% of base-model accuracy on MATH, MMLU, and MMMLU. This shows that even existing pre-trained models can be converted to temporally extended MoEs with lightweight training, with the deliberation cost allowing model trainers to trade off switching rates against capability. We hope this opens a principled path, grounded in the options framework, for memory-efficient serving and continual learning in ever-growing MoE models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时间扩展的混合专家模型
混合专家模型如今因能在固定推理速度下扩展容量而流行，但几乎在每个词元处切换专家。一旦模型超出可用GPU内存，这种频繁切换会使卸载和预取等优化失效。我们论证强化学习中的选项框架是解决此问题的完美匹配，并主张采用时间扩展的混合专家层。基于带有决策成本的选项-批评框架，我们在每层添加一个控制器，学习何时切换专家集以及加载哪些专家。通过将此法应用于带有低秩适配器和自蒸馏奖励的gpt-oss-20b模型，我们的方法将切换率从超过50%降至低于5%，同时在MATH、MMLU和MMMU上保留高达90%的基础模型准确率。这表明即使是现有的预训练模型，也能通过轻量训练转换为时间扩展的MoE，而决策成本允许模型训练者在切换率与能力之间进行权衡。我们希望这能开辟一条基于选项框架的原则性路径，用于日益增长的MoE模型的内存高效服务和持续学习。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of standard Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models, which switch experts at nearly every token, causing high memory churn that undermines optimizations like offloading when models exceed GPU memory. The authors propose a temporally extended MoE layer inspired by the options framework in reinforcement learning, adding a controller that learns when to switch expert sets and which to load, guided by an option-critic approach with deliberation costs. FELA: A Multi-Agent Evolutionary System for Feature Engineering of Industrial Event Log Data
Authors: Kun Ouyang, Haoyu Wang, Dong Fang
First: 2025-10-29T06:57:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T03:39:54+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Event log data, recording fine-grained user actions and system events, represent one of the most valuable assets for modern digital services. However, the complexity and heterogeneity of industrial event logs--characterized by large scale, high dimensionality, diverse data types, and intricate temporal or relational structures--make feature engineering extremely challenging. Existing automatic feature engineering approaches, such as AutoML or genetic methods, often suffer from limited explainability, rigid predefined operations, and poor adaptability to complicated heterogeneous data. In this paper, we propose FELA (Feature Engineering LLM Agents), a multi-agent evolutionary system that autonomously extracts meaningful and high-performing features from complex industrial event log data. FELA integrates the reasoning and coding capabilities of large language models (LLMs) with an insight-guided self-evolution paradigm. Specifically, FELA employs specialized agents--Idea Agents, Code Agents, and Critic Agents--to collaboratively generate, validate, and implement novel feature ideas. An Evaluation Agent summarizes feedback and updates a hierarchical knowledge base and dual-memory system to enable continual improvement. Moreover, FELA introduces an agentic evolution algorithm, combining reinforcement learning and genetic algorithm principles to balance exploration and exploitation across the idea space. Extensive experiments on real industrial datasets demonstrate that FELA can generate explainable, domain-relevant features that significantly improve model performance while reducing manual effort. Our results highlight the potential of LLM-based multi-agent systems as a general framework for automated, interpretable, and adaptive feature engineering in complex real-world environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FELA：面向工业事件日志数据特征工程的多智能体进化系统
事件日志数据记录了细粒度的用户行为和系统事件，是现代数字服务中最有价值的资产之一。然而，工业事件日志的复杂性和异质性——表现为大规模、高维度、多样数据类型以及复杂的时间或关系结构——使得特征工程极具挑战性。现有的自动特征工程方法（如AutoML或遗传方法）通常存在可解释性有限、操作预定义僵化以及对复杂异构数据适应性差等问题。本文提出FELA（特征工程大语言模型智能体），一种多智能体进化系统，能够从复杂的工业事件日志数据中自主提取有意义且高性能的特征。FELA将大语言模型的推理与编码能力与洞察引导的自我进化范式相结合。具体而言，FELA采用专门智能体——创意智能体、代码智能体和评论智能体——协同生成、验证并实现新颖的特征创意。评估智能体汇总反馈并更新分层知识库与双记忆系统，以实现持续改进。此外，FELA引入智能体进化算法，结合强化学习与遗传算法原理，在创意空间中平衡探索与利用。在真实工业数据集上的大量实验表明，FELA能够生成可解释且与领域相关的特征，显著提升模型性能，同时减少人工投入。我们的结果凸显了基于大语言模型的多智能体系统作为复杂真实环境中自动化、可解释且自适应特征工程通用框架的潜力。

Toward Safe Autonomous Robotic Endovascular Interventions using World Models
Authors: Harry Robertshaw, Nikola Fischer, Han-Ru Wu, Andrea Walker Perez, Weiyuan Deng, Benjamin Jackson, Christos Bergeles, Alejandro Granados, Thomas C Booth
Venue: IROS
First: 2026-04-22T03:32:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T03:32:18+00:00
Comments: This manuscript is a preprint and has been submitted to the IEEE/RSJ International Conference on Intelligent Robots and Systems (IROS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous mechanical thrombectomy (MT) presents substantial challenges due to highly variable vascular geometries and the requirements for accurate, real-time control. While reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for the automation of endovascular navigation, existing approaches often show limited robustness when faced with diverse patient anatomies or extended navigation horizons. In this work, we investigate a world-model-based framework for autonomous endovascular navigation built on TD-MPC2, a model-based RL method that integrates planning and learned dynamics. We evaluate a TD-MPC2 agent trained on multiple navigation tasks across hold out patient-specific vasculatures and benchmark its performance against the state-of-the-art Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm agent. Both approaches are further validated in vitro using patient-specific vascular phantoms under fluoroscopic guidance. In simulation, TD-MPC2 demonstrates a significantly higher mean success rate than SAC (58% vs. 36%, p < 0.001), and mean tip contact forces of 0.15 N, well below the proposed 1.5 N vessel rupture threshold. Mean success rates for TD-MPC2 (68%) were comparable to SAC (60%) in vitro, but TD-MPC2 achieved superior path ratios (p = 0.017) at the cost of longer procedure times (p < 0.001). Together, these results provide the first demonstration of autonomous MT navigation validated across both hold out in silico data and fluoroscopy-guided in vitro experiments, highlighting the promise of world models for safe and generalizable AI-assisted endovascular interventions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于世界模型的安全自主机器人血管内介入治疗
