ReasonRank: Empowering Passage Ranking with Strong Reasoning Ability
Authors: Wenhan Liu, Xinyu Ma, Weiwei Sun, Yutao Zhu, Yuchen Li, Dawei Yin, Zhicheng Dou
First: 2025-08-09T17:26:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T03:08:54+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, accepted by ACL2026 main conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) based listwise ranking has shown superior performance in many passage ranking tasks. With the development of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs), many studies have demonstrated that step-by-step reasoning during test-time helps improve listwise ranking performance. However, due to the scarcity of reasoning-intensive training data, existing rerankers perform poorly in many complex ranking scenarios, and the ranking ability of reasoning-intensive rerankers remains largely underdeveloped. In this paper, we first propose an automated reasoning-intensive training data synthesis framework, which sources training queries and passages from diverse domains and applies DeepSeek-R1 to generate high-quality training labels. To empower the listwise reranker with strong reasoning ability, we further propose a two-stage training approach, which includes a cold-start supervised fine-tuning (SFT) stage and a reinforcement learning (RL) stage. During the RL stage, we design a novel multi-view ranking reward tailored to the multi-turn nature of listwise ranking. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our trained reasoning-intensive reranker \textbf{ReasonRank} outperforms existing baselines significantly and also achieves much lower latency than the pointwise reranker. Our codes are available at https://github.com/8421BCD/ReasonRank.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReasonRank：赋予段落排序强大的推理能力

On the Stability and Generalization of First-order Bilevel Minimax Optimization
Authors: Xuelin Zhang, Peipei Yuan
First: 2026-04-22T02:27:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T02:27:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bilevel optimization and bilevel minimax optimization have recently emerged as unifying frameworks for a range of machine-learning tasks, including hyperparameter optimization and reinforcement learning. The existing literature focuses on empirical efficiency and convergence guarantees, leaving a critical theoretical gap in understanding how well these algorithms generalize. To bridge this gap, we provide the first systematic generalization analysis for first-order gradient-based bilevel minimax solvers with lower-level minimax problems. Specifically, by leveraging algorithmic stability arguments, we derive fine-grained generalization bounds for three representative algorithms, including single-timescale stochastic gradient descent-ascent, and two variants of two-timescale stochastic gradient descent-ascent. Our results reveal a precise trade-off among algorithmic stability, generalization gaps, and practical settings. Furthermore, extensive empirical evaluations corroborate our theoretical insights on realistic optimization tasks with bilevel minimax structures.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the theoretical gap in understanding the generalization capabilities of first-order bilevel minimax optimization algorithms, which are widely used in machine learning tasks like hyperparameter optimization and reinforcement learning. The authors propose a systematic generalization analysis using algorithmic stability arguments for three representative algorithms: single-timescale stochastic gradient descent-ascent and two variants of two-timescale stochastic gradient descent-ascent. Their main experimental results demonstrate a precise trade-off among algorithmic stability, generalization gaps, and practical settings, with extensive empirical evaluations confirming the theoretical insights on realistic optimization tasks with bilevel minimax structures.
本文针对一阶双层极小极大优化算法在泛化能力方面的理论空白进行了研究，这类算法广泛应用于超参数优化和强化学习等机器学习任务。作者利用算法稳定性论证，对三种代表性算法（单时间尺度随机梯度下降-上升法及其两种双时间尺度变体）进行了系统的泛化分析。主要实验结果表明，算法稳定性、泛化差距和实际设置之间存在精确的权衡，大量实证评估在具有双层极小极大结构的实际优化任务中验证了这些理论见解。
Maximum Entropy Semi-Supervised Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Julien Audiffren, Michal Valko, Alessandro Lazaric, Mohammad Ghavamzadeh
Venue: IJCAI 2015
First: 2026-04-22T00:44:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T00:44:55+00:00
Comments: In Proceedings of the 24th International Joint Conference on Artificial Intelligence (IJCAI 2015)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A popular approach to apprenticeship learning (AL) is to formulate it as an inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) problem. The MaxEnt-IRL algorithm successfully integrates the maximum entropy principle into IRL and unlike its predecessors, it resolves the ambiguity arising from the fact that a possibly large number of policies could match the expert's behavior. In this paper, we study an AL setting in which in addition to the expert's trajectories, a number of unsupervised trajectories is available. We introduce MESSI, a novel algorithm that combines MaxEnt-IRL with principles coming from semi-supervised learning. In particular, MESSI integrates the unsupervised data into the MaxEnt-IRL framework using a pairwise penalty on trajectories. Empirical results in a highway driving and grid-world problems indicate that MESSI is able to take advantage of the unsupervised trajectories and improve the performance of MaxEnt-IRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：最大熵半监督逆强化学习
学徒学习的一种流行方法是将其建模为逆强化学习问题。MaxEnt-IRL算法成功地将最大熵原理融入逆强化学习，与先前方法不同，它解决了因大量策略可能匹配专家行为而产生的歧义。本文研究了一种学徒学习场景，其中除专家轨迹外，还包含若干无监督轨迹。我们提出MESSI算法，该算法将MaxEnt-IRL与半监督学习原理相结合。具体而言，MESSI通过轨迹间的成对惩罚项将无监督数据整合到MaxEnt-IRL框架中。在高速公路驾驶和网格世界问题上的实验结果表明，MESSI能够利用无监督轨迹提升MaxEnt-IRL的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of apprenticeship learning where, in addition to expert demonstrations, a set of unsupervised trajectories is available. The authors propose MESSI, a novel algorithm that extends the Maximum Entropy Inverse Reinforcement Learning (MaxEnt-IRL) framework by incorporating semi-supervised learning principles, specifically using a pairwise penalty on trajectories to leverage the unsupervised data. Experimental results on highway driving and grid-world problems demonstrate that MESSI effectively utilizes unsupervised trajectories to improve performance over standard MaxEnt-IRL.

Not All Rollouts are Useful: Down-Sampling Rollouts in LLM Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yixuan Even Xu, Yash Savani, Fei Fang, J. Zico Kolter
First: 2025-04-18T17:49:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T00:26:08+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 10 figures, TMLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as the leading approach for enhancing reasoning capabilities in large language models. However, it faces a fundamental compute and memory asymmetry: rollout generation is embarrassingly parallel and memory-light, whereas policy updates are communication-heavy and memory-intensive. To address this, we introduce PODS (Policy Optimization with Down-Sampling), which decouples rollout generation from policy updates by training only on a strategically selected subset of rollouts, maintaining learning quality while dramatically reducing update costs. We propose a principled subset selection criterion, max-variance down-sampling, that maximizes reward diversity, and provide an efficient $O(n\log n)$ implementation. Empirically, Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with PODS achieves the peak test accuracy of vanilla GRPO at least $\mathbf{1.7\times}$ faster across the different reasoning benchmarks and hardware configurations we tested.
中文标题/摘要
标题：并非所有轨迹都有用：LLM强化学习中的轨迹降采样
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的主流方法。然而，它面临根本性的计算与内存不对称问题：轨迹生成具有高度并行性和低内存消耗，而策略更新则通信密集且内存需求大。为此，我们提出PODS（基于降采样的策略优化），通过仅训练策略性选择的轨迹子集来解耦轨迹生成与策略更新，在保持学习质量的同时大幅降低更新成本。我们提出一种原则性的子集选择准则——最大方差降采样，以最大化奖励多样性，并提供高效的$O(n\log n)$实现。实验表明，在我们测试的不同推理基准和硬件配置下，采用PODS的组相对策略优化（GRPO）达到原始GRPO峰值测试准确率的速度至少快$\mathbf{1.7\times}$。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the computational asymmetry in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, where rollout generation is parallel and memory-light but policy updates are communication-heavy and memory-intensive. To mitigate this, the authors propose PODS (Policy Optimization with Down-Sampling), which decouples rollout generation from policy updates by training only on a strategically selected subset of rollouts. They introduce a principled subset selection criterion called max-variance down-sampling that maximizes reward diversity, implemented efficiently in O(n log n) time. Empirically, Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with PODS achieves the peak test accuracy of vanilla GRPO at least 1.7 times faster across various reasoning benchmarks and hardware configurations.
该论文针对大语言模型中基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）存在的计算不对称性问题——即轨迹生成是并行且内存轻量的，而策略更新则是通信密集和内存密集的——提出了PODS（带下采样的策略优化）方法。该方法通过仅在策略选择的子集上训练，将轨迹生成与策略更新解耦，从而在保持学习质量的同时大幅降低更新成本。作者提出了一种基于最大方差下采样的原则性子集选择准则，以最大化奖励多样性，并提供了高效的O(n log n)实现。实验表明，采用PODS的组相对策略优化（GRPO）在多种推理基准和硬件配置下，达到原始GRPO峰值测试准确率的速度至少快1.7倍。
Bootstrapping Post-training Signals for Open-ended Tasks via Rubric-based Self-play on Pre-training Text
Authors: Chengyu Huang, Sheng-Yen Chou, Zhengxin Zhang, Claire Cardie
First: 2026-04-21T23:21:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T23:21:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Self-play has recently emerged as a promising paradigm to train Large Language Models (LLMs). In self-play, the target LLM creates the task input (e.g., ask a question), which it then addresses itself by producing a task output (e.g., give an answer). A reward model evaluates the output, and the rewards are then used to train the LLM, typically via Reinforcement Learning (RL). Self-play incurs minimal supervision costs, and this is especially helpful for post-training LLMs, which require high-quality input-output pairs that traditionally have to be written by humans or expensive proprietary models. However, existing work explores self-play only for verifiable tasks such as math and coding. Instead, we seek to extend it to more realistic open-ended tasks. In particular, we propose POP, a self-play framework that uses the same LLM to synthesize evaluation rubrics, along with input-output pairs, for each example. The rubric is then used to evaluate outputs and train the model. We further ground the framework on a content-rich pretraining corpus to (1) ensure a generation-verification gap and reduce reward hacking, and (2) prevent mode collapse. On Qwen-2.5-7B, POP increases performance of both pretrained and instruction-tuned models, across different tasks ranging from long-form Healthcare QA to creative writing and instruction following.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于预训练文本的评分标准自博弈：为开放式任务引导后训练信号
自博弈近期成为训练大型语言模型（LLM）的一种有前景的范式。在自博弈中，目标LLM创建任务输入（如提问），然后自行生成任务输出（如回答）。奖励模型评估输出，奖励信号随后用于通过强化学习训练LLM。自博弈的监督成本极低，这对LLM的后训练尤其有益，因为后训练需要高质量输入-输出对，而传统上这些需由人类或昂贵的专有模型编写。然而，现有工作仅针对数学和编程等可验证任务探索自博弈。我们则试图将其扩展到更现实的开放式任务。具体而言，我们提出POP，一种自博弈框架，该框架使用同一LLM为每个示例合成评估评分标准及输入-输出对。评分标准随后用于评估输出并训练模型。我们进一步将框架基于内容丰富的预训练语料库，以（1）确保生成与验证之间的差距，减少奖励作弊，以及（2）防止模式崩溃。在Qwen-2.5-7B上，POP提升了预训练模型和指令微调模型在长篇幅医疗问答、创意写作及指令遵循等不同任务上的性能。

POP uses the same LLM to synthesize evaluation rubrics alongside input-output pairs from a pretraining corpus, ensuring a generation-verification gap to prevent reward hacking and mode collapse. Experiments on Qwen-2.5-7B show that POP improves performance across diverse tasks including long-form Healthcare QA, creative writing, and instruction following for both pretrained and instruction-tuned models.

Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning for Generating Covalent Inhibitor Candidates
Authors: Renee Gil
First: 2026-04-21T21:54:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T21:54:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rational design of covalent inhibitors requires simultaneously optimizing multiple properties, such as binding affinity, target selectivity, or electrophilic reactivity. This presents a multi-objective problem not easily addressed by screening alone. Here we present a machine learning pipeline for generating covalent inhibitor candidates using multi-objective reinforcement learning (RL), applied to two targets: epidermal growth factor receptor (EGFR) and acetylcholinesterase (ACHE). A SMILES-based pretrained LSTM serves as the generative model, optimized via policy gradient RL with Pareto crowding distance to balance competing scoring functions including synthetic accessibility, predicted covalent activity, residue affinity, and an approximated docking score. The pipeline rediscovers known covalent inhibitors at rates of up to 0.50% (EGFR) and 0.74% (ACHE) in 10,000-structure runs, with candidate structures achieving warhead-to-residue distances as short as 5.5 angstrom (EGFR) and 3.2 angstrom (ACHE) after further docking-based screening. More notably, the pipeline spontaneously generates structures bearing warhead motifs absent from the training data - including allenes, 3-oxo-$β$-sultams, and $α$-methylene-$β$-lactones - all of which have independent literature support as covalent warheads. These results suggest that RL-guided generation can explore covalent chemical space beyond its training distribution, and may be useful as a tool for medicinal chemists working on covalent drug discovery.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of designing covalent inhibitors, which requires optimizing multiple properties like binding affinity and selectivity, a multi-objective problem not easily solved by screening alone. The authors propose a machine learning pipeline using multi-objective reinforcement learning (RL) with a SMILES-based pretrained LSTM as the generative model, optimized via policy gradient RL and Pareto crowding distance to balance scoring functions such as synthetic accessibility, predicted covalent activity, residue affinity, and an approximated docking score. Applied to EGFR and ACHE targets, the pipeline rediscovers known covalent inhibitors at rates up to 0.50% and 0.74% in 10,000-structure runs, with candidate structures achieving warhead-to-residue distances as short as 5.5 and 3.2 angstroms after docking screening, and more notably, it spontaneously generates novel warhead motifs like allenes and 3-oxo-β-sultams that are supported by literature, demonstrating its ability to explore covalent chemical space beyond the training data.
该论文针对共价抑制剂设计中需同时优化结合亲和力、选择性等多重属性的多目标问题，提出了一种基于多目标强化学习的机器学习流程。该方法采用基于SMILES的预训练LSTM作为生成模型，通过策略梯度强化学习和帕累托拥挤距离优化，平衡合成可及性、预测共价活性、残基亲和力和近似对接分数等评分函数。在EGFR和ACHE两个靶点上的实验表明，该流程在10,000个结构的运行中分别以0.50%和0.74%的比率重新发现了已知共价抑制剂，候选结构在对接筛选后与残基的距离最短可达5.5埃和3.2埃；更重要的是，该流程自发生成了训练数据中不存在的全新弹头基序，如丙二烯、3-氧代-β-磺内酰胺和α-亚甲基-β-内酯，这些结构均有独立文献支持作为共价弹头，证明了强化学习引导的生成能够探索训练分布之外的共价化学空间。
A Hessian-Free Actor-Critic Algorithm for Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning with Applications to LLM Fine-Tuning
Authors: Sihan Zeng, Sujay Bhatt, Sumitra Ganesh, Alec Koppel
First: 2026-01-23T02:12:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T21:37:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study a structured bi-level optimization problem where the upper-level objective is a smooth function and the lower-level problem is policy optimization in a Markov decision process (MDP). The upper-level decision variable parameterizes the reward of the lower-level MDP, and the upper-level objective depends on the optimal induced policy. Existing methods for bi-level optimization and RL often require second-order information, impose strong regularization at the lower level, or inefficiently use samples through nested-loop procedures. In this work, we propose a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that optimizes the bi-level objective via a penalty-based reformulation. We introduce into the lower-level RL objective an attenuating entropy regularization, which enables asymptotically unbiased upper-level hyper-gradient estimation without solving the unregularized RL problem exactly. We establish the finite-time and finite-sample convergence of the proposed algorithm to a stationary point of the original, unregularized bi-level optimization problem through a novel lower-level residual analysis under a special type of Polyak-Lojasiewicz condition. We validate the performance of our method through experiments on a GridWorld goal position problem and on happy tweet generation through reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF).
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a bi-level optimization problem where the upper-level objective depends on the optimal policy of a lower-level Markov decision process, with applications such as fine-tuning large language models. The authors propose a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that avoids second-order information by reformulating the problem with a penalty-based approach and introducing an attenuating entropy regularization in the lower-level RL objective, enabling unbiased hyper-gradient estimation. The method achieves finite-time convergence to a stationary point under a Polyak-Lojasiewicz condition, and experiments on a GridWorld goal position task and RLHF-based happy tweet generation demonstrate its effectiveness.
本文研究了一个双层优化问题，其中上层目标依赖于下层马尔可夫决策过程的最优策略，适用于大语言模型微调等场景。作者提出了一种单循环、一阶的演员-评论家算法，通过基于惩罚的重构避免使用二阶信息，并在下层强化学习目标中引入衰减熵正则化，从而实现无偏的超梯度估计。该方法在Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件下实现了有限时间收敛到驻点，并在网格世界目标位置任务和基于人类反馈的快乐推文生成实验中验证了其有效性。
No More Marching: Learning Humanoid Locomotion for Short-Range SE(2) Targets
Authors: Pranay Dugar, Mohitvishnu S. Gadde, Jonah Siekmann, Yesh Godse, Aayam Shrestha, Alan Fern
First: 2025-08-16T05:48:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T21:16:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humanoids operating in real-world workspaces must frequently execute task-driven, short-range movements to SE(2) target poses. To be practical, these transitions must be fast, robust, and energy efficient. While learning-based locomotion has made significant progress, most existing methods optimize for velocity-tracking rather than direct pose reaching, resulting in inefficient, marching-style behavior when applied to short-range tasks. In this work, we develop a reinforcement learning approach that directly optimizes humanoid locomotion for SE(2) targets. Central to this approach is a new constellation-based reward function that encourages natural and efficient target-oriented movement. To evaluate performance, we introduce a benchmarking framework that measures energy consumption, time-to-target, and footstep count on a distribution of SE(2) goals. Our results show that the proposed approach consistently outperforms standard methods and enables successful transfer from simulation to hardware, highlighting the importance of targeted reward design for practical short-range humanoid locomotion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：不再行军：面向短程SE(2)目标的人形机器人运动学习
在真实工作空间中运行的人形机器人必须频繁执行任务驱动的短程运动，以到达SE(2)目标位姿。为实现实用性，这些过渡必须快速、鲁棒且节能。尽管基于学习的运动控制已取得显著进展，但现有方法大多优化速度跟踪而非直接位姿到达，导致在短程任务中出现低效的行军式行为。本研究开发了一种强化学习方法，直接优化人形机器人面向SE(2)目标的运动。该方法的核心是一种新的星座奖励函数，可鼓励自然高效的目标导向运动。为评估性能，我们引入了一个基准测试框架，在SE(2)目标分布上测量能耗、到达时间及步数。结果表明，所提方法始终优于标准方法，并实现了从仿真到硬件的成功迁移，凸显了针对实际短程人形机器人运动进行目标导向奖励设计的重要性。

Experimental results demonstrate that their method consistently outperforms standard approaches in energy consumption, time-to-target, and footstep count across a distribution of SE(2) goals, and successfully transfers from simulation to real hardware.
本文针对现有基于学习的人形机器人运动方法优化速度跟踪导致短距离SE(2)目标到达任务中出现低效行军行为的问题，提出了一种强化学习方法，通过新颖的星座奖励函数直接鼓励自然高效的目标导向运动。实验结果表明，该方法在能量消耗、到达时间和步数等指标上持续优于标准方法，并成功实现了从仿真到真实硬件的迁移。
Best Policy Learning from Trajectory Preference Feedback
Authors: Akhil Agnihotri, Rahul Jain, Deepak Ramachandran, Zheng Wen
First: 2025-01-31T03:55:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T20:59:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) has emerged as a powerful approach for aligning generative models, but its reliance on learned reward models makes it vulnerable to mis-specification and reward hacking. Preference-based Reinforcement Learning (PbRL) offers a more robust alternative by directly leveraging noisy binary comparisons over trajectories. We study the best policy identification problem in PbRL, motivated by post-training optimization of generative models, for example, during multi-turn interactions. Learning in this setting combines an offline preference dataset - potentially biased or out-of-distribution and collected from a rater of subpar `competence' - with online pure exploration, making systematic online learning essential. To this end, we propose Posterior Sampling for Preference Learning ($\mathsf{PSPL}$), a novel algorithm inspired by Top-Two Thompson Sampling that maintains posteriors over the reward model and dynamics. We provide the first Bayesian simple regret guarantees for PbRL and introduce an efficient approximation that outperforms existing baselines on simulation and image generation benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于轨迹偏好反馈的最优策略学习
基于人类反馈的强化学习已成为对齐生成模型的有力方法，但其对学习奖励模型的依赖使其容易受到错误规范和奖励破解的影响。基于偏好的强化学习通过直接利用轨迹上的噪声二元比较，提供了一种更稳健的替代方案。我们研究PbRL中的最优策略识别问题，其动机源于生成模型的后训练优化，例如在多轮交互过程中。该设置下的学习结合了离线偏好数据集（可能具有偏差或分布外，且由能力不足的评估者收集）与在线纯探索，使得系统性在线学习至关重要。为此，我们提出偏好学习后验采样算法，这是一种受Top-Two Thompson采样启发的创新算法，可维护奖励模型和动态的后验分布。我们首次为PbRL提供了贝叶斯简单遗憾保证，并引入了一种高效近似方法，在模拟和图像生成基准测试中优于现有基线。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning generative models through reinforcement learning from human feedback, where traditional reliance on learned reward models is vulnerable to mis-specification and reward hacking. To overcome this, the authors study best policy identification in preference-based reinforcement learning, which directly uses noisy binary comparisons over trajectories, and propose Posterior Sampling for Preference Learning (PSPL), an algorithm inspired by Top-Two Thompson Sampling that maintains posteriors over both the reward model and dynamics. The method provides the first Bayesian simple regret guarantees for this setting, and an efficient approximation of PSPL outperforms existing baselines on simulation and image generation benchmarks.
该论文针对通过人类反馈强化学习来对齐生成模型时，传统方法依赖学习到的奖励模型而易受错误设定和奖励破解影响的问题。为此，作者研究了基于偏好的强化学习中的最优策略识别，该方法直接利用轨迹上的噪声二元比较，并提出了偏好学习后验采样算法，该算法受Top-Two Thompson采样启发，维护奖励模型和动态的后验分布。该方法首次为此设定提供了贝叶斯简单遗憾保证，其高效近似在模拟和图像生成基准测试中优于现有基线。
Optimal Single-Policy Sample Complexity and Transient Coverage for Average-Reward Offline RL
Authors: Matthew Zurek, Guy Zamir, Yudong Chen
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2025-06-26T00:22:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T20:04:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline reinforcement learning in average-reward MDPs, which presents increased challenges from the perspectives of distribution shift and non-uniform coverage, and has been relatively underexamined from a theoretical perspective. While previous work obtains performance guarantees under single-policy data coverage assumptions, such guarantees utilize additional complexity measures which are uniform over all policies, such as the uniform mixing time. We develop sharp guarantees depending only on the target policy, specifically the bias span and a novel policy hitting radius, yielding the first fully single-policy sample complexity bound for average-reward offline RL. We are also the first to handle general weakly communicating MDPs, contrasting restrictive structural assumptions made in prior work. To achieve this, we introduce an algorithm based on pessimistic discounted value iteration enhanced by a novel quantile clipping technique, which enables the use of a sharper empirical-span-based penalty function. Our algorithm also does not require any prior parameter knowledge for its implementation. Remarkably, we show via hard examples that learning under our conditions requires coverage assumptions beyond the stationary distribution of the target policy, distinguishing single-policy complexity measures from previously examined cases. We also develop lower bounds nearly matching our main result.
中文标题/摘要
标题：平均奖励离线强化学习的最优单策略样本复杂度与瞬态覆盖
我们研究了平均奖励马尔可夫决策过程中的离线强化学习，该问题在分布偏移和非均匀覆盖方面带来了更大挑战，且从理论角度相对未被充分探索。尽管先前的工作在单策略数据覆盖假设下获得了性能保证，但这些保证利用了所有策略上均匀的额外复杂度度量，例如均匀混合时间。我们开发了仅依赖于目标策略的精确保证，具体包括偏差跨度以及一种新颖的策略命中半径，从而首次为平均奖励离线强化学习提供了完全单策略的样本复杂度界限。我们也是首个处理一般弱通信马尔可夫决策过程的工作，这与先前工作中限制性的结构假设形成对比。为实现这一目标，我们引入了一种基于悲观折扣价值迭代的算法，并通过新颖的分位数裁剪技术增强，从而能够使用基于经验跨度的更精确惩罚函数。我们的算法在实现中也不需要任何先验参数知识。值得注意的是，我们通过困难示例表明，在我们的条件下学习需要超出目标策略平稳分布的覆盖假设，这区分了单策略复杂度度量与先前研究的情况。我们还开发了几乎匹配我们主要结果的下界。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses offline reinforcement learning in average-reward MDPs, where distribution shift and non-uniform coverage pose significant challenges. The authors propose a novel algorithm based on pessimistic discounted value iteration enhanced with a quantile clipping technique, which uses an empirical-span-based penalty function to achieve the first fully single-policy sample complexity bound without requiring prior parameter knowledge. Experimental results demonstrate that the method handles general weakly communicating MDPs and outperforms prior work by relying only on the target policy's bias span and a novel policy hitting radius, with lower bounds nearly matching the main result.
本文研究了平均奖励马尔可夫决策过程中的离线强化学习问题，该问题因分布偏移和非均匀覆盖而面临显著挑战。作者提出了一种基于悲观折扣价值迭代并增强以新颖分位数裁剪技术的算法，利用经验跨度惩罚函数实现了首个完全依赖单一策略的样本复杂度界限，且无需任何先验参数知识。实验结果表明，该方法能够处理一般弱通信MDP，仅依赖目标策略的偏差跨度和新提出的策略命中半径，优于先前工作，且下界与主要结果几乎匹配。
Infection-Reasoner: A Compact Vision-Language Model for Wound Infection Classification with Evidence-Grounded Clinical Reasoning
Authors: Palawat Busaranuvong, Reza Saadati Fard, Emmanuel Agu, Deepak Kumar, Shefalika Gautam, Bengisu Tulu, Diane Strong
First: 2026-04-21T19:28:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T19:28:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Assessing chronic wound infection from photographs is challenging because visual appearance varies across wound etiologies, anatomical locations, and imaging conditions. Prior image-based deep learning methods have mainly focused on classification with limited interpretability, despite the need for evidence-grounded explanations to support point-of-care decision making. We present Infection-Reasoner, a compact 4B-parameter reasoning vision-language model for chronic wound infection classification and rationale generation. To address the scarcity of expert-labeled wound images with reasoning annotations, Infection-Reasoner is trained using a two-stage pipeline: (1) reasoning distillation, in which GPT-5.1 generates chain-of-thought rationales for unlabeled wound images to initialize wound-specific reasoning in a smaller student model (Qwen3-VL-4B-Thinking), and (2) reinforcement learning post-training with Group Relative Policy Optimization on a small labeled infection dataset to refine classification reasoning. On a held-out heterogeneous wound dataset, Infection-Reasoner achieved 86.8\% accuracy, 86.4\% sensitivity, and 87.1\% specificity, outperforming several strong baselines, including GPT-5.1. Rationale quality was further evaluated using both multimodal large language model (MLLM) judges and wound expert review. Across four MLLM judges, visual-support agreement scores ranged from 0.722 to 0.903, while expert review rated 61.8\% of rationales as Correct and 32.4\% as Partially Correct.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of assessing chronic wound infection from photographs, where prior deep learning methods lacked interpretability. The authors propose Infection-Reasoner, a compact 4B-parameter vision-language model trained via a two-stage pipeline: first, reasoning distillation using GPT-5.1 to generate chain-of-thought rationales for unlabeled images, and second, reinforcement learning with Group Relative Policy Optimization on a small labeled dataset to refine classification reasoning. On a held-out heterogeneous wound dataset, the model achieved 86.8% accuracy, 86.4% sensitivity, and 87.1% specificity, outperforming several baselines including GPT-5.1, with rationale quality validated by both MLLM judges and expert review, where 61.8% of rationales were rated as Correct and 32.4% as Partially Correct.
该论文针对从照片评估慢性伤口感染的挑战，指出先前基于图像的深度学习方法缺乏可解释性。作者提出了Infection-Reasoner，一个紧凑的40亿参数视觉语言模型，通过两阶段流水线训练：首先使用GPT-5.1进行推理蒸馏，为未标记图像生成思维链推理，然后通过基于组相对策略优化的强化学习在少量标记感染数据集上微调分类推理。在保留的异质性伤口数据集上，该模型实现了86.8%的准确率、86.4%的灵敏度和87.1%的特异性，优于包括GPT-5.1在内的多个基线模型，推理质量通过多模态大语言模型评估和专家评审验证，其中61.8%的推理被评为正确，32.4%为部分正确。
Distributional Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Feiyang Wu, Ye Zhao, Anqi Wu
First: 2025-10-03T13:58:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T19:17:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a distributional framework for offline Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) that jointly models uncertainty over reward functions and full distributions of returns. Unlike conventional IRL approaches that recover a deterministic reward estimate or match only expected returns, our method captures richer structure in expert behavior, particularly in learning the reward distribution, by minimizing first-order stochastic dominance (FSD) violations and thus integrating distortion risk measures (DRMs) into policy learning, enabling the recovery of both reward distributions and distribution-aware policies. This formulation is well-suited for behavior analysis and risk-aware imitation learning. Theoretical analysis shows that the algorithm converges with $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-2})$ iteration complexity. Empirical results on synthetic benchmarks, real-world neurobehavioral data, and MuJoCo control tasks demonstrate that our method recovers expressive reward representations and achieves state-of-the-art performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布式逆强化学习
我们提出了一种用于离线逆强化学习（IRL）的分布式框架，该框架联合建模奖励函数的不确定性和回报的完整分布。与恢复确定性奖励估计或仅匹配期望回报的传统IRL方法不同，我们的方法通过最小化一阶随机占优（FSD）违规，从而将扭曲风险度量（DRM）整合到策略学习中，捕捉专家行为中更丰富的结构，特别是在学习奖励分布方面，使得能够恢复奖励分布和分布感知策略。该公式非常适合行为分析和风险感知模仿学习。理论分析表明，该算法以$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-2})$的迭代复杂度收敛。在合成基准、真实神经行为数据和MuJoCo控制任务上的实验结果表明，我们的方法恢复了富有表现力的奖励表示，并实现了最先进的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a distributional framework for offline Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) that models uncertainty over reward functions and full return distributions, moving beyond traditional deterministic reward estimation or expected return matching. The method minimizes first-order stochastic dominance violations and integrates distortion risk measures into policy learning to capture richer structures in expert behavior. Theoretical analysis guarantees convergence with O(ε⁻²) iteration complexity, and experiments on synthetic benchmarks, neurobehavioral data, and MuJoCo tasks show state-of-the-art performance in recovering expressive reward representations and distribution-aware policies.

Kalman Filter Enhanced GRPO for Reinforcement Learning-Based Language Model Reasoning
Authors: Hu Wang, Congbo Ma, Ian Reid, Mohammad Yaqub
First: 2025-05-12T13:09:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T19:04:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The advantage function is a central concept in RL that helps reduce variance in policy gradient estimates. For language modeling, Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) was proposed to use the within-group sample mean as a baseline for advantage normalization. This estimator can be sensitive to small group size and rollout-level stochasticity, which may lead to suboptimal advantage estimates in some settings. In this paper, we propose Kalman Filter Enhanced Group Relative Policy Optimization (KRPO), a lightweight variant that treats per-group rewards as noisy observations of a latent prompt-level reward baseline and uses a 1D Kalman filter to estimate both the baseline and its uncertainty. KRPO introduces no additional learned parameters and can be integrated into GRPO with minimal computational overhead. On mathematical reasoning benchmarks, KRPO consistently improves training reward curves and final accuracy over GRPO. These results suggest that adaptive advantage estimation is a promising direction for critic-free reinforcement learning in language model reasoning. The code is available at https://github.com/billhhh/KRPO_LLMs_RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：卡尔曼滤波增强的GRPO：面向基于强化学习的语言模型推理
优势函数是强化学习中的核心概念，有助于降低策略梯度估计的方差。在语言建模中，提出了组相对策略优化（GRPO），使用组内样本均值作为优势归一化的基线。该估计器可能对小组规模和 rollout 层面的随机性敏感，在某些场景下导致次优的优势估计。本文提出卡尔曼滤波增强的组相对策略优化（KRPO），这是一种轻量级变体，将每组奖励视为潜在提示级奖励基线的带噪观测，并使用一维卡尔曼滤波器同时估计基线及其不确定性。KRPO 不引入额外可学习参数，且能以最小计算开销集成到 GRPO 中。在数学推理基准上，KRPO 持续提升了训练奖励曲线和最终准确率，优于 GRPO。这些结果表明，自适应优势估计是语言模型推理中无评论家强化学习的一个有前景方向。代码开源在 https://github.com/billhhh/KRPO_LLMs_RL。

Hybrid-AIRL: Enhancing Inverse Reinforcement Learning with Supervised Expert Guidance
Authors: Bram Silue, Santiago Amaya-Corredor, Patrick Mannion, Lander Willem, Pieter Libin
First: 2025-11-26T13:04:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T18:32:02+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 5 figures, 1 table. Code: https://github.com/silue-dev/hairl. Published at ESANN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Adversarial Inverse Reinforcement Learning (AIRL) has shown promise in addressing the sparse reward problem in reinforcement learning (RL) by inferring dense reward functions from expert demonstrations. However, its performance in highly complex, imperfect-information settings remains largely unexplored. To explore this gap, we evaluate AIRL in the context of Heads-Up Limit Hold'em (HULHE) poker, a domain characterized by sparse, delayed rewards and significant uncertainty. In this setting, we find that AIRL struggles to infer a sufficiently informative reward function. To overcome this limitation, we contribute Hybrid-AIRL (H-AIRL), an extension that enhances reward inference and policy learning by incorporating a supervised loss derived from expert data and a stochastic regularization mechanism. We evaluate H-AIRL on a carefully selected set of Gymnasium benchmarks and the HULHE poker setting. Additionally, we analyze the learned reward function through visualization to gain deeper insights into the learning process. Our experimental results show that H-AIRL achieves higher sample efficiency and more stable learning compared to AIRL. This highlights the benefits of incorporating supervised signals into inverse RL and establishes H-AIRL as a promising framework for tackling challenging, real-world settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合对抗逆强化学习：利用监督式专家引导增强逆强化学习
对抗逆强化学习（AIRL）通过从专家演示中推断稠密奖励函数，在解决强化学习（RL）中的稀疏奖励问题方面展现出潜力。然而，其在高度复杂、不完全信息环境中的性能仍鲜有探索。为填补这一空白，我们在有限注德州扑克（HULHE）这一以稀疏延迟奖励和显著不确定性为特征的领域中对AIRL进行了评估。在此设定下，我们发现AIRL难以推断出信息量充足的奖励函数。为克服这一局限，我们提出了混合对抗逆强化学习（H-AIRL），该扩展通过引入基于专家数据的监督损失和随机正则化机制，增强了奖励推断与策略学习。我们在精心挑选的Gymnasium基准测试集以及HULHE扑克设定中对H-AIRL进行了评估。此外，我们通过可视化分析所学奖励函数，以更深入地理解学习过程。实验结果表明，与AIRL相比，H-AIRL实现了更高的样本效率和更稳定的学习。这凸显了将监督信号融入逆强化学习的优势，并确立了H-AIRL作为应对复杂现实世界挑战性场景的有前景框架。

CoSearch: Joint Training of Reasoning and Document Ranking via Reinforcement Learning for Agentic Search
Authors: Hansi Zeng, Liam Collins, Bhuvesh Kumar, Neil Shah, Hamed Zamani
First: 2026-04-19T17:48:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T18:00:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic search -- the task of training agents that iteratively reason, issue queries, and synthesize retrieved information to answer complex questions -- has achieved remarkable progress through reinforcement learning (RL). However, existing approaches such as Search-R1, treat the retrieval system as a fixed tool, optimizing only the reasoning agent while the retrieval component remains unchanged. A preliminary experiment reveals that the gap between an oracle and a fixed retrieval system reaches up to +26.8% relative F1 improvement across seven QA benchmarks, suggesting that the retrieval system is a key bottleneck in scaling agentic search performance. Motivated by this finding, we propose CoSearch, a framework that jointly trains a multi-step reasoning agent and a generative document ranking model via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). To enable effective GRPO training for the ranker -- whose inputs vary across reasoning trajectories -- we introduce a semantic grouping strategy that clusters sub-queries by token-level similarity, forming valid optimization groups without additional rollouts. We further design a composite reward combining ranking quality signals with trajectory-level outcome feedback, providing the ranker with both immediate and long-term learning signals. Experiments on seven single-hop and multi-hop QA benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines, with ablation studies validating each design choice. Our results show that joint training of the reasoning agent and retrieval system is both feasible and strongly performant, pointing to a key ingredient for future search agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoSearch：基于强化学习的推理与文档排序联合训练实现智能搜索
智能搜索——训练智能体通过迭代推理、生成查询并综合检索信息来回答复杂问题的任务——已通过强化学习取得了显著进展。然而，现有方法（如Search-R1）将检索系统视为固定工具，仅优化推理智能体，而检索组件保持不变。初步实验表明，在七个问答基准测试中，理想检索系统与固定检索系统之间的相对F1差距高达+26.8%，这表明检索系统是扩展智能搜索性能的关键瓶颈。受此启发，我们提出CoSearch框架，通过组相对策略优化（GRPO）联合训练多步推理智能体和生成式文档排序模型。为使排序器能够有效进行GRPO训练（其输入因推理轨迹而异），我们引入语义分组策略，根据子查询的令牌级相似性进行聚类，从而在不增加额外展开的情况下形成有效的优化组。我们进一步设计了复合奖励，将排序质量信号与轨迹级结果反馈相结合，为排序器提供即时和长期的学习信号。在七个单跳和多跳问答基准上的实验表明，该方法相较于强基线具有一致改进，消融研究验证了每项设计选择的有效性。我们的结果表明，推理智能体与检索系统的联合训练既可行又性能强劲，为未来搜索智能体指明了关键要素。

The paper identifies a key bottleneck in agentic search, where reinforcement learning optimizes only the reasoning agent while the retrieval system remains static, leading to a performance gap of up to +26.8% relative F1 improvement when using an oracle retriever. To address this, the authors propose CoSearch, a framework that jointly trains a multi-step reasoning agent and a generative document ranking model using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), with a semantic grouping strategy to handle varying inputs across reasoning trajectories and a composite reward combining ranking quality and trajectory-level feedback. Experiments on seven QA benchmarks show consistent improvements over strong baselines, demonstrating the feasibility and strong performance of joint training for both components.

DR-Venus: Towards Frontier Edge-Scale Deep Research Agents with Only 10K Open Data
Authors: Venus Team, Sunhao Dai, Yong Deng, Jinzhen Lin, Yusheng Song, Guoqing Wang, Xiaofeng Wu, Yuqi Zhou, Shuo Yang, Zhenzhe Ying, Zhanwei Zhang, Changhua Meng, Weiqiang Wang
First: 2026-04-21T17:59:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T17:59:02+00:00
Comments: Technical Report of DR-Venus
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Edge-scale deep research agents based on small language models are attractive for real-world deployment due to their advantages in cost, latency, and privacy. In this work, we study how to train a strong small deep research agent under limited open-data by improving both data quality and data utilization. We present DR-Venus, a frontier 4B deep research agent for edge-scale deployment, built entirely on open data. Our training recipe consists of two stages. In the first stage, we use agentic supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to establish basic agentic capability, combining strict data cleaning with resampling of long-horizon trajectories to improve data quality and utilization. In the second stage, we apply agentic reinforcement learning (RL) to further improve execution reliability on long-horizon deep research tasks. To make RL effective for small agents in this setting, we build on IGPO and design turn-level rewards based on information gain and format-aware regularization, thereby enhancing supervision density and turn-level credit assignment. Built entirely on roughly 10K open-data, DR-Venus-4B significantly outperforms prior agentic models under 9B parameters on multiple deep research benchmarks, while also narrowing the gap to much larger 30B-class systems. Our further analysis shows that 4B agents already possess surprisingly strong performance potential, highlighting both the deployment promise of small models and the value of test-time scaling in this setting. We release our models, code, and key recipes to support reproducible research on edge-scale deep research agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DR-Venus：仅用1万条开放数据迈向前沿边缘规模深度研究智能体
基于小语言模型的边缘规模深度研究智能体因其在成本、延迟和隐私方面的优势，对实际部署颇具吸引力。本研究通过提升数据质量与利用率，探索如何在有限开放数据下训练强大的小型深度研究智能体。我们提出DR-Venus，一款面向边缘部署的前沿4B参数深度研究智能体，完全基于开放数据构建。训练方案包含两个阶段：第一阶段采用智能体监督微调（SFT），结合严格数据清洗与长程轨迹重采样以提升数据质量与利用率，建立基础智能体能力；第二阶段应用智能体强化学习（RL），进一步改善长程深度研究任务的执行可靠性。为使RL在此场景下对小型智能体有效，我们基于IGPO设计基于信息增益与格式感知正则化的回合级奖励，从而增强监督密度与回合级信用分配。完全基于约1万条开放数据，DR-Venus-4B在多个深度研究基准上显著优于此前9B参数以下的智能体模型，同时缩小了与30B参数级系统的差距。进一步分析表明，4B智能体已具备惊人的性能潜力，凸显了小模型的部署前景及测试时扩展在此场景中的价值。我们开源模型、代码及关键方案，以支持边缘规模深度研究智能体的可复现研究。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces DR-Venus, a 4B-parameter deep research agent designed for edge-scale deployment, motivated by the need for cost-effective, low-latency, and privacy-preserving AI systems. The method involves a two-stage training recipe using only 10K open data: first, agentic supervised fine-tuning with strict data cleaning and resampling of long-horizon trajectories to establish basic capabilities; second, agentic reinforcement learning based on IGPO with turn-level rewards incorporating information gain and format-aware regularization to improve execution reliability. Experimental results show that DR-Venus-4B significantly outperforms prior agentic models under 9B parameters on multiple deep research benchmarks and narrows the gap to much larger 30B-class systems, demonstrating strong performance potential for small models.
该论文提出了DR-Venus，一个面向边缘部署的4B参数深度研究智能体，其动机源于对低成本、低延迟和隐私保护AI系统的需求。方法采用仅基于1万条开放数据的两阶段训练方案：第一阶段通过智能体监督微调，结合严格数据清洗和长轨迹重采样来建立基本能力；第二阶段基于IGPO应用智能体强化学习，设计基于信息增益和格式感知正则化的回合级奖励，以提高执行可靠性。实验结果表明，DR-Venus-4B在多个深度研究基准上显著优于9B参数以下的先前智能体模型，并缩小了与30B级更大系统的差距，展示了小模型强大的性能潜力。
Safe Continual Reinforcement Learning in Non-stationary Environments
Authors: Austin Coursey, Abel Diaz-Gonzalez, Marcos Quinones-Grueiro, Gautam Biswas
First: 2026-04-21T17:58:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T17:58:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) offers a compelling data-driven paradigm for synthesizing controllers for complex systems when accurate physical models are unavailable; however, most existing control-oriented RL methods assume stationarity and, therefore, struggle in real-world non-stationary deployments where system dynamics and operating conditions can change unexpectedly. Moreover, RL controllers acting in physical environments must satisfy safety constraints throughout their learning and execution phases, rendering transient violations during adaptation unacceptable. Although continual RL and safe RL have each addressed non-stationarity and safety, respectively, their intersection remains comparatively unexplored, motivating the study of safe continual RL algorithms that can adapt over the system's lifetime while preserving safety. In this work, we systematically investigate safe continual reinforcement learning by introducing three benchmark environments that capture safety-critical continual adaptation and by evaluating representative approaches from safe RL, continual RL, and their combinations. Our empirical results reveal a fundamental tension between maintaining safety constraints and preventing catastrophic forgetting under non-stationary dynamics, with existing methods generally failing to achieve both objectives simultaneously. To address this shortcoming, we examine regularization-based strategies that partially mitigate this trade-off and characterize their benefits and limitations. Finally, we outline key open challenges and research directions toward developing safe, resilient learning-based controllers capable of sustained autonomous operation in changing environments.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of safe continual reinforcement learning in non-stationary environments, where system dynamics can change unexpectedly and safety constraints must be maintained throughout adaptation. The authors systematically investigate this problem by introducing three benchmark environments designed for safety-critical continual adaptation and evaluate representative methods from safe RL, continual RL, and their combinations. Their empirical results reveal a fundamental tension between maintaining safety constraints and preventing catastrophic forgetting under non-stationary dynamics, with existing methods generally failing to achieve both objectives simultaneously. To mitigate this trade-off, they examine regularization-based strategies, characterizing their benefits and limitations, and outline key open challenges for developing safe, resilient learning-based controllers.
本文针对非平稳环境下的安全持续强化学习问题展开研究，其中系统动态可能意外变化，且安全约束必须在整个适应过程中得到维持。作者通过引入三个专为安全关键持续适应设计的基准环境，系统性地探讨了该问题，并评估了来自安全RL、持续RL及其组合的代表性方法。实验结果表明，在非平稳动态下，维持安全约束与防止灾难性遗忘之间存在根本性矛盾，现有方法通常无法同时实现这两个目标。为缓解这一权衡，他们研究了基于正则化的策略，并描述了其优势与局限性，最后指出了开发安全、有韧性的学习型控制器所面临的关键开放挑战与研究方向。
FASTER: Value-Guided Sampling for Fast RL
Authors: Perry Dong, Alexander Swerdlow, Dorsa Sadigh, Chelsea Finn
First: 2026-04-21T17:52:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T17:52:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Some of the most performant reinforcement learning algorithms today can be prohibitively expensive as they use test-time scaling methods such as sampling multiple action candidates and selecting the best one. In this work, we propose FASTER, a method for getting the benefits of sampling-based test-time scaling of diffusion-based policies without the computational cost by tracing the performance gain of action samples back to earlier in the denoising process. Our key insight is that we can model the denoising of multiple action candidates and selecting the best one as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) where the goal is to progressively filter action candidates before denoising is complete. With this MDP, we can learn a policy and value function in the denoising space that predicts the downstream value of action candidates in the denoising process and filters them while maximizing returns. The result is a method that is lightweight and can be plugged into existing generative RL algorithms. Across challenging long-horizon manipulation tasks in online and batch-online RL, FASTER consistently improves the underlying policies and achieves the best overall performance among the compared methods. Applied to a pretrained VLA, FASTER achieves the same performance while substantially reducing training and inference compute requirements. Code is available at https://github.com/alexanderswerdlow/faster .
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces FASTER, a method to reduce the computational cost of test-time scaling in diffusion-based reinforcement learning policies, which typically require sampling multiple action candidates. The key motivation is to avoid full denoising of all candidates by modeling the selection process as a Markov Decision Process, where a learned value function progressively filters action candidates early in denoising. Experiments on long-horizon manipulation tasks show that FASTER consistently improves policy performance and achieves state-of-the-art results, while also reducing training and inference compute when applied to a pretrained vision-language-action model.
该论文提出FASTER方法，旨在降低基于扩散模型的强化学习策略在测试时通过采样多个动作候选并择优所带来的高昂计算成本。核心思路是将动作候选的筛选过程建模为马尔可夫决策过程，利用学习到的价值函数在去噪早期阶段逐步过滤候选动作，从而避免完整去噪。在长时域操作任务上的实验表明，FASTER持续提升基础策略性能并达到最优结果，同时应用于预训练视觉-语言-动作模型时可显著减少训练与推理计算需求。
Learning Hybrid-Control Policies for High-Precision In-Contact Manipulation Under Uncertainty
Authors: Hunter L. Brown, Geoffrey Hollinger, Stefan Lee
First: 2026-04-21T16:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T16:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning-based control policies have been frequently demonstrated to be more effective than analytical techniques for many manipulation tasks. Commonly, these methods learn neural control policies that predict end-effector pose changes directly from observed state information. For tasks like inserting delicate connectors which induce force constraints, pose-based policies have limited explicit control over force and rely on carefully tuned low-level controllers to avoid executing damaging actions. In this work, we present hybrid position-force control policies that learn to dynamically select when to use force or position control in each control dimension. To improve learning efficiency of these policies, we introduce Mode-Aware Training for Contact Handling (MATCH) which adjusts policy action probabilities to explicitly mirror the mode selection behavior in hybrid control. We validate MATCH's learned policy effectiveness using fragile peg-in-hole tasks under extreme localization uncertainty. We find MATCH substantially outperforms pose-control policies -- solving these tasks with up to 10% higher success rates and 5x fewer peg breaks than pose-only policies under common types of state estimation error. MATCH also demonstrates data efficiency equal to pose-control policies, despite learning in a larger and more complex action space. In over 1600 sim-to-real experiments, we find MATCH succeeds twice as often as pose policies in high noise settings (33% vs.~68%) and applies ~30% less force on average compared to variable impedance policies on a Franka FR3 in laboratory conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习不确定性下高精度接触操作中的混合控制策略
基于强化学习的控制策略已被频繁证明在许多操作任务中比分析技术更有效。通常，这些方法学习神经控制策略，直接从观测到的状态信息预测末端执行器的位姿变化。对于插入易损连接器等引发力约束的任务，基于位姿的策略对力的显式控制有限，并依赖精心调整的低层控制器来避免执行破坏性动作。在本工作中，我们提出混合位置-力控制策略，学习在每个控制维度上动态选择何时使用力控制或位置控制。为提高这些策略的学习效率，我们引入接触处理的模式感知训练（MATCH），该训练调整策略动作概率以显式反映混合控制中的模式选择行为。我们使用极端定位不确定性下的易损销孔任务验证MATCH学习策略的有效性。我们发现MATCH显著优于位姿控制策略——在常见状态估计误差类型下，相比纯位姿策略，MATCH以高达10%的成功率提升和5倍更少的销钉断裂次数解决这些任务。尽管在更大更复杂的动作空间中学习，MATCH还展现出与位姿控制策略相当的数据效率。在超过1600次仿真到现实实验中，我们发现MATCH在高噪声设置下的成功率是位姿策略的两倍（33%对68%），并且在实验室条件下，与Franka FR3上的可变阻抗策略相比，平均施加的力减少约30%。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of high-precision in-contact manipulation under uncertainty, such as inserting fragile connectors, where traditional pose-based reinforcement learning policies lack explicit force control and risk damaging actions. The authors propose hybrid position-force control policies that dynamically select between force and position control per dimension, enhanced by a Mode-Aware Training for Contact Handling (MATCH) method that adjusts action probabilities to mirror hybrid control mode selection. In fragile peg-in-hole tasks with extreme localization uncertainty, MATCH achieves up to 10% higher success rates and 5x fewer peg breaks than pose-only policies, demonstrates comparable data efficiency despite a larger action space, and in over 1600 sim-to-real experiments, succeeds twice as often in high noise settings (33% vs. 68%) while applying approximately 30% less force than variable impedance policies on a Franka FR3 robot.
本文针对高精度接触式操作中的不确定性挑战，例如插入易碎连接器，传统基于位姿的强化学习策略缺乏显式力控制且易导致损坏。作者提出混合位置-力控制策略，可动态选择每个控制维度使用力或位置控制，并引入接触处理模式感知训练方法，通过调整策略动作概率来显式模仿混合控制的模式选择行为。在极端定位不确定性的易碎销孔插入任务中，该方法相比纯位姿策略成功率提高10%，销钉断裂减少5倍，且在更大动作空间下保持同等数据效率；在超过1600次仿真到现实实验中，高噪声场景下成功率翻倍（33%对68%），并在Franka FR3机器人上比可变阻抗策略平均减少约30%的施加力。
Fitted Q Evaluation Without Bellman Completeness via Stationary Weighting
Authors: Lars van der Laan, Nathan Kallus
First: 2025-12-29T19:04:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:40:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fitted Q-evaluation (FQE) is a foundational method for off-policy evaluation in reinforcement learning, but existing theory typically relies on Bellman completeness of the function class, a condition often violated in practice. This reliance is due to a fundamental norm mismatch: the Bellman operator is gamma-contractive in the L^2 norm induced by the target policy's stationary distribution, whereas standard FQE fits Bellman regressions under the behavior distribution. To resolve this mismatch, we reweight each Bellman regression step by an estimate of the stationary density ratio, inspired by emphatic weighting in temporal-difference learning. This makes the update behave as if it were performed under the target stationary distribution, restoring contraction without Bellman completeness while preserving the simplicity of regression-based evaluation. Illustrative experiments, including Baird's classical counterexample, show that stationary weighting can stabilize FQE under off-policy sampling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于平稳加权的无需贝尔曼完备性的拟合Q评估
拟合Q评估（FQE）是强化学习中离线策略评估的基础方法，但现有理论通常依赖于函数类的贝尔曼完备性，这一条件在实践中常被违反。这种依赖源于根本的范数不匹配：贝尔曼算子在目标策略平稳分布诱导的L^2范数下是γ-压缩的，而标准FQE在行为分布下进行贝尔曼回归拟合。为解决这一不匹配，我们受时序差分学习中强调加权的启发，通过估计平稳密度比对每个贝尔曼回归步骤进行重新加权。这使得更新过程仿佛在目标平稳分布下进行，从而在无需贝尔曼完备性的情况下恢复压缩性，同时保持基于回归的评估的简洁性。包括贝尔德经典反例在内的实验表明，平稳加权能在离线策略采样下稳定FQE。
Reasoning Over Space: Enabling Geographic Reasoning for LLM-Based Generative Next POI Recommendation
Authors: Dongyi Lv, Qiuyu Ding, Heng-Da Xu, Zhaoxu Sun, Zhi Wang, Feng Xiong, Mu Xu
First: 2026-01-08T03:46:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:25:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative recommendation with large language models (LLMs) reframes prediction as sequence generation, yet existing LLM-based recommenders remain limited in leveraging geographic signals that are crucial in mobility and local-services scenarios. Here, we present Reasoning Over Space (ROS), a framework that utilizes geography as a vital decision variable within the reasoning process. ROS introduces a Hierarchical Spatial Semantic ID (SID) that discretizes coarse-to-fine locality and POI semantics into compositional tokens, and endows LLM with a three-stage Mobility Chain-of-Thought (CoT) paradigm that models user personality, constructs an intent-aligned candidate space, and performs locality informed pruning. We further align the model with real world geography via spatial-guided Reinforcement Learning (RL). Experiments on three widely used location-based social network (LBSN) datasets show that ROS achieves over 10% relative gains in hit rate over strongest LLM-based baselines and improves cross-city transfer, despite using a smaller backbone model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：空间推理：为基于LLM的生成式下一兴趣点推荐赋予地理推理能力
基于大语言模型（LLM）的生成式推荐将预测重构为序列生成，然而现有LLM推荐器在利用对移动和本地服务场景至关重要的地理信号方面仍存在局限。本文提出空间推理（ROS）框架，将地理信息作为推理过程中的关键决策变量。ROS引入分层空间语义ID（SID），将粗粒度到细粒度的位置与POI语义离散化为组合式标记，并通过三阶段移动思维链（CoT）范式赋予LLM建模用户个性、构建意图对齐候选空间及执行位置感知剪枝的能力。我们进一步通过空间引导的强化学习（RL）使模型与现实地理对齐。在三个广泛使用的基于位置的社交网络（LBSN）数据集上的实验表明，尽管使用更小的骨干模型，ROS在命中率上相较于最强LLM基线实现了超过10%的相对提升，并改善了跨城市迁移性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of existing LLM-based generative next POI recommenders in leveraging geographic signals crucial for mobility tasks. The proposed Reasoning Over Space (ROS) framework introduces a Hierarchical Spatial Semantic ID to discretize locality and POI semantics into tokens, employs a three-stage Mobility Chain-of-Thought paradigm for reasoning over user personality, intent-aligned candidates, and locality pruning, and aligns the model with real-world geography via spatial-guided reinforcement learning. Experiments on three LBSN datasets demonstrate that ROS achieves over 10% relative gains in hit rate over the strongest LLM-based baselines and improves cross-city transfer, even with a smaller backbone model.
该论文针对现有基于大语言模型的生成式下一个兴趣点推荐系统在利用地理信号方面的不足，提出了推理空间框架。该框架通过分层空间语义标识将粗到细的区位和兴趣点语义离散化为词元，采用三阶段移动思维链范式对用户个性、意图对齐候选空间和区位剪枝进行推理，并通过空间引导的强化学习使模型与真实地理对齐。在三个基于位置的社交网络数据集上的实验表明，尽管使用了更小的骨干模型，该框架在命中率上相比最强的大语言模型基线实现了超过10%的相对提升，并改善了跨城市迁移性能。
Lyapunov-Certified Direct Switching Theory for Q-Learning
Authors: Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-04-21T15:22:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:22:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Q-learning is one of the most fundamental algorithms in reinforcement learning. We analyze constant-stepsize Q-learning through a direct stochastic switching system representation. The key observation is that the Bellman maximization error can be represented exactly by a stochastic policy. Therefore, the Q-learning error admits a switched linear conditional-mean recursion with martingale-difference noise. The intrinsic drift rate is the joint spectral radius (JSR) of the direct switching family, which can be strictly smaller than the standard row-sum rate. Using this representation, we derive a finite-time final-iterate bound via a JSR-induced Lyapunov function and then give a computable quadratic-certificate version.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于李雅普诺夫认证的直接切换理论的Q学习
Q学习是强化学习中最基础的算法之一。我们通过直接随机切换系统表示来分析恒定步长Q学习。关键观察在于，贝尔曼最大化误差可以精确地由随机策略表示。因此，Q学习误差允许一个带有鞅差噪声的切换线性条件均值递归。内在漂移率是直接切换族的联合谱半径（JSR），它可以严格小于标准行和率。利用这一表示，我们通过JSR诱导的李雅普诺夫函数推导出有限时间最终迭代界，然后给出一个可计算的二次认证版本。
Summary / 总结
This paper reanalyzes constant-stepsize Q-learning by modeling it as a direct stochastic switching system. The key motivation is that the Bellman maximization error can be exactly represented by a stochastic policy, allowing the Q-learning error to be expressed as a switched linear conditional-mean recursion with martingale-difference noise. The method introduces the joint spectral radius (JSR) of the switching family as the intrinsic drift rate, which can be strictly smaller than the standard row-sum rate. Main results include a finite-time final-iterate bound derived via a JSR-induced Lyapunov function and a computable quadratic-certificate version, providing tighter theoretical guarantees for Q-learning convergence.
本文通过直接随机切换系统表示重新分析了常数步长Q学习。其核心动机在于，贝尔曼最大化误差可被随机策略精确表示，从而将Q学习误差建模为带有鞅差噪声的切换线性条件均值递归。该方法引入切换族的联合谱半径作为内在漂移率，该指标可能严格小于标准行和率。主要实验结果包括：通过联合谱半径诱导的李雅普诺夫函数推导出有限时间最终迭代界，并给出可计算的二次证书版本，为Q学习的收敛性提供了更紧的理论保证。
Multi-modal Reasoning with LLMs for Visual Semantic Arithmetic
Authors: Chuou Xu, Liya Ji, Qifeng Chen
First: 2026-04-21T15:19:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:19:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) as post-training is crucial for enhancing the reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs) in coding and math. However, their capacity for visual semantic arithmetic, inferring relationships from images, remains underexplored. The classic text analogy "king"-"man"+"woman" = "queen" illustrates relational reasoning, yet replacing text with images of "king" and "man" significantly reduces performance because it requires commonsense knowledge and the extraction of concise concepts from irrelevant visual details. This capability is important for service and domestic robotics in unstructured environments, where robots must infer semantic relationships among objects, agents, and actions. In a kitchen, recognizing from images that "powder" and "cake" are related by "is made of" grounds symbolic relations in perception, enabling tool substitution, task generalization, and improved semantic reasoning. Prior work approaches semantic arithmetic by decoding image features after vector arithmetic, but suffers from modality gaps and lacks systematic evaluation. In this paper, we formulate two novel tasks, two-term subtraction and three-term operations, and construct the Image-Relation-Pair Dataset (IRPD) for benchmarking. We further propose Semantic Arithmetic Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (SAri-RFT), which post-trains large vision-language models (LVLMs) using a verifiable function and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Our method achieves state-of-the-art results on IRPD and the real-world Visual7W-Telling dataset. By equipping LVLMs with robust cross-modal relational reasoning, this work advances domestic robots' ability to ground symbolic reasoning in perception, enhancing decision-making, tool adaptability, and human-robot interaction in complex environments. Datasets and source code are provided in the supplementary material.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the underexplored problem of visual semantic arithmetic, where large language models struggle to infer relational analogies from images due to modality gaps and irrelevant visual details. The authors propose Semantic Arithmetic Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (SAri-RFT), which post-trains large vision-language models using a verifiable function and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) on two novel tasks: two-term subtraction and three-term operations. They construct the Image-Relation-Pair Dataset (IRPD) for benchmarking and achieve state-of-the-art results on both IRPD and the real-world Visual7W-Telling dataset, demonstrating improved cross-modal relational reasoning for applications like domestic robotics.
本文针对视觉语义算术这一未被充分探索的问题展开研究，指出大语言模型在从图像中推理关系类比时，因模态差距和无关视觉细节而表现不佳。作者提出了语义算术强化微调方法（SAri-RFT），通过可验证函数和分组相对策略优化（GRPO）对大型视觉语言模型进行后训练，并设计了二项减法和三项运算两种新任务。他们构建了图像关系对数据集（IRPD）作为基准，在IRPD和真实世界的Visual7W-Telling数据集上均取得了最优结果，展示了在家庭机器人等应用中增强跨模态关系推理的能力。
ASVSim (AirSim for Surface Vehicles): A High-Fidelity Simulation Framework for Autonomous Surface Vehicle Research
Authors: Bavo Lesy, Siemen Herremans, Robin Kerstens, Jan Steckel, Walter Daems, Siegfried Mercelis, Ali Anwar
First: 2025-06-27T12:39:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:14:46+00:00
Comments: 18 Pages, 13 Figures. Accepted at IEEE ACCESS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The transport industry has recently shown significant interest in unmanned surface vehicles (USVs), specifically for port and inland waterway transport. These systems can improve operational efficiency and safety, which is especially relevant in the European Union, where initiatives such as the Green Deal are driving a shift towards increased use of inland waterways. At the same time, a shortage of qualified personnel is accelerating the adoption of autonomous solutions. However, there is a notable lack of open-source, high-fidelity simulation frameworks and datasets for developing and evaluating such solutions. To address these challenges, we introduce AirSim for Surface Vehicles (ASVSim), an open-source simulation framework specifically designed for autonomous shipping research in inland and port environments. The framework combines simulated vessel dynamics with marine sensor simulation capabilities, including radar and camera systems and supports the generation of synthetic datasets for training computer vision models and reinforcement learning (RL) agents. Built upon Cosys-AirSim, ASVSim provides a comprehensive platform for developing autonomous navigation algorithms and generating synthetic datasets. The simulator supports research of both traditional control methods and deep learning-based approaches. Through experiments in waterway segmentation and autonomous navigation, we demonstrate the capabilities of the simulator in these research areas. ASVSim is provided as an open-source project under the MIT license, making autonomous navigation research accessible to a larger part of the ocean engineering community. See https://github.com/BavoLesy/ASVSim.

BAPO: Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization for Reliable Agentic Search
Authors: Shiyu Liu, Yongjing Yin, Jianhao Yan, Yunbo Tang, Qinggang Zhang, Bei Li, Xin Chen, Jingang Wang, Xunliang Cai, Jinsong Su
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-16T07:06:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T14:08:51+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Conference. Code is available at https://github.com/Liushiyu-0709/BAPO-Reliable-Search
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
RL-based agentic search enables LLMs to solve complex questions via dynamic planning and external search. While this approach significantly enhances accuracy with agent policies optimized via large-scale reinforcement learning, we identify a critical gap in reliability: these agents fail to recognize their reasoning boundaries and rarely admit ``I DON'T KNOW'' (IDK) even when evidence is insufficient or reasoning reaches its limit. The lack of reliability often leads to plausible but unreliable answers, introducing significant risks in many real-world scenarios. To this end, we propose Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization (BAPO), a novel RL framework designed to cultivate reliable boundary awareness without compromising accuracy. BAPO introduces two key components: (i) a group-based boundary-aware reward that encourages an IDK response only when the reasoning reaches its limit, and (ii) an adaptive reward modulator that strategically suspends this reward during early exploration, preventing the model from exploiting IDK as a shortcut. Extensive experiments on four benchmarks demonstrate that BAPO substantially enhances the overall reliability of agentic search.

标题：BAPO：面向可靠智能体搜索的边界感知策略优化
基于强化学习的智能体搜索使大语言模型能够通过动态规划和外部搜索解决复杂问题。虽然这种方法通过大规模强化学习优化的智能体策略显著提升了准确性，但我们发现了一个关键可靠性缺陷：这些智能体无法识别自身的推理边界，即使在证据不足或推理达到极限时也极少承认“我不知道”（IDK）。这种可靠性缺失常导致看似合理但不可靠的答案，在许多实际场景中引入重大风险。为此，我们提出边界感知策略优化（BAPO），一种新颖的强化学习框架，旨在在不牺牲准确性的前提下培养可靠的边界感知能力。BAPO引入两个关键组件：(i) 基于群体的边界感知奖励，仅在推理达到极限时鼓励IDK响应；(ii) 自适应奖励调节器，在早期探索阶段策略性地暂停该奖励，防止模型将IDK作为捷径利用。在四个基准上的大量实验表明，BAPO显著提升了智能体搜索的整体可靠性。

To address this, the authors propose Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization (BAPO), a novel RL framework that introduces a group-based boundary-aware reward to encourage IDK responses only when reasoning reaches its limit, along with an adaptive reward modulator that suspends this reward during early exploration to prevent shortcut exploitation. Extensive experiments on four benchmarks demonstrate that BAPO substantially enhances the overall reliability of agentic search without compromising accuracy.

EVPO: Explained Variance Policy Optimization for Adaptive Critic Utilization in LLM Post-Training
Authors: Chengjun Pan, Shichun Liu, Jiahang Lin, Dingwei Zhu, Jiazheng Zhang, Shihan Dou, Songyang Gao, Zhenhua Han, Binghai Wang, Rui Zheng, Xuanjing Huang, Tao Gui, Yansong Feng
First: 2026-04-21T14:07:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T14:07:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for LLM post-training faces a fundamental design choice: whether to use a learned critic as a baseline for policy optimization. Classical theory favors critic-based methods such as PPO for variance reduction, yet critic-free alternatives like GRPO have gained widespread adoption due to their simplicity and competitive performance. We show that in sparse-reward settings, a learned critic can inject estimation noise that exceeds the state signal it captures, increasing rather than reducing advantage variance. By casting baseline selection as a Kalman filtering problem, we unify PPO and GRPO as two extremes of the Kalman gain and prove that explained variance (EV), computable from a single training batch, identifies the exact boundary: positive EV indicates the critic reduces variance, while zero or negative EV signals that it inflates variance. Building on this insight, we propose Explained Variance Policy Optimization (EVPO), which monitors batch-level EV at each training step and adaptively switches between critic-based and batch-mean advantage estimation, provably achieving no greater variance than the better of the two at every step. Across four tasks spanning classical control, agentic interaction, and mathematical reasoning, EVPO consistently outperforms both PPO and GRPO regardless of which fixed baseline is stronger on a given task. Further analysis confirms that the adaptive gating tracks critic maturation over training and that the theoretically derived zero threshold is empirically optimal.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVPO：基于解释方差的自适应评论家策略优化用于大语言模型后训练
强化学习（RL）用于大语言模型后训练面临一个基本设计选择：是否使用学习到的评论家作为策略优化的基线。经典理论倾向于基于评论家的方法（如PPO）以减少方差，但无评论家的替代方案（如GRPO）因其简单性和竞争性表现而得到广泛采用。我们证明，在稀疏奖励设置中，学习到的评论家可能注入超过其捕获状态信号的估计噪声，从而增加而非减少优势方差。通过将基线选择视为卡尔曼滤波问题，我们将PPO和GRPO统一为卡尔曼增益的两个极端，并证明可从单个训练批次计算出的解释方差（EV）能识别精确边界：正EV表示评论家减少方差，而零或负EV则表明其增加方差。基于这一见解，我们提出解释方差策略优化（EVPO），它在每个训练步骤监控批次级EV，并在基于评论家和基于批次均值的优势估计之间自适应切换，理论上保证每一步的方差不超过两者中较优者。在涵盖经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理的四项任务中，无论给定任务上哪个固定基线更强，EVPO始终优于PPO和GRPO。进一步分析证实，自适应门控机制能追踪评论家随训练过程的成熟度，且理论推导的零阈值在经验上是最优的。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the design choice in reinforcement learning for LLM post-training between critic-based methods like PPO and critic-free methods like GRPO, motivated by the observation that in sparse-reward settings, a learned critic can increase advantage variance due to estimation noise. The authors propose Explained Variance Policy Optimization (EVPO), which frames baseline selection as a Kalman filtering problem and uses explained variance (EV) computed from a single batch to determine whether the critic reduces or inflates variance, adaptively switching between critic-based and batch-mean advantage estimation. Experiments across classical control, agentic interaction, and mathematical reasoning tasks show that EVPO consistently outperforms both PPO and GRPO, with the zero threshold for EV being empirically optimal.
该论文针对大语言模型后训练中强化学习的设计选择问题，即是否使用学习到的评论家作为基线，动机源于在稀疏奖励场景下，学习到的评论家可能因估计噪声而增加优势方差。作者提出解释方差策略优化（EVPO），将基线选择建模为卡尔曼滤波问题，利用单批次数据计算解释方差（EV）来判断评论家是降低还是增加方差，并自适应地在基于评论家和批次均值优势估计之间切换。在经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理等四个任务上的实验表明，EVPO始终优于PPO和GRPO，且EV的零阈值在经验上是最优的。
Global Optimization of Gaussian Process Acquisition Functions Using a Piecewise-Linear Kernel Approximation
Authors: Yilin Xie, Shiqiang Zhang, Joel A. Paulson, Calvin Tsay
First: 2024-10-22T10:56:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T13:45:21+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 4 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization relies on iteratively constructing and optimizing an acquisition function. The latter turns out to be a challenging, non-convex optimization problem itself. Despite the relative importance of this step, most algorithms employ sampling- or gradient-based methods, which do not provably converge to global optima. This work investigates mixed-integer programming (MIP) as a paradigm for global acquisition function optimization. Specifically, our Piecewise-linear Kernel Mixed Integer Quadratic Programming (PK-MIQP) formulation introduces a piecewise-linear approximation for Gaussian process kernels and admits a corresponding MIQP representation for acquisition functions. The proposed method is applicable to uncertainty-based acquisition functions for any stationary or dot-product kernel. We analyze the theoretical regret bounds of the proposed approximation, and empirically demonstrate the framework on synthetic functions, constrained benchmarks, and a hyperparameter tuning task.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用分段线性核近似的高斯过程采集函数全局优化
贝叶斯优化依赖于迭代构建和优化采集函数。后者本身是一个具有挑战性的非凸优化问题。尽管该步骤相对重要，但大多数算法采用基于采样或梯度的方法，这些方法无法保证收敛到全局最优。本研究探讨了混合整数规划作为全局采集函数优化的范式。具体而言，我们的分段线性核混合整数二次规划公式引入了高斯过程核的分段线性近似，并为采集函数提供了相应的混合整数二次规划表示。该方法适用于任何平稳或点积核的基于不确定性的采集函数。我们分析了所提近似的理论遗憾界，并在合成函数、约束基准测试和超参数调优任务上实证展示了该框架。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the challenge of globally optimizing acquisition functions in Bayesian optimization, which are typically non-convex and difficult to optimize with standard sampling or gradient methods. The authors propose a mixed-integer programming (MIP) approach, introducing a piecewise-linear kernel approximation that transforms the acquisition function optimization into a mixed-integer quadratic programming (MIQP) problem, applicable to any stationary or dot-product kernel. Theoretical regret bounds are analyzed, and empirical results on synthetic functions, constrained benchmarks, and hyperparameter tuning demonstrate the effectiveness of the method in achieving global optima.
该工作针对贝叶斯优化中采集函数全局优化困难的问题，提出了一种混合整数规划方法。通过引入高斯过程核的分段线性近似，将采集函数优化转化为混合整数二次规划问题，适用于任何平稳或点积核。理论分析了近似方法的遗憾界，并在合成函数、约束基准测试和超参数调优任务上验证了该方法在实现全局最优方面的有效性。
Learning Evolution via Optimization Knowledge Adaptation
Authors: Chao Wang, Lingling Li, Licheng Jiao, Jiaxuan Zhao, Fang Liu, Shuyuan Yang
First: 2025-01-04T05:35:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T12:31:45+00:00
Comments: This work has been accepted by IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The iterative search process of evolutionary algorithms (EAs) encapsulates optimization knowledge within historical populations and fitness evaluations. Effective utilization of this knowledge is crucial for facilitating knowledge transfer and online adaptation. However, current research typically addresses these goals in isolation and faces distinct limitations: evolutionary sequential transfer optimization often suffers from incomplete utilization of prior knowledge, while adaptive strategies, utilizing real-time knowledge, are limited to tailoring specific evolutionary operators. To simultaneously achieve these two capabilities, we introduce the Optimization Knowledge Adaptation Evolutionary Model (OKAEM), a unified learnable evolutionary framework capable of adaptively updating parameters based on available optimization knowledge. By parameterizing evolutionary operators via attention mechanisms, OKAEM enables learnable update rules that facilitate the utilization of optimization knowledge via two phases: pre-training to integrate extensive prior knowledge for efficient transfer, and adaptive optimization to dynamically update parameters based on real-time knowledge. Experimental results confirm that OKAEM significantly outperforms state-of-the-art sequential transfer methods across 12 transfer scenarios via pre-training, and surpasses advanced learnable EAs solely through its self-tuning mechanism in prior-free settings. Beyond demonstrating practical utility in prompt tuning for vision-language models, ablation studies validate the necessity of the learnable components, while visualization analyses reveal the model's capacity to autonomously discover interpretable evolutionary principles. The code can be accessed at https://gitee.com/Anonymity_Paper/code-of-okaem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过优化知识适应学习进化
进化算法（EAs）的迭代搜索过程将优化知识封装在历史种群和适应度评估中。有效利用这些知识对于促进知识迁移和在线适应至关重要。然而，当前研究通常孤立地处理这些目标，并面临不同的局限性：进化序列迁移优化往往因未能充分利用先验知识而受损，而利用实时知识的自适应策略则局限于定制特定的进化算子。为同时实现这两种能力，我们引入了优化知识适应进化模型（OKAEM），这是一个统一的可学习进化框架，能够基于可用优化知识自适应更新参数。通过注意力机制参数化进化算子，OKAEM实现了可学习的更新规则，通过两个阶段促进优化知识的利用：预训练以整合大量先验知识实现高效迁移，以及自适应优化以基于实时知识动态更新参数。实验结果表明，OKAEM通过预训练在12个迁移场景中显著优于最先进的序列迁移方法，并在无先验设置中仅通过自调优机制超越了先进的可学习进化算法。除了在视觉-语言模型的提示调优中展示实际效用外，消融研究验证了可学习组件的必要性，而可视化分析揭示了模型自主发现可解释进化原理的能力。代码可访问https://gitee.com/Anonymity_Paper/code-of-okaem。
