HP-Edit: A Human-Preference Post-Training Framework for Image Editing
Authors: Fan Li, Chonghuinan Wang, Lina Lei, Yuping Qiu, Jiaqi Xu, Jiaxiu Jiang, Xinran Qin, Zhikai Chen, Fenglong Song, Zhixin Wang, Renjing Pei, Wangmeng Zuo
First: 2026-04-21T12:29:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T12:29:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Common image editing tasks typically adopt powerful generative diffusion models as the leading paradigm for real-world content editing. Meanwhile, although reinforcement learning (RL) methods such as Diffusion-DPO and Flow-GRPO have further improved generation quality, efficiently applying Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) to diffusion-based editing remains largely unexplored, due to a lack of scalable human-preference datasets and frameworks tailored to diverse editing needs. To fill this gap, we propose HP-Edit, a post-training framework for Human Preference-aligned Editing, and introduce RealPref-50K, a real-world dataset across eight common tasks and balancing common object editing. Specifically, HP-Edit leverages a small amount of human-preference scoring data and a pretrained visual large language model (VLM) to develop HP-Scorer--an automatic, human preference-aligned evaluator. We then use HP-Scorer both to efficiently build a scalable preference dataset and to serve as the reward function for post-training the editing model. We also introduce RealPref-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating real-world editing performance. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly enhances models such as Qwen-Image-Edit-2509, aligning their outputs more closely with human preference.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HP-Edit：面向图像编辑的人类偏好后训练框架
常见的图像编辑任务通常采用强大的生成扩散模型作为现实内容编辑的主流范式。同时，尽管Diffusion-DPO和Flow-GRPO等强化学习方法进一步提升了生成质量，但由于缺乏可扩展的人类偏好数据集和针对多样化编辑需求的框架，将基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）高效应用于基于扩散的编辑仍鲜有探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出HP-Edit——一个面向人类偏好对齐的后训练框架，并引入RealPref-50K——一个涵盖八种常见任务并平衡常见物体编辑的真实世界数据集。具体而言，HP-Edit利用少量人类偏好评分数据和预训练的视觉大语言模型（VLM）开发HP-Scorer——一个自动的、与人类偏好对齐的评估器。随后，我们使用HP-Scorer高效构建可扩展的偏好数据集，并作为后训练编辑模型的奖励函数。我们还引入RealPref-Bench——一个评估真实世界编辑性能的基准。大量实验表明，我们的方法显著增强了Qwen-Image-Edit-2509等模型，使其输出更贴近人类偏好。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces HP-Edit, a post-training framework designed to align diffusion-based image editing models with human preferences, motivated by the lack of scalable human-preference datasets and efficient RLHF methods for editing tasks. The method leverages a small amount of human-preference scoring data and a pretrained visual large language model to develop HP-Scorer, an automatic evaluator that both constructs a scalable preference dataset and serves as a reward function for post-training. Extensive experiments show that HP-Edit significantly enhances models like Qwen-Image-Edit-2509, aligning their outputs more closely with human preference on the introduced RealPref-Bench benchmark.
该论文提出了HP-Edit，一个用于将基于扩散模型的图像编辑模型与人类偏好对齐的后训练框架，其动机是缺乏可扩展的人类偏好数据集和针对编辑任务的高效RLHF方法。该方法利用少量人类偏好评分数据和预训练视觉大语言模型开发了HP-Scorer，这是一个自动评估器，既能构建可扩展的偏好数据集，又能作为后训练的奖励函数。大量实验表明，HP-Edit显著提升了Qwen-Image-Edit-2509等模型，使其输出在引入的RealPref-Bench基准上更符合人类偏好。
LPO: Towards Accurate GUI Agent Interaction via Location Preference Optimization
Authors: Jiaqi Tang, Yu Xia, Yi-Feng Wu, Yuwei Hu, Yuhui Chen, Qing-Guo Chen, Xiaogang Xu, Xiangyu Wu, Hao Lu, Yanqing Ma, Shiyin Lu, Qifeng Chen
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-06-11T03:43:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T11:50:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The advent of autonomous agents is transforming interactions with Graphical User Interfaces (GUIs) by employing natural language as a powerful intermediary. Despite the predominance of Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) methods in current GUI agents for achieving spatial localization, these methods face substantial challenges due to their limited capacity to accurately perceive positional data. Existing strategies, such as reinforcement learning, often fail to assess positional accuracy effectively, thereby restricting their utility. In response, we introduce Location Preference Optimization (LPO), a novel approach that leverages locational data to optimize interaction preferences. LPO uses information entropy to predict interaction positions by focusing on zones rich in information. Besides, it further introduces a dynamic location reward function based on physical distance, reflecting the varying importance of interaction positions. Supported by Group Relative Preference Optimization (GRPO), LPO facilitates an extensive exploration of GUI environments and significantly enhances interaction precision. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate LPO's superior performance, achieving SOTA results across both offline benchmarks and real-world online evaluations. Our code will be made publicly available soon, at https://github.com/jqtangust/LPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LPO：通过位置偏好优化实现精准GUI代理交互
自主代理的出现正通过将自然语言作为强大中介，改变与图形用户界面（GUI）的交互方式。尽管当前GUI代理中广泛采用监督微调（SFT）方法来实现空间定位，但这些方法因准确感知位置数据的能力有限而面临重大挑战。现有策略（如强化学习）往往无法有效评估位置准确性，从而限制了其实用性。为此，我们提出位置偏好优化（LPO），一种利用位置数据优化交互偏好的新方法。LPO通过关注信息丰富的区域，使用信息熵预测交互位置。此外，它进一步引入基于物理距离的动态位置奖励函数，反映交互位置的不同重要性。在组相对偏好优化（GRPO）的支持下，LPO促进了对GUI环境的广泛探索，并显著提升了交互精度。全面实验表明，LPO性能优越，在离线基准测试和真实世界在线评估中均达到最先进（SOTA）结果。我们的代码将很快在https://github.com/jqtangust/LPO公开。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Location Preference Optimization (LPO), a novel method to improve the accuracy of GUI agent interactions by addressing the limitations of Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) in perceiving positional data. LPO leverages information entropy to predict interaction positions in information-rich zones and incorporates a dynamic location reward function based on physical distance to reflect varying positional importance, all optimized via Group Relative Preference Optimization (GRPO). Experiments demonstrate that LPO achieves state-of-the-art results on both offline benchmarks and real-world online evaluations, significantly enhancing interaction precision.
该论文提出了位置偏好优化（LPO）方法，旨在解决监督微调（SFT）在GUI代理中感知位置数据能力有限的问题。LPO利用信息熵预测信息丰富区域的交互位置，并引入基于物理距离的动态位置奖励函数以反映不同位置的重要性，通过组相对偏好优化（GRPO）进行优化。实验表明，LPO在离线基准测试和真实在线评估中均取得了最先进的结果，显著提升了交互精度。
LASER: Learning Active Sensing for Continuum Field Reconstruction
Authors: Huayu Deng, Jinghui Zhong, Xiangming Zhu, Yunbo Wang, Xiaokang Yang
First: 2026-04-21T11:36:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T11:36:09+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
High-fidelity measurements of continuum physical fields are essential for scientific discovery and engineering design but remain challenging under sparse and constrained sensing. Conventional reconstruction methods typically rely on fixed sensor layouts, which cannot adapt to evolving physical states. We propose LASER, a unified, closed-loop framework that formulates active sensing as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP). At its core, LASER employs a continuum field latent world model that captures the underlying physical dynamics and provides intrinsic reward feedback. This enables a reinforcement learning policy to simulate ''what-if'' sensing scenarios within a latent imagination space. By conditioning sensor movements on predicted latent states, LASER navigates toward potentially high-information regions beyond current observations. Our experiments demonstrate that LASER consistently outperforms static and offline-optimized strategies, achieving high-fidelity reconstruction under sparsity across diverse continuum fields.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LASER：面向连续场重建的学习型主动感知
连续物理场的高保真测量对科学发现和工程设计至关重要，但在稀疏且受限的感知条件下仍具挑战。传统重建方法通常依赖固定传感器布局，无法适应演变的物理状态。我们提出LASER，一个统一的闭环框架，将主动感知建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）。其核心采用连续场潜在世界模型，捕捉底层物理动力学并提供内在奖励反馈，使强化学习策略能在潜在想象空间中模拟“假设”感知场景。通过将传感器移动与预测的潜在状态关联，LASER能导航至当前观测之外的高信息潜力区域。实验表明，LASER在多种连续场中始终优于静态和离线优化策略，在稀疏条件下实现高保真重建。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LASER, a framework for high-fidelity reconstruction of continuum physical fields under sparse sensing constraints, motivated by the limitations of fixed sensor layouts that cannot adapt to evolving states. The method formulates active sensing as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process, using a continuum field latent world model to capture dynamics and provide intrinsic rewards, enabling a reinforcement learning policy to simulate sensing scenarios in latent space and guide sensor movements toward high-information regions. Experimental results show that LASER consistently outperforms static and offline-optimized strategies, achieving superior reconstruction fidelity across diverse continuum fields under sparsity.
该论文提出LASER框架，旨在解决稀疏传感下连续物理场高保真重建的挑战，其动机源于固定传感器布局无法适应动态物理状态的局限性。方法将主动传感建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，利用连续场潜在世界模型捕捉物理动态并提供内在奖励，使强化学习策略能在潜在想象空间中模拟传感场景，并引导传感器向高信息区域移动。实验结果表明，LASER在多种连续场稀疏重建任务中一致优于静态和离线优化策略，实现了更高的重建保真度。
Resource-aware Mixed-precision Quantization for Enhancing Deployability of Transformers for Time-series Forecasting on Embedded FPGAs
Authors: Tianheng Ling, Chao Qian, Gregor Schiele
First: 2024-10-04T10:12:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T10:27:28+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 8 figures, 6 tables, accepted by the 21st EAI International Conference on Mobile and Ubiquitous Systems: Computing, Networking and Services (MobiQuitous2024)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study addresses the deployment challenges of integer-only quantized Transformers on resource-constrained embedded FPGAs (Xilinx Spartan-7 XC7S15). We enhanced the flexibility of our VHDL template by introducing a selectable resource type for storing intermediate results across model layers, thereby breaking the deployment bottleneck by utilizing BRAM efficiently. Moreover, we developed a resource-aware mixed-precision quantization approach that enables researchers to explore hardware-level quantization strategies without requiring extensive expertise in Neural Architecture Search. This method provides accurate resource utilization estimates with a precision discrepancy as low as 3%, compared to actual deployment metrics. Compared to previous work, our approach has successfully facilitated the deployment of model configurations utilizing mixed-precision quantization, thus overcoming the limitations inherent in five previously non-deployable configurations with uniform quantization bitwidths. Consequently, this research enhances the applicability of Transformers in embedded systems, facilitating a broader range of Transformer-powered applications on edge devices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向资源感知的混合精度量化以增强Transformer在嵌入式FPGA上时间序列预测的可部署性
本研究解决了整数量化Transformer在资源受限的嵌入式FPGA（Xilinx Spartan-7 XC7S15）上的部署挑战。我们通过引入可选择的资源类型来存储模型层间的中间结果，从而增强了VHDL模板的灵活性，并利用BRAM高效打破了部署瓶颈。此外，我们开发了一种资源感知的混合精度量化方法，使研究人员无需具备神经架构搜索的广泛专业知识即可探索硬件级量化策略。该方法提供的资源利用率估计与实际部署指标相比，精度偏差低至3%。与先前工作相比，我们的方法成功实现了采用混合精度量化的模型配置部署，从而克服了五种先前因均匀量化位宽而无法部署的配置的固有限制。因此，本研究增强了Transformer在嵌入式系统中的适用性，促进了边缘设备上更广泛的Transformer驱动应用。

Remote Rowhammer Attack using Adversarial Observations on Federated Learning Clients
Authors: Jinsheng Yuan, Yuhang Hao, Weisi Guo, Yun Wu, Chongyan Gu
First: 2025-05-09T17:27:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T09:43:38+00:00
Comments: Under review for IEEE Transactions on Dependable and Secure Computing
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated Learning (FL) has the potential for simultaneous global learning amongst a large number of parallel agents, enabling emerging AI such as LLMs to be trained across demographically diverse data. Central to this being efficient is the ability for FL to perform sparse gradient updates and remote direct memory access at the central server. Most of the research in FL security focuses on protecting data privacy at the edge client or in the communication channels between the client and server. Client-facing attacks on the server are less well investigated as the assumption is that a large collective of clients offer resilience. Here, we show that by attacking certain clients that lead to a high frequency repetitive memory update in the server, we can remote initiate a rowhammer attack on the server memory. For the first time, we do not need backdoor access to the server, and a reinforcement learning (RL) attacker can learn how to maximize server repetitive memory updates by manipulating the client's sensor observation. The consequence of the remote rowhammer attack is that we are able to achieve bit flips, which can corrupt the server memory. We demonstrate the feasibility of our attack using a large-scale FL automatic speech recognition (ASR) systems with sparse updates, our adversarial attacking agent can achieve around 70% repeated update rate (RUR) in the targeted server model, effectively inducing bit flips on server DRAM. The security implications are that can cause disruptions to learning or may inadvertently cause elevated privilege. This paves the way for further research on practical mitigation strategies in FL and hardware design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用联邦学习客户端对抗性观测的远程Rowhammer攻击
联邦学习（FL）具有在大量并行代理之间实现同步全局学习的潜力，使得新兴人工智能（如大型语言模型）能够在多样化人口统计数据上进行训练。其高效性的核心在于FL能够在中央服务器执行稀疏梯度更新和远程直接内存访问。目前FL安全研究主要关注边缘客户端或客户端与服务器通信通道中的数据隐私保护。由于假设大量客户端集群具有弹性，针对服务器的客户端攻击研究较少。本文证明，通过攻击某些导致服务器高频重复内存更新的客户端，可以远程发起对服务器内存的Rowhammer攻击。首次无需后门访问服务器，强化学习（RL）攻击者可通过操纵客户端传感器观测值，学习如何最大化服务器重复内存更新。远程Rowhammer攻击的后果是实现比特翻转，从而破坏服务器内存。我们通过大规模稀疏更新FL自动语音识别（ASR）系统验证了攻击可行性，对抗攻击代理在目标服务器模型上可实现约70%的重复更新率（RUR），有效诱导服务器DRAM比特翻转。安全影响包括可能导致学习中断或意外权限提升，为FL及硬件设计的实用缓解策略研究开辟了新方向。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces a novel remote Rowhammer attack on federated learning (FL) servers, motivated by the overlooked security risk of client-side attacks on server memory. The method uses a reinforcement learning (RL) agent to manipulate client sensor observations, causing high-frequency repetitive memory updates in the server via sparse gradient updates and remote direct memory access, thereby triggering Rowhammer bit flips without backdoor access. Experimental results on a large-scale FL automatic speech recognition (ASR) system show that the adversarial agent achieves approximately 70% repeated update rate (RUR) on the targeted server model, successfully inducing bit flips in server DRAM and demonstrating potential for learning disruption or privilege escalation.
该论文提出了一种针对联邦学习服务器的新型远程Rowhammer攻击，动机在于客户端对服务器内存的攻击风险常被忽视。方法利用强化学习代理操纵客户端传感器观测，通过稀疏梯度更新和远程直接内存访问在服务器中引发高频重复内存更新，从而无需后门访问即可触发Rowhammer比特翻转。在大型联邦学习自动语音识别系统上的实验结果表明，对抗代理在目标服务器模型上实现了约70%的重复更新率，成功诱导服务器DRAM中的比特翻转，展示了干扰学习或提升权限的潜在威胁。
TROJail: Trajectory-Level Optimization for Multi-Turn Large Language Model Jailbreaks with Process Rewards
Authors: Xiqiao Xiong, Ouxiang Li, Zhuo Liu, Moxin Li, Wentao Shi, Fengbin Zhu, Qifan Wang, Fuli Feng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-08T17:42:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T08:41:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models have seen widespread adoption, yet they remain vulnerable to multi-turn jailbreak attacks, threatening their safe deployment. This has led to the task of training automated multi-turn attackers to probe model safety vulnerabilities. However, existing approaches typically rely on turn-level optimization, which is insufficient for learning long-term attack strategies. To bridge this gap, we formulate this task as a multi-turn reinforcement learning problem, directly optimizing the harmfulness of the final-turn response as the outcome reward. To address the sparse supervision of the outcome reward, we introduce TROJail, which employs two process rewards to evaluate the utility of intermediate prompts and integrate them into advantage estimation. These rewards (1) penalize overly harmful prompts that trigger the model's refusal mechanism, and (2) encourage steering the semantic relevance of responses toward the targeted harmful content. Experimental results show improved attack success rates across multiple models and benchmarks, highlighting the effectiveness of our approach. The code is available at https://github.com/xxiqiao/TROJail. Warning: This paper contains examples of harmful content.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TROJail：基于过程奖励的多轮大语言模型越狱轨迹级优化
大语言模型已得到广泛应用，但仍易受多轮越狱攻击威胁，影响其安全部署。这促使需要训练自动化多轮攻击者以探测模型安全漏洞。然而，现有方法通常依赖轮次级优化，难以学习长期攻击策略。为弥补这一不足，我们将该任务形式化为多轮强化学习问题，直接优化最终轮回复的危害性作为结果奖励。针对结果奖励监督稀疏的问题，我们提出TROJail，采用两种过程奖励评估中间提示的效用并将其整合到优势估计中。这些奖励（1）惩罚触发模型拒绝机制的过度有害提示，（2）鼓励将回复的语义相关性导向目标有害内容。实验结果表明，该方法在多个模型和基准测试中提升了攻击成功率，凸显了其有效性。代码见https://github.com/xxiqiao/TROJail。警告：本文包含有害内容示例。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of large language models to multi-turn jailbreak attacks, where existing turn-level optimization methods fail to learn long-term attack strategies. To overcome this, the authors formulate the task as a multi-turn reinforcement learning problem, directly optimizing the harmfulness of the final-turn response as the outcome reward. They introduce TROJail, which uses two process rewards to evaluate intermediate prompts: one penalizes overly harmful prompts that trigger refusal, and the other encourages steering semantic relevance toward targeted harmful content. Experimental results demonstrate improved attack success rates across multiple models and benchmarks, validating the effectiveness of the approach.
该论文针对大语言模型在多轮对话中易受越狱攻击的漏洞，指出现有基于单轮优化的方法难以学习长期攻击策略。为此，作者将任务建模为多轮强化学习问题，直接以最终轮回复的危害性作为结果奖励进行优化。他们提出TROJail方法，采用两种过程奖励评估中间提示：一种惩罚过度有害而触发拒绝机制的提示，另一种鼓励将回复语义导向目标有害内容。实验结果表明，该方法在多个模型和基准测试上提升了攻击成功率，验证了其有效性。
Reasoning-Aware AIGC Detection via Alignment and Reinforcement
Authors: Zhao Wang, Max Xiong, Jianxun Lian, Zhicheng Dou
First: 2026-04-21T07:29:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T07:29:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement and widespread adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) have elevated the need for reliable AI-generated content (AIGC) detection, which remains challenging as models evolve. We introduce AIGC-text-bank, a comprehensive multi-domain dataset with diverse LLM sources and authorship scenarios, and propose REVEAL, a detection framework that generates interpretable reasoning chains before classification. Our approach uses a two-stage training strategy: supervised fine-tuning to establish reasoning capabilities, followed by reinforcement learning to improve accuracy, improve logical consistency, and reduce hallucinations. Extensive experiments show that REVEAL achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmarks, offering a robust and transparent solution for AIGC detection. The project is open-source at https://aka.ms/reveal
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对齐与强化学习的推理感知型AIGC检测
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展和广泛应用，对可靠的人工智能生成内容（AIGC）检测的需求日益迫切，而这一任务随着模型的演进仍充满挑战。我们提出了AIGC-text-bank，一个涵盖多领域、多LLM来源及作者身份场景的综合数据集，并设计了REVEAL检测框架，该框架在分类前生成可解释的推理链。我们的方法采用两阶段训练策略：首先通过监督微调建立推理能力，随后利用强化学习提升准确性、增强逻辑一致性并减少幻觉。大量实验表明，REVEAL在多个基准测试中达到了最先进的性能，为AIGC检测提供了稳健且透明的解决方案。该项目已开源，地址为https://aka.ms/reveal
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of detecting AI-generated content (AIGC) as large language models evolve, motivated by the need for reliable detection. The authors propose REVEAL, a framework that generates interpretable reasoning chains before classification, using a two-stage training strategy: supervised fine-tuning to establish reasoning capabilities, followed by reinforcement learning to improve accuracy, logical consistency, and reduce hallucinations. They also introduce AIGC-text-bank, a comprehensive multi-domain dataset. Extensive experiments show that REVEAL achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmarks, offering a robust and transparent solution for AIGC detection.
该论文针对大语言模型快速发展带来的AI生成内容检测挑战，提出了一种名为REVEAL的检测框架。该方法在分类前先生成可解释的推理链，采用两阶段训练策略：先通过监督微调建立推理能力，再通过强化学习提升准确性、逻辑一致性并减少幻觉。同时，论文引入了包含多领域数据源的AIGC-text-bank数据集。大量实验表明，REVEAL在多个基准测试中达到了最先进的性能，为AI生成内容检测提供了稳健且透明的解决方案。
Quantum spatial best-arm identification via quantum walks
Authors: Tomoki Yamagami, Etsuo Segawa, Takatomo Mihana, André Röhm, Atsushi Uchida, Ryoichi Horisaki
First: 2025-09-07T01:53:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T07:28:56+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum reinforcement learning has emerged as a framework combining quantum computation with sequential decision-making, and applications to the multi-armed bandit (MAB) problem have been reported. The graph bandit problem extends the MAB setting by introducing spatial constraints, where the accessibility of arms is restricted by graph connectivity, yet quantum approaches to this setting remain limited. In this paper, we formulate best-arm identification in graph bandits and propose a quantum algorithmic framework, termed Quantum Spatial Best-Arm Identification (QSBAI), which is applicable to general graph structures. This framework uses quantum walks to encode superpositions over graph-constrained actions, thereby extending amplitude amplification and generalizing the quantum BAI algorithm via Szegedy's walk framework. We focus our theoretical analysis on complete and bipartite graphs, deriving the maximal success probability of identifying the best arm and the time step at which it is achieved. Our results clarify how quantum-walk-based search can be adapted to structurally constrained decision problems and provide a foundation for quantum best-arm identification in graph-structured environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于量子游走的量子空间最优臂识别
量子强化学习已成为将量子计算与序列决策相结合的一个框架，并已有应用于多臂老虎机问题的报道。图老虎机问题通过引入空间约束扩展了多臂老虎机设置，其中臂的可访问性受限于图连通性，但针对该设置的量子方法仍然有限。本文提出了图老虎机中的最优臂识别问题，并构建了一个量子算法框架，称为量子空间最优臂识别，该框架适用于一般图结构。该框架利用量子游走对图约束动作的叠加态进行编码，从而扩展了振幅放大，并通过Szegedy游走框架推广了量子最优臂识别算法。我们将理论分析聚焦于完全图和二分图，推导出识别最优臂的最大成功概率及其达到的时间步。我们的结果阐明了如何将基于量子游走的搜索适应于结构约束的决策问题，并为图结构环境中的量子最优臂识别提供了基础。

RL-ABC: Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control
Authors: Anwar Ibrahim, Fedor Ratnikov, Maxim Kaledin, Alexey Petrenko, Denis Derkach
First: 2026-04-21T06:52:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:52:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Particle accelerator beamline optimization is a high-dimensional control problem traditionally requiring significant expert intervention. We present RLABC (Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control), an open-source Python framework that automatically transforms standard Elegant beamline configurations into reinforcement learning environments. RLABC integrates with the widely-used Elegant beam dynamics simulation code via SDDS-based interfaces, enabling researchers to apply modern RL algorithms to beamline optimization with minimal RL-specific development. The main contribution is a general methodology for formulating beamline tuning as a Markov decision process: RLABC automatically preprocesses lattice files to insert diagnostic watch points before each tunable element, constructs a 57-dimensional state representation from beam statistics, covariance information, and aperture constraints, and provides a configurable reward function for transmission optimization. The framework supports multiple RL algorithms through Stable-Baselines3 compatibility and implements stage learning strategies for improved training efficiency. Validation on a test beamline derived from the VEPP-5 injection complex (37 control parameters across 11 quadrupoles and 4 dipoles) demonstrates that the framework successfully enables RL-based optimization, with a Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient agent achieving 70.3\% particle transmission -- performance matching established methods such as differential evolution. The framework's stage learning capability allows decomposition of complex optimization problems into manageable subproblems, improving training efficiency. The complete framework, including configuration files and example notebooks, is available as open-source software to facilitate adoption and further research.

标题：RL-ABC：用于加速器束线控制的强化学习
粒子加速器束线优化是一个高维控制问题，传统上需要大量专家干预。我们提出RLABC（用于加速器束线控制的强化学习），这是一个开源Python框架，可自动将标准Elegant束线配置转换为强化学习环境。RLABC通过基于SDDS的接口与广泛使用的Elegant束流动力学模拟代码集成，使研究人员能够以最少的RL特定开发工作，将现代RL算法应用于束线优化。 主要贡献在于将束线调谐表述为马尔可夫决策过程的一般方法论：RLABC自动预处理晶格文件，在每个可调元件前插入诊断监视点，从束流统计量、协方差信息和孔径约束构建57维状态表示，并提供用于传输优化的可配置奖励函数。该框架通过Stable-Baselines3兼容性支持多种RL算法，并实现了阶段学习策略以提高训练效率。 在源自VEPP-5注入复合体的测试束线（11个四极磁铁和4个二极磁铁共37个控制参数）上的验证表明，该框架成功实现了基于RL的优化，深度确定性策略梯度智能体达到了70.3%的粒子传输率——性能与微分进化等成熟方法相当。框架的阶段学习能力允许将复杂优化问题分解为可管理的子问题，从而提高训练效率。完整框架（包括配置文件和示例笔记本）以开源软件形式提供，以促进采用和进一步研究。

ARM: Advantage Reward Modeling for Long-Horizon Manipulation
Authors: Yiming Mao, Zixi Yu, Weixin Mao, Yinhao Li, Qirui Hu, Zihan Lan, Minzhao Zhu, Hua Chen
First: 2026-04-03T13:45:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:50:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-horizon robotic manipulation remains challenging for reinforcement learning (RL) because sparse rewards provide limited guidance for credit assignment. Practical policy improvement thus relies on richer intermediate supervision, such as dense progress rewards, which are costly to obtain and ill-suited to non-monotonic behaviors such as backtracking and recovery. To address this, we propose Advantage Reward Modeling (ARM), a framework that shifts from hard-to-quantify absolute progress to estimating relative advantage. We introduce a cost-effective tri-state labeling strategy -- Progressive, Regressive, and Stagnant -- that reduces human cognitive overhead while ensuring high cross-annotator consistency. By training on these intuitive signals, ARM enables automated progress annotation for both complete demonstrations and fragmented DAgger-style data. Integrating ARM into an offline RL pipeline allows for adaptive action-reward reweighting, effectively filtering suboptimal samples. Our approach achieves a 99.4% success rate on a challenging long-horizon towel-folding task, demonstrating improved stability and data efficiency over current VLA baselines with near-zero human intervention during policy training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARM：面向长时程操控的优势奖励建模

Bootstrapping Code Translation with Weighted Multilanguage Exploration
Authors: Yuhan Wu, Huan Zhang, Wei Cheng, Chen Shen, Jingyue Yang, Wei Hu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-07T01:56:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:44:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted in the 64th Annual Meeting of the Association for Computational Linguistics (ACL 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Code translation across multiple programming languages is essential yet challenging due to two vital obstacles: scarcity of parallel data paired with executable test oracles, and optimization imbalance when handling diverse language pairs. We propose BootTrans, a bootstrapping method that resolves both obstacles. Its key idea is to leverage the functional invariance and cross-lingual portability of test suites, adapting abundant pivot-language unit tests to serve as universal verification oracles for multilingual reinforcement learning (RL) training. Our method introduces a dual-pool architecture with seed and exploration pools to progressively expand training data via execution-guided experience collection. Furthermore, we design a language-aware weighting mechanism that dynamically prioritizes harder translation directions based on relative performance across sibling languages, mitigating optimization imbalance. Extensive experiments on the HumanEval-X and TransCoder-Test benchmarks demonstrate substantial improvements over baseline LLMs across all translation directions, with ablation studies validating the effectiveness of both bootstrapping and weighting components.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于加权多语言探索的代码翻译自举方法

BootTrans旨在解决多语言代码翻译中的两个关键障碍：缺乏带有可执行测试预言机的平行数据，以及处理不同语言对时的优化不平衡问题。该方法利用测试套件的功能不变性和跨语言可移植性，将枢轴语言的单元测试作为通用验证预言机用于强化学习训练。它采用种子池和探索池的双池架构逐步扩展训练数据，并设计了一种语言感知加权机制，根据兄弟语言间的相对表现动态优先处理更难的翻译方向。在HumanEval-X和TransCoder-Test基准上的大量实验表明，该方法在所有翻译方向上均显著优于基线大语言模型，消融研究也验证了引导和加权组件的有效性。
The Rise of Verbal Tics in Large Language Models: A Systematic Analysis Across Frontier Models
Authors: Shuai Wu, Xue Li, Yanna Feng, Yufang Li, Zhijun Wang, Ran Wang
First: 2026-04-21T06:43:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:43:01+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 17 figures, 8 tables. Technical report
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Large Language Models (LLMs) continue to evolve through alignment techniques such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Constitutional AI, a growing and increasingly conspicuous phenomenon has emerged: the proliferation of verbal tics -- repetitive, formulaic linguistic patterns that pervade model outputs. These range from sycophantic openers ("That's a great question!", "Awesome!") to pseudo-empathetic affirmations ("I completely understand your concern", "I'm right here to catch you") and overused vocabulary ("delve", "tapestry", "nuanced"). In this paper, we present a systematic analysis of the verbal tic phenomenon across eight state-of-the-art LLMs: GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.7, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Grok 4.2, Doubao-Seed-2.0-pro, Kimi K2.5, DeepSeek V3.2, and MiMo-V2-Pro. Utilizing a custom evaluation framework for standardized API-based evaluation, we assess 10,000 prompts across 10 task categories in both English and Chinese, yielding 160,000 model responses. We introduce the Verbal Tic Index (VTI), a composite metric quantifying tic prevalence, and analyze its correlation with sycophancy, lexical diversity, and human-perceived naturalness. Our findings reveal significant inter-model variation: Gemini 3.1 Pro exhibits the highest VTI (0.590), while DeepSeek V3.2 achieves the lowest (0.295). We further demonstrate that verbal tics accumulate over multi-turn conversations, are amplified in subjective tasks, and show distinct cross-lingual patterns. Human evaluation (N = 120) confirms a strong inverse relationship between sycophancy and perceived naturalness (r = -0.87, p < 0.001). These results underscore the "alignment tax" of current training paradigms and highlight the urgent need for more authentic human-AI interaction frameworks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型中口头禅现象的兴起：跨前沿模型的系统分析
随着大型语言模型通过人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）和宪法AI等对齐技术持续演进，一个日益显著的现象逐渐浮现：口头禅的泛滥——即模型输出中重复性、公式化的语言模式。这些模式包括谄媚式开场白（“问得好！”“太棒了！”）、伪共情式肯定（“我完全理解您的顾虑”“我随时为您提供支持”）以及过度使用的词汇（“深入探讨”“交织”“微妙”）。本文对八种最先进的大型语言模型（GPT-5.4、Claude Opus 4.7、Gemini 3.1 Pro、Grok 4.2、豆包-Seed-2.0-pro、Kimi K2.5、DeepSeek V3.2和MiMo-V2-Pro）中的口头禅现象进行了系统分析。我们采用自定义评估框架进行标准化API评估，在英语和中文两种语言中，针对10个任务类别评估了10,000个提示，生成了160,000个模型响应。我们引入了口头禅指数（VTI），这是一个量化口头禅流行度的复合指标，并分析了其与谄媚性、词汇多样性和人类感知自然度的相关性。研究结果揭示了显著的模型间差异：Gemini 3.1 Pro的VTI最高（0.590），而DeepSeek V3.2最低（0.295）。我们进一步证明，口头禅在多轮对话中累积，在主观任务中被放大，并表现出明显的跨语言模式。人类评估（N=120）证实了谄媚性与感知自然度之间存在强烈的负相关关系（r=-0.87，p<0.001）。这些结果凸显了当前训练范式的“对齐代价”，并强调了构建更真实人机交互框架的迫切需求。

本文系统分析了大型语言模型中的口头禅现象，其动机源于观察到RLHF和Constitutional AI等对齐技术导致模型输出中出现重复、公式化的语言模式。作者提出了口头禅指数（VTI）作为综合指标，并在英语和中文的10,000个提示上评估了八个前沿模型，生成了160,000个响应。主要结果显示，Gemini 3.1 Pro的VTI最高（0.590），而DeepSeek V3.2最低（0.295），人类评估表明谄媚与感知自然度之间存在强负相关（r = -0.87），凸显了当前训练范式的对齐代价。
Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation for Noisy Subset Selection
Authors: Yiheng Xu, Danxuan Liu, Bin Zhang, Weiyong Yang, Chao Qian
First: 2025-01-12T14:04:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:35:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Subset selection is a fundamental problem in combinatorial optimization, which has a wide range of applications such as influence maximization and sparse regression. The goal is to select a subset of limited size from a ground set in order to maximize a given objective function. However, the evaluation of the objective function in real-world scenarios is often noisy. Previous algorithms, including the greedy algorithm and multi-objective evolutionary algorithms POSS and PONSS, either struggle in noisy environments or consume excessive computational resources. In this paper, we focus on the noisy subset selection problem with a cardinality constraint, where the evaluation of a subset is noisy. We propose a novel approach based on Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation for noisy subset selection (PORE), which maximizes a robust evaluation function and minimizes the subset size simultaneously. PORE can efficiently identify well-structured solutions and handle computational resources, addressing the limitations observed in PONSS. Our experiments, conducted on real-world datasets for influence maximization and sparse regression, demonstrate that PORE significantly outperforms previous methods, including the classical greedy algorithm, POSS, and PONSS. Further validation through ablation studies confirms the effectiveness of our robust evaluation function.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于鲁棒评估的帕累托优化用于含噪子集选择
子集选择是组合优化中的基本问题，广泛应用于影响力最大化和稀疏回归等领域。其目标是从候选集中选取有限大小的子集以最大化给定目标函数。然而，现实场景中目标函数的评估往往存在噪声。现有算法（包括贪心算法和多目标进化算法POSS与PONSS）在噪声环境下表现不佳或消耗过多计算资源。本文聚焦于带基数约束的含噪子集选择问题，其中子集评估存在噪声。我们提出了一种基于鲁棒评估的帕累托优化方法（PORE），该方法同时最大化鲁棒评估函数并最小化子集规模。PORE能高效识别结构良好的解并管理计算资源，克服了PONSS的局限性。在影响力最大化和稀疏回归的真实数据集上的实验表明，PORE显著优于包括经典贪心算法、POSS和PONSS在内的现有方法。消融研究进一步验证了鲁棒评估函数的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the noisy subset selection problem under a cardinality constraint, where objective function evaluations are often noisy in real-world applications, and previous methods like greedy algorithms and multi-objective evolutionary algorithms POSS and PONSS either struggle with noise or consume excessive computational resources. The authors propose a novel approach called Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation (PORE), which simultaneously maximizes a robust evaluation function and minimizes subset size to efficiently identify well-structured solutions while managing computational costs. Experiments on real-world datasets for influence maximization and sparse regression show that PORE significantly outperforms classical greedy, POSS, and PONSS methods, with ablation studies further confirming the effectiveness of the robust evaluation function.
本文针对带基数约束的噪声子集选择问题，其中实际场景中目标函数的评估常受噪声干扰，而现有方法如贪心算法及多目标进化算法POSS和PONSS，要么在噪声环境下表现不佳，要么消耗过多计算资源。作者提出了一种基于鲁棒评估的帕累托优化方法（PORE），通过同时最大化鲁棒评估函数和最小化子集大小，高效识别结构良好的解并控制计算开销。在影响力最大化和稀疏回归的真实数据集上的实验表明，PORE显著优于经典贪心算法、POSS和PONSS，消融研究进一步验证了鲁棒评估函数的有效性。
Temp-R1: A Unified Autonomous Agent for Complex Temporal KGQA via Reverse Curriculum Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhaoyan Gong, Zhiqiang Liu, Songze Li, Xiaoke Guo, Yuanxiang Liu, Xinle Deng, Zhizhen Liu, Lei Liang, Huajun Chen, Wen Zhang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-26T09:23:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:22:33+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Temporal Knowledge Graph Question Answering (TKGQA) is inherently challenging, as it requires sophisticated reasoning over dynamic facts with multi-hop dependencies and complex temporal constraints. Existing methods rely on fixed workflows and expensive closed-source APIs, limiting flexibility and scalability. We propose Temp-R1, the first autonomous end-to-end agent for TKGQA trained through reinforcement learning. To address cognitive overload in single-action reasoning, we expand the action space with specialized internal actions alongside external action. To prevent shortcut learning on simple questions, we introduce reverse curriculum learning that trains on difficult questions first, forcing the development of sophisticated reasoning before transferring to easier cases. Our 8B-parameter Temp-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance on MultiTQ and TimelineKGQA, improving 19.8% over strong baselines on complex questions. Our work establishes a new paradigm for autonomous temporal reasoning agents. The code is available at https://github.com/zjukg/Temp-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Temp-R1：基于逆向课程强化学习的统一自主智能体，用于复杂时序知识图谱问答
时序知识图谱问答（TKGQA）本质上具有挑战性，因为它需要对具有多跳依赖关系和复杂时序约束的动态事实进行复杂推理。现有方法依赖固定工作流程和昂贵的闭源API，限制了灵活性和可扩展性。我们提出Temp-R1，这是首个通过强化学习训练的自主端到端TKGQA智能体。为解决单动作推理中的认知过载问题，我们扩展了动作空间，在外部动作之外增加了专门的内部动作。为防止在简单问题上出现捷径学习，我们引入了逆向课程学习，即先训练困难问题，迫使智能体发展复杂推理能力，再迁移到简单案例。我们的8B参数Temp-R1在MultiTQ和TimelineKGQA上达到了最先进性能，在复杂问题上相比强基线提升了19.8%。我们的工作为自主时序推理智能体建立了新范式。代码已开源：https://github.com/zjukg/Temp-R1。
Summary / 总结
Temporal Knowledge Graph Question Answering (TKGQA) requires reasoning over dynamic facts with multi-hop dependencies and temporal constraints, but existing methods rely on fixed workflows and expensive APIs. To address this, the authors propose Temp-R1, the first autonomous end-to-end agent trained via reinforcement learning, which expands the action space with specialized internal actions and uses reverse curriculum learning to train on difficult questions first, preventing shortcut learning. The 8B-parameter model achieves state-of-the-art performance on MultiTQ and TimelineKGQA, improving 19.8% over strong baselines on complex questions.

Reinforcement Learning Enabled Adaptive Multi-Task Control for Bipedal Soccer Robots
Authors: Yulai Zhang, Yinrong Zhang, Ting Wu, Linqi Ye
First: 2026-04-21T05:27:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T05:27:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing bipedal football robots in dynamiccombat environments presents challenges related to motionstability and deep coupling of multiple tasks, as well ascontrol switching issues between different states such as up-right walking and fall recovery. To address these problems,this paper proposes a modular reinforcement learning (RL)framework for achieving adaptive multi-task control. Firstly,this framework combines an open-loop feedforward oscilla-tor with a reinforcement learning-based feedback residualstrategy, effectively separating the generation of basic gaitsfrom complex football actions. Secondly, a posture-driven statemachine is introduced, clearly switching between the ballseeking and kicking network (BSKN) and the fall recoverynetwork (FRN), fundamentally preventing state interference.The FRN is efficiently trained through a progressive forceattenuation curriculum learning strategy. The architecture wasverified in Unity simulations of bipedal robots, demonstratingexcellent spatial adaptability-reliably finding and kicking theball even in restricted corner scenarios-and rapid autonomousfall recovery (with an average recovery time of 0.715 seconds).This ensures seamless and stable operation in complex multi-task environments.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of motion stability, multi-task coupling, and control switching in bipedal soccer robots by proposing a modular reinforcement learning framework. The method combines an open-loop feedforward oscillator with a reinforcement learning-based feedback residual to separate basic gait generation from complex football actions, and introduces a posture-driven state machine to switch between ball seeking/kicking and fall recovery networks, with the latter trained via progressive force attenuation curriculum learning. Experiments in Unity simulations show that the robot achieves excellent spatial adaptability in corner scenarios and rapid fall recovery with an average time of 0.715 seconds, ensuring stable multi-task operation.
本文针对双足足球机器人在动态对抗环境中的运动稳定性、多任务深度耦合以及不同状态间的控制切换问题，提出了一种模块化强化学习框架。该方法将开环前馈振荡器与基于强化学习的反馈残差策略相结合，有效分离了基本步态生成与复杂足球动作，并引入姿态驱动状态机，在寻球踢球网络和跌倒恢复网络之间进行清晰切换，其中跌倒恢复网络通过渐进力衰减课程学习高效训练。在Unity仿真中的实验表明，该机器人即使在受限角落场景中也能可靠地找到并踢球，且平均跌倒恢复时间为0.715秒，确保了复杂多任务环境下的无缝稳定运行。
Multi-Gait Learning for Humanoid Robots Using Reinforcement Learning with Selective Adversarial Motion Prior
Authors: Yuanye Wu, Keyi Wang, Linqi Ye, Boyang Xing
First: 2026-04-21T05:26:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T05:26:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning diverse locomotion skills for humanoid robots in a unified reinforcement learning framework remains challenging due to the conflicting requirements of stability and dynamic expressiveness across different gaits. We present a multi-gait learning approach that enables a humanoid robot to master five distinct gaits -- walking, goose-stepping, running, stair climbing, and jumping -- using a consistent policy structure, action space, and reward formulation. The key contribution is a selective Adversarial Motion Prior (AMP) strategy: AMP is applied to periodic, stability-critical gaits (walking, goose-stepping, stair climbing) where it accelerates convergence and suppresses erratic behavior, while being deliberately omitted for highly dynamic gaits (running, jumping) where its regularization would over-constrain the motion. Policies are trained via PPO with domain randomization in simulation and deployed on a physical 12-DOF humanoid robot through zero-shot sim-to-real transfer. Quantitative comparisons demonstrate that selective AMP outperforms a uniform AMP policy across all five gaits, achieving faster convergence, lower tracking error, and higher success rates on stability-focused gaits without sacrificing the agility required for dynamic ones.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of learning multiple diverse locomotion gaits for humanoid robots within a single reinforcement learning framework, where stability and dynamic expressiveness often conflict. The authors propose a multi-gait learning method using a selective Adversarial Motion Prior (AMP) strategy, applying AMP to periodic, stability-critical gaits like walking and stair climbing to accelerate convergence and reduce erratic behavior, while omitting it for highly dynamic gaits like running and jumping to avoid over-constraining motion. Policies are trained with PPO and domain randomization in simulation, then deployed zero-shot on a physical 12-DOF humanoid robot. Experimental results show that selective AMP outperforms a uniform AMP policy across all five gaits, achieving faster convergence, lower tracking error, and higher success rates on stability-focused gaits without sacrificing agility for dynamic ones.
该论文针对在统一强化学习框架中让人形机器人学习多种不同步态所面临的稳定性与动态表现力冲突的挑战。作者提出了一种多步态学习方法，采用选择性对抗性运动先验（AMP）策略，对周期性、稳定性关键的步态（如行走和爬楼梯）应用AMP以加速收敛并抑制异常行为，而对高度动态的步态（如跑步和跳跃）则有意省略AMP以避免过度约束运动。策略通过PPO和域随机化在仿真中训练，并零样本迁移到物理12自由度人形机器人上。实验结果表明，选择性AMP在所有五种步态上均优于统一AMP策略，在稳定性步态上实现了更快的收敛、更低的跟踪误差和更高的成功率，同时未牺牲动态步态所需的敏捷性。
OLLM: Options-based Large Language Models
Authors: Shashank Sharma, Janina Hoffmann, Vinay Namboodiri
First: 2026-04-21T04:59:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:59:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Options LLM (OLLM), a simple, general method that replaces the single next-token prediction of standard LLMs with a \textit{set of learned options} for the next token, indexed by a discrete latent variable. Instead of relying on temperature or sampling heuristics to induce diversity, OLLM models variation explicitly: a small latent space parametrizes multiple plausible next-token options which can be selected or searched by a downstream policy. Architecturally, OLLM is a lightweight "plug-in" that inserts two layers: an encoder and a decoder, before the output head, allowing almost any pretrained LLM to be converted with minimal additional parameters. We apply OLLM to a 1.7B-parameter backbone (only $1.56\%$ of parameters trainable) trained on OpenMathReasoning and evaluated on OmniMath. The SOTA LoRA-adapted baselines peak at $51\%$ final answer correctness, while OLLM's option set allows up to $\sim 70\%$ under optimal latent selection. We then train a compact policy in the latent space that emits latents to control generation. Operating in a low-dimensional option space makes reward optimization far more sample-efficient and substantially reduces common misalignments (e.g., language switching or degenerate reasoning), as the policy is constrained to options learned during SFT. Crucially, this alignment arises from model structure rather than additional KL or handcrafted alignment losses. Our results demonstrate that optionized next-token modeling enhances controllability, robustness, and efficiency in math reasoning, and highlight latent-space policy learning as a promising direction for reinforcement learning in LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OLLM：基于选项的大型语言模型
我们提出选项LLM（OLLM），这是一种简单通用的方法，用一组针对下一个词元的“学习选项”（由离散潜变量索引）替代标准LLM的单一词元预测。OLLM不依赖温度或采样启发式来诱导多样性，而是显式建模变异性：一个小的潜空间参数化多个合理的下一个词元选项，可由下游策略选择或搜索。架构上，OLLM是一个轻量级“插件”，在输出头前插入编码器和解码器两层，使几乎任何预训练LLM都能以最少额外参数转换。我们将OLLM应用于1.7B参数骨干模型（仅1.56%参数可训练），在OpenMathReasoning上训练并在OmniMath上评估。SOTA LoRA适配基线在最终答案正确率上最高达51%，而OLLM的选项集在最优潜变量选择下可达约70%。随后我们在潜空间中训练一个紧凑策略，通过发射潜变量控制生成。在低维选项空间中操作使奖励优化样本效率大幅提升，并显著减少常见失调（如语言切换或退化推理），因为策略被约束在SFT期间学习的选项内。关键在于，这种对齐源于模型结构而非额外的KL或手工设计的对齐损失。我们的结果表明，选项化下一个词元建模增强了数学推理中的可控性、鲁棒性和效率，并凸显了潜空间策略学习作为LLM强化学习的一个有前景方向。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces OLLM, a method that replaces standard next-token prediction in large language models with a set of learned options indexed by a discrete latent variable, enabling explicit modeling of variation. Architecturally, OLLM inserts a lightweight encoder-decoder plug-in before the output head, converting pretrained models with minimal parameter overhead. Applied to a 1.7B-parameter backbone trained on OpenMathReasoning and evaluated on OmniMath, OLLM achieves up to approximately 70% final answer correctness under optimal latent selection, surpassing the 51% peak of SOTA LoRA-adapted baselines. A compact policy trained in the low-dimensional latent space further enhances sample efficiency and reduces misalignments like language switching, demonstrating that optionized modeling improves controllability and robustness in math reasoning without additional alignment losses.
该论文提出OLLM方法，用离散潜变量索引的一组学习选项替代标准大语言模型的单一下一个词预测，从而显式建模生成多样性。架构上，OLLM在输出头前插入轻量级编码器-解码器插件，能以极少额外参数转换预训练模型。在基于OpenMathReasoning训练、OmniMath评估的1.7B参数骨干模型上，OLLM在最优潜变量选择下达到约70%的最终答案正确率，超过最强LoRA基线51%的峰值。在低维选项空间中训练的紧凑策略进一步提升了样本效率，并减少了语言切换等失调问题，表明选项化建模无需额外对齐损失即可增强数学推理的可控性和鲁棒性。
FaithLens: Detecting and Explaining Faithfulness Hallucination
Authors: Shuzheng Si, Qingyi Wang, Haozhe Zhao, Yuzhuo Bai, Guanqiao Chen, Kangyang Luo, Gang Chen, Fanchao Qi, Minjia Zhang, Baobao Chang, Maosong Sun
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-23T09:20:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:28:11+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 (Findings)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recognizing whether outputs from large language models (LLMs) contain faithfulness hallucination is crucial for real-world applications, e.g., retrieval-augmented generation and summarization. In this paper, we introduce FaithLens, a cost-efficient and effective faithfulness hallucination detection model that can jointly provide binary predictions and corresponding explanations to improve trustworthiness. To achieve this, we first synthesize training data with explanations via advanced LLMs and apply a well-defined data filtering strategy to ensure label correctness, explanation quality, and data diversity. Subsequently, we fine-tune the model on these well-curated training data as a cold start and further optimize it with rule-based reinforcement learning, using rewards for both prediction correctness and explanation quality. Results on 12 diverse tasks show that the 8B-parameter FaithLens outperforms advanced models such as GPT-5.2 and o3. Also, FaithLens can produce high-quality explanations, delivering a distinctive balance of trustworthiness, efficiency, and effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FaithLens：检测与解释忠实性幻觉
识别大型语言模型（LLM）的输出是否包含忠实性幻觉，对于检索增强生成和摘要等实际应用至关重要。本文提出FaithLens，一种经济高效且有效的忠实性幻觉检测模型，能够同时提供二元预测和相应解释，以提升可信度。为此，我们首先通过先进LLM合成带有解释的训练数据，并应用定义明确的数据过滤策略，确保标签正确性、解释质量和数据多样性。随后，以这些精心整理的数据作为冷启动对模型进行微调，并利用基于规则的强化学习进一步优化，奖励预测正确性和解释质量。在12个不同任务上的结果表明，8B参数的FaithLens优于GPT-5.2和o3等先进模型。此外，FaithLens能生成高质量解释，在可信度、效率和有效性之间实现独特平衡。
Summary / 总结
FaithLens addresses the challenge of detecting faithfulness hallucinations in large language model outputs, which is critical for applications like retrieval-augmented generation and summarization. The method involves synthesizing training data with explanations using advanced LLMs, applying a filtering strategy to ensure quality, and fine-tuning an 8B-parameter model with rule-based reinforcement learning that rewards both prediction accuracy and explanation quality. Experimental results across 12 diverse tasks demonstrate that FaithLens outperforms advanced models such as GPT-5.2 and o3, while also producing high-quality explanations that balance trustworthiness, efficiency, and effectiveness.
FaithLens旨在解决大型语言模型输出中忠实性幻觉的检测问题，这对检索增强生成和摘要等实际应用至关重要。该方法通过使用先进大模型合成带有解释的训练数据，并应用精心定义的数据过滤策略确保标签正确性、解释质量和数据多样性，随后对8B参数模型进行冷启动微调，并利用基于规则的强化学习优化，奖励预测正确性和解释质量。在12个不同任务上的实验结果显示，FaithLens超越了GPT-5.2和o3等先进模型，同时能生成高质量解释，在可信度、效率和有效性之间实现了独特平衡。
TRN-R1-Zero: Text-rich Network Reasoning via LLMs with Reinforcement Learning Only
Authors: Yilun Liu, Ruihong Qiu, Zi Huang
First: 2026-04-21T04:24:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:24:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Zero-shot reasoning on text-rich networks (TRNs) remains a challenging frontier, as models must integrate textual semantics with relational structure without task-specific supervision. While graph neural networks rely on fixed label spaces and supervised objectives, recent large language model (LLM)-based approaches often overlook graph context or depend on distillation from larger models, limiting generalisation. We propose TRN-R1-Zero, a post-training framework for TRN reasoning trained solely via reinforcement learning. TRN-R1-Zero directly optimises base LLMs using a Neighbour-aware Group Relative Policy Optimisation objective that dynamically adjusts rewards based on a novel margin gain metric for the informativeness of neighbouring signals, effectively guiding the model toward relational reasoning. Unlike prior methods, TRN-R1-Zero requires no supervised fine-tuning or chain-of-thought data generated from large reasoning models. Extensive experiments across citation, hyperlink, social and co-purchase TRN benchmarks demonstrate the superiority and robustness of TRN-R1-Zero. Moreover, relying strictly on node-level training, TRN-R1-Zero achieves zero-shot inference on edge- and graph-level tasks, extending beyond cross-domain transfer. The codebase is publicly available at https://github.com/superallen13/TRN-R1-Zero.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of zero-shot reasoning on text-rich networks, where models must combine textual semantics with relational structure without task-specific supervision. The authors propose TRN-R1-Zero, a post-training framework that uses reinforcement learning only, specifically a Neighbour-aware Group Relative Policy Optimisation objective with a margin gain metric to dynamically adjust rewards based on the informativeness of neighboring signals, eliminating the need for supervised fine-tuning or chain-of-thought data. Experiments on citation, hyperlink, social, and co-purchase network benchmarks show that TRN-R1-Zero achieves superior and robust performance, and with only node-level training, it generalizes to zero-shot edge- and graph-level tasks across domains.
该论文针对文本丰富网络中的零样本推理挑战，要求模型在无任务特定监督下整合文本语义与关系结构。作者提出TRN-R1-Zero，一种仅使用强化学习的后训练框架，通过邻居感知组相对策略优化目标，利用新颖的边际增益指标动态调整基于邻居信号信息量的奖励，无需监督微调或思维链数据。在引文、超链接、社交和共同购买网络基准上的实验表明，TRN-R1-Zero实现了优越且鲁棒的性能，且仅通过节点级训练即可零样本泛化到边和图级任务，跨领域迁移效果显著。
MRS: Multi-Resolution Skills for HRL Agents
Authors: Shashank Sharma, Janina Hoffmann, Vinay Namboodiri
First: 2025-05-27T16:38:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:20:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) decomposes the policy into a manager and a worker, enabling long-horizon planning but introducing a performance gap on tasks requiring agility. We identify a root cause: in subgoal-based HRL, the manager's goal representation is typically learned without constraints on reachability or temporal distance from the current state, preventing precise local subgoal selection. We further show that the optimal subgoal distance is both task- and state-dependent: nearby subgoals enable precise control but amplify prediction noise, while distant subgoals produce smoother motion at the cost of geometric precision. We propose Multi-Resolution Skills (MRS), which learns multiple goal-prediction modules each specialized to a fixed temporal horizon, with a jointly trained meta-controller that selects among them based on the current state. MRS consistently outperforms fixed-resolution baselines and significantly reduces the performance gap between HRL and non-HRL state-of-the-art on DeepMind Control Suite, Gym-Robotics, and long-horizon AntMaze tasks. [Project page: https://sites.google.com/view/multi-res-skills/home]
中文标题/摘要
标题：MRS：面向分层强化学习智能体的多分辨率技能
分层强化学习（HRL）将策略分解为管理者和工作者，能够实现长时域规划，但在需要敏捷性的任务上引入了性能差距。我们识别出一个根本原因：在基于子目标的HRL中，管理者的目标表示通常是在没有对可达性或与当前状态的时间距离施加约束的情况下学习的，这阻碍了精确的局部子目标选择。我们进一步证明，最优子目标距离既依赖于任务也依赖于状态：邻近的子目标能实现精确控制但会放大预测噪声，而较远的子目标以几何精度为代价产生更平滑的运动。我们提出多分辨率技能（MRS），该方法学习多个专门针对固定时间范围的目标预测模块，并联合训练一个基于当前状态进行选择的元控制器。MRS在DeepMind Control Suite、Gym-Robotics和长时域AntMaze任务上持续优于固定分辨率基线，并显著缩小了HRL与非HRL最先进方法之间的性能差距。[项目页面：https://sites.google.com/view/multi-res-skills/home]
Summary / 总结
Hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) decomposes policy into manager and worker for long-horizon planning but suffers a performance gap on agile tasks due to unconstrained goal representations that lack reachability or temporal distance awareness, leading to suboptimal subgoal selection. The authors propose Multi-Resolution Skills (MRS), which learns multiple goal-prediction modules each specialized to a fixed temporal horizon, with a meta-controller that selects among them based on the current state. Experiments on DeepMind Control Suite, Gym-Robotics, and long-horizon AntMaze tasks show MRS consistently outperforms fixed-resolution baselines and significantly reduces the performance gap between HRL and non-HRL state-of-the-art methods.
分层强化学习将策略分解为管理者和工作者以实现长程规划，但在敏捷任务上存在性能差距，其根本原因是基于子目标的分层强化学习中，管理者学习的目标表示缺乏可达性或时间距离约束，导致子目标选择不精确。作者提出多分辨率技能方法，学习多个分别针对固定时间跨度的目标预测模块，并由一个元控制器根据当前状态选择使用哪个模块。在DeepMind控制套件、Gym-Robotics和长程AntMaze任务上的实验表明，该方法持续优于固定分辨率基线，并显著缩小了分层强化学习与非分层强化学习最先进方法之间的性能差距。
Reinforcement Learning Improves LLM Accuracy and Reasoning in Disease Classification from Radiology Reports
Authors: Yishu Wei, Yi Lin, Adam Flanders, George Shih, Yifan Peng
First: 2026-04-21T04:09:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:09:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate disease classification from radiology reports is essential for many applications. While supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of lightweight LLMs improves accuracy, it can degrade reasoning. We propose a two-stage approach: SFT on disease labels followed by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to refine predictions by optimizing accuracy and format without reasoning supervision. Across three radiologist-annotated datasets, SFT outperformed baselines and GRPO further improved classification and enhanced reasoning recall and comprehensiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习提升放射学报告中疾病分类的LLM准确性与推理能力
从放射学报告中准确分类疾病对许多应用至关重要。虽然对轻量级LLM进行监督微调（SFT）能提升准确性，但可能削弱推理能力。我们提出两阶段方法：先对疾病标签进行SFT，再通过群体相对策略优化（GRPO）优化准确性和格式来细化预测，无需推理监督。在三个放射科医生标注的数据集上，SFT优于基线，GRPO进一步改进了分类并增强了推理的召回率和全面性。

The paper addresses the challenge of improving disease classification from radiology reports using lightweight LLMs, where supervised fine-tuning (SFT) boosts accuracy but harms reasoning. The authors propose a two-stage method: first SFT on disease labels, then Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to refine predictions by optimizing accuracy and format without reasoning supervision. Experiments on three radiologist-annotated datasets show that SFT outperforms baselines, and GRPO further enhances classification accuracy while improving reasoning recall and comprehensiveness.
该论文针对从放射学报告中利用轻量级大语言模型进行疾病分类的挑战，指出监督微调（SFT）虽能提升准确性但会损害推理能力。作者提出两阶段方法：先对疾病标签进行SFT，再通过组相对策略优化（GRPO）在无推理监督下优化准确性和格式来细化预测。在三个放射科医生标注的数据集上，SFT优于基线，而GRPO进一步提升了分类性能，并增强了推理的召回率和全面性。
QTMRL: An Agent for Quantitative Trading Decision-Making Based on Multi-Indicator Guided Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingfeng Pan, Jiahao Chen
First: 2025-08-28T06:37:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:38:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In the highly volatile and uncertain global financial markets, traditional quantitative trading models relying on statistical modeling or empirical rules often fail to adapt to dynamic market changes and black swan events due to rigid assumptions and limited generalization. To address these issues, this paper proposes QTMRL (Quantitative Trading Multi-Indicator Reinforcement Learning), an intelligent trading agent combining multi-dimensional technical indicators with reinforcement learning (RL) for adaptive and stable portfolio management. We first construct a comprehensive multi-indicator dataset using 23 years of S&P 500 daily OHLCV data (2000-2022) for 16 representative stocks across 5 sectors, enriching raw data with trend, volatility, and momentum indicators to capture holistic market dynamics. Then we design a lightweight RL framework based on the Advantage Actor-Critic (A2C) algorithm, including data processing, A2C algorithm, and trading agent modules to support policy learning and actionable trading decisions. Extensive experiments compare QTMRL with 9 baselines (e.g., ARIMA, LSTM, moving average strategies) across diverse market regimes, verifying its superiority in profitability, risk adjustment, and downside risk control. The code of QTMRL is publicly available at https://github.com/ChenJiahaoJNU/QTMRL.git
Summary / 总结
To overcome the limitations of traditional quantitative trading models that struggle with dynamic market changes and black swan events due to rigid assumptions, this paper introduces QTMRL, an intelligent agent that integrates multi-dimensional technical indicators with reinforcement learning for adaptive portfolio management. The method constructs a comprehensive dataset from 23 years of S&P 500 data, enriching it with trend, volatility, and momentum indicators, and employs an Advantage Actor-Critic (A2C) algorithm within a lightweight RL framework to support policy learning and trading decisions. Extensive experiments across diverse market regimes demonstrate that QTMRL outperforms nine baselines, including ARIMA, LSTM, and moving average strategies, in terms of profitability, risk adjustment, and downside risk control.
为了解决传统量化交易模型因刚性假设和泛化能力有限而难以适应动态市场变化和黑天鹅事件的问题，本文提出了QTMRL，一种将多维技术指标与强化学习相结合的智能交易代理，用于自适应和稳定的投资组合管理。该方法利用23年的标普500日线数据构建了包含趋势、波动性和动量指标的综合数据集，并基于优势演员-评论家（A2C）算法设计了一个轻量级强化学习框架，以支持策略学习和可执行的交易决策。在多种市场环境下的广泛实验表明，QTMRL在盈利能力、风险调整和下行风险控制方面均优于包括ARIMA、LSTM和移动平均策略在内的九种基线模型。
Intentional Updates for Streaming Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Arsalan Sharifnassab, Mohamed Elsayed, Kris De Asis, A. Rupam Mahmood, Richard S. Sutton
First: 2026-04-21T03:33:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:33:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In gradient-based learning, a step size chosen in parameter units does not produce a predictable per-step change in function output. This often leads to instability in the streaming setting (i.e., batch size=1), where stochasticity is not averaged out and update magnitudes can momentarily become arbitrarily big or small. Instead, we propose intentional updates: first specify the intended outcome of an update and then solve for the step size that approximately achieves it. This strategy has precedent in online supervised linear regression via Normalized Least Mean Squares algorithm, which selects a step size to yield a specified change in the function output proportional to the current error. We extend this principle to streaming deep reinforcement learning by defining appropriate intended outcomes: Intentional TD aims for a fixed fractional reduction of the TD error, and Intentional Policy Gradient aims for a bounded per-step change in the policy, limiting local KL divergence. We propose practical algorithms combining eligibility traces and diagonal scaling. Empirically, these methods yield state-of-the-art streaming performance, frequently performing on par with batch and replay-buffer approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流式强化学习中的意图性更新
在基于梯度的学习中，以参数单位选择的步长无法产生函数输出中可预测的每步变化。这通常会导致流式设置（即批量大小=1）中的不稳定性，其中随机性不会被平均化，更新幅度可能瞬间变得任意大或小。相反，我们提出意图性更新：首先指定更新的预期结果，然后求解近似实现该结果的步长。该策略在在线监督线性回归中通过归一化最小均方算法已有先例，该算法选择步长以产生与当前误差成比例的指定函数输出变化。我们将这一原理扩展到流式深度强化学习，通过定义适当的预期结果：意图性TD旨在实现TD误差的固定分数减少，而意图性策略梯度旨在实现策略的每步有界变化，限制局部KL散度。我们提出了结合资格迹和对角缩放的实际算法。实验表明，这些方法实现了最先进的流式性能，通常与批处理和回放缓冲区方法表现相当。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses instability in streaming reinforcement learning (batch size=1) caused by unpredictable per-step changes in function output from gradient-based updates. The authors propose intentional updates, which first specify the intended outcome (e.g., a fixed fractional reduction of TD error for Intentional TD, or a bounded per-step change in policy for Intentional Policy Gradient) and then solve for the step size that approximately achieves it, extending the principle from Normalized Least Mean Squares. Empirically, their methods with eligibility traces and diagonal scaling achieve state-of-the-art streaming performance, often matching batch and replay-buffer approaches.
该论文针对流式强化学习（批大小为1）中因梯度更新导致函数输出每步变化不可预测而引发的不稳定性问题。作者提出意图性更新方法，先指定预期更新目标（如意图性TD旨在固定比例降低TD误差，意图性策略梯度限制每步策略变化的KL散度），再求解近似实现该目标的步长，这一思路源于归一化最小均方算法。实验表明，结合资格迹和对角缩放的方法在流式场景中达到最优性能，常与批处理和回放缓冲区方法相当。
Benchmarking Swarm Optimization Algorithms for Parameter Initialization in the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm
Authors: Shashank Sanjay Bhat, Peiyong Wang, Udaya Parampalli
First: 2025-06-07T13:14:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:23:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) is a prominent variational algorithm for solving combinatorial optimization problems such as the Max Cut problem. A key challenge in QAOA is the efficient identification of variational parameters (γ, \{beta}) that yield high-quality solutions. In this work, we investigate swarm optimization methods as robust strategies for exploring the QAOA parameter space. We evaluate Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), Fully Informed Particle Swarm Optimization (FIPSO), Quantum Particle Swarm Optimization (QPSO), and an Adam-assisted FIPSO variant on weighted MaxCut instances across multiple system sizes, circuit depths, and noise regimes, including shot noise. Our results show that these methods achieve lower approximation gaps and more stable convergence compared to standard optimizers such as Adam, COBYLA, and SPSA. In particular, we observe that swarm methods maintain superior performance under noisy and shot limited conditions. These findings suggest that population based search is effective for navigating the complex QAOA landscape and is a promising approach for parameter optimization in near-term quantum algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：群智能优化算法在量子近似优化算法参数初始化中的基准测试
量子近似优化算法（QAOA）是一种用于解决组合优化问题（如最大割问题）的重要变分算法。QAOA的关键挑战在于高效识别能产生高质量解的变分参数（γ, β）。本研究探索了群智能优化方法作为鲁棒策略来搜索QAOA参数空间。我们在加权最大割实例上，针对多种系统规模、电路深度和噪声环境（包括散粒噪声），评估了粒子群优化（PSO）、全知粒子群优化（FIPSO）、量子粒子群优化（QPSO）以及Adam辅助的FIPSO变体。结果表明，与Adam、COBYLA和SPSA等标准优化器相比，这些方法实现了更低的近似间隙和更稳定的收敛。特别地，我们观察到群智能方法在噪声和散粒噪声受限条件下仍保持优越性能。这些发现表明，基于种群的搜索能有效导航复杂的QAOA景观，是近期量子算法中参数优化的有前景方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of efficiently initializing variational parameters in the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) for solving Max Cut problems. The authors propose using swarm optimization algorithms, including Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), Fully Informed Particle Swarm Optimization (FIPSO), Quantum Particle Swarm Optimization (QPSO), and an Adam-assisted FIPSO variant, to robustly explore the QAOA parameter space. Experimental results on weighted MaxCut instances across various system sizes, circuit depths, and noise regimes demonstrate that these swarm methods achieve lower approximation gaps and more stable convergence than standard optimizers like Adam, COBYLA, and SPSA, particularly under noisy and shot-limited conditions, indicating that population-based search is effective for navigating the complex QAOA landscape.
该论文针对量子近似优化算法（QAOA）中变分参数初始化的难题，以解决最大割问题为动机，提出了使用群智能优化算法（包括粒子群优化PSO、全知粒子群优化FIPSO、量子粒子群优化QPSO以及Adam辅助的FIPSO变体）来鲁棒地探索QAOA参数空间。实验在加权最大割实例上，针对不同系统规模、电路深度和噪声环境（包括散粒噪声）进行，结果表明这些群智能方法相比Adam、COBYLA和SPSA等标准优化器，能实现更低的近似比差距和更稳定的收敛，尤其在噪声和有限采样条件下表现更优，说明基于种群的搜索策略能有效导航复杂的QAOA参数空间。
Policy Gradient Primal-Dual Method for Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback
Authors: Qiang Liu, Adrienne Kline, Ermin Wei
First: 2026-04-21T03:20:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:20:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (Safe RLHF) has recently achieved empirical success in developing helpful and harmless large language models by decoupling human preferences regarding helpfulness and harmlessness. Existing approaches typically rely on fitting fixed horizon reward models from human feedback and have only been validated empirically. In this paper, we formulate safe RLHF as an infinite horizon discounted Con- strained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), since humans may interact with the model over a continuing sequence of interactions rather than within a single finite episode. We propose two Safe RLHF algorithms that do not require reward model fitting and, in contrast to prior work assuming fixed-length trajectories, support flexible trajectory lengths for training. Both algo- rithms are based on the primal-dual method and achieve global convergence guarantees with polynomial rates in terms of policy gradient iterations, trajectory sample lengths, and human preference queries. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to study infinite horizon discounted CMDP under human feedback and establish global, non-asymptotic convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向安全人类反馈强化学习的策略梯度原始-对偶方法
安全人类反馈强化学习（Safe RLHF）通过解耦人类对有用性和无害性的偏好，近期在开发有用且无害的大语言模型方面取得了实证成功。现有方法通常依赖从人类反馈中拟合固定时域奖励模型，且仅经过实证验证。本文中，我们将Safe RLHF建模为无限时域折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP），因为人类可能在与模型的持续交互序列中而非单一有限回合内进行交互。我们提出两种无需拟合奖励模型的Safe RLHF算法，与假设固定长度轨迹的先前工作不同，这两种算法支持灵活的训练轨迹长度。两种算法均基于原始-对偶方法，并在策略梯度迭代次数、轨迹样本长度和人类偏好查询次数方面实现了多项式速率的全局收敛保证。据我们所知，这是首个研究人类反馈下无限时域折扣CMDP并建立全局非渐近收敛性的工作。
