This paper addresses Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (Safe RLHF) by formulating it as an infinite horizon discounted Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), motivated by the need to model continuing human-model interactions beyond fixed finite episodes. The authors propose two primal-dual algorithms that avoid fitting reward models and support flexible trajectory lengths, unlike prior work. Theoretically, they prove global convergence with polynomial rates in policy gradient iterations, sample lengths, and human queries, marking the first study to establish non-asymptotic convergence for infinite horizon CMDP under human feedback.
本文针对基于人类反馈的安全强化学习（Safe RLHF）问题，将其建模为无限时域折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP），以模拟人类与模型之间持续交互而非固定有限回合的场景。作者提出了两种基于原始-对偶方法的算法，无需拟合奖励模型，并支持灵活轨迹长度，区别于以往依赖固定长度轨迹的研究。理论上，他们证明了算法在策略梯度迭代、轨迹样本长度和人类偏好查询次数上具有多项式速率的全局收敛性，这是首个为无限时域CMDP下人类反馈建立非渐近收敛性的工作。
LEPO: Latent Reasoning Policy Optimization for Large Language Models
Authors: Yuyan Zhou, Jiarui Yu, Hande Dong, Zhezheng Hao, Hong Wang, Jianqing Zhang, Qiang Lin
First: 2026-04-20T07:05:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:14:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recently, latent reasoning has been introduced into large language models (LLMs) to leverage rich information within a continuous space. However, without stochastic sampling, these methods inevitably collapse to deterministic inference, failing to discover diverse reasoning paths. To bridge the gap, we inject controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, restoring LLMs' exploratory capacity and enhancing their compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL). Building on this, we propose \textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO}), a novel framework that applies RL directly to continuous latent representations. Specifically, in rollout stage, LEPO maintains stochasticity to enable diverse trajectory sampling, while in optimization stage, LEPO constructs a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens. Extensive experiments show that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for discrete and latent reasoning.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LEPO, a framework designed to address the limitation of deterministic inference in latent reasoning for large language models by injecting controllable stochasticity via Gumbel-Softmax, which restores exploratory capacity and enhances compatibility with reinforcement learning. The method applies RL directly to continuous latent representations, maintaining stochasticity during rollout for diverse trajectory sampling and constructing a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens during optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for both discrete and latent reasoning tasks.
该论文提出了LEPO框架，旨在通过Gumbel-Softmax注入可控随机性，解决大语言模型潜在推理中确定性推理的局限性，恢复探索能力并增强与强化学习的兼容性。该方法将强化学习直接应用于连续潜在表示，在展开阶段保持随机性以实现多样化轨迹采样，并在优化阶段为潜在表示和离散令牌构建统一的梯度估计。大量实验表明，LEPO在离散和潜在推理任务上均显著优于现有的强化学习方法。
UDM-GRPO: Stable and Efficient Group Relative Policy Optimization for Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models
Authors: Jiaqi Wang, Haoge Deng, Ting Pan, Yang Liu, Chengyuan Wang, Fan Zhang, Yonggang Qi, Xinlong Wang
First: 2026-04-20T17:16:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:05:09+00:00
Comments: Code is available at https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Uniform Discrete Diffusion Model (UDM) has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for discrete generative modeling; however, its integration with reinforcement learning remains largely unexplored. We observe that naively applying GRPO to UDM leads to training instability and marginal performance gains. To address this, we propose UDM-GRPO, the first framework to integrate UDM with RL. Our method is guided by two key insights: (i) treating the final clean sample as the action provides more accurate and stable optimization signals; and (ii) reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process better aligns probability paths with the pretraining distribution. Additionally, we introduce two strategies, Reduced-Step and CFG-Free, to further improve training efficiency. UDM-GRPO significantly improves base model performance across multiple T2I tasks. Notably, GenEval accuracy improves from $69\%$ to $96\%$ and PickScore increases from $20.46$ to $23.81$, achieving state-of-the-art performance in both continuous and discrete settings. On the OCR benchmark, accuracy rises from $8\%$ to $57\%$, further validating the generalization ability of our method. Code is available at https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UDM-GRPO：面向均匀离散扩散模型的稳定高效组相对策略优化
均匀离散扩散模型（UDM）近期作为离散生成建模的一种有前景范式出现，但其与强化学习的结合仍鲜有探索。我们观察到，将GRPO直接应用于UDM会导致训练不稳定且性能提升有限。为此，我们提出UDM-GRPO，这是首个将UDM与强化学习集成的框架。该方法基于两个关键见解：（i）将最终干净样本视为动作，可提供更准确、稳定的优化信号；（ii）通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹，能更好地使概率路径与预训练分布对齐。此外，我们引入两种策略——减少步数和无CFG——以进一步提升训练效率。UDM-GRPO在多个T2I任务上显著提升了基础模型性能。值得注意的是，GenEval准确率从69%提升至96%，PickScore从20.46提升至23.81，在连续和离散设置中均达到最先进性能。在OCR基准上，准确率从8%提升至57%，进一步验证了方法的泛化能力。代码见https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of integrating reinforcement learning with Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models (UDM), where naive application of GRPO leads to instability and limited gains. The proposed UDM-GRPO framework introduces two key innovations: treating the final clean sample as the action for more stable optimization, and reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process to align with the pretraining distribution. Additionally, Reduced-Step and CFG-Free strategies improve training efficiency. Experiments on text-to-image tasks show significant improvements, with GenEval accuracy rising from 69% to 96% and PickScore from 20.46 to 23.81, achieving state-of-the-art results. On the OCR benchmark, accuracy increases from 8% to 57%, demonstrating strong generalization.
该论文针对均匀离散扩散模型（UDM）与强化学习结合时，直接应用GRPO导致训练不稳定且性能提升有限的问题，提出了首个集成框架UDM-GRPO。方法基于两个关键洞察：将最终干净样本作为动作以提供更准确的优化信号，以及通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹以对齐预训练分布。此外，引入Reduced-Step和CFG-Free策略提升训练效率。在文本到图像任务中，GenEval准确率从69%提升至96%，PickScore从20.46增至23.81，达到连续和离散设置下的最优性能。OCR基准测试中准确率从8%升至57%，进一步验证了方法的泛化能力。
Guiding Distribution Matching Distillation with Gradient-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Linwei Dong, Ruoyu Guo, Ge Bai, Zehuan Yuan, Yawei Luo, Changqing Zou
First: 2026-04-21T02:57:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T02:57:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion distillation, exemplified by Distribution Matching Distillation (DMD), has shown great promise in few-step generation but often sacrifices quality for sampling speed. While integrating Reinforcement Learning (RL) into distillation offers potential, a naive fusion of these two objectives relies on suboptimal raw sample evaluation. This sample-based scoring creates inherent conflicts with the distillation trajectory and produces unreliable rewards due to the noisy nature of early-stage generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose GDMD, a novel framework that redefines the reward mechanism by prioritizing distillation gradients over raw pixel outputs as the primary signal for optimization. By reinterpreting the DMD gradients as implicit target tensors, our framework enables existing reward models to directly evaluate the quality of distillation updates. This gradient-level guidance functions as an adaptive weighting that synchronizes the RL policy with the distillation objective, effectively neutralizing optimization divergence. Empirical results show that GDMD sets a new SOTA for few-step generation. Specifically, our 4-step models outperform the quality of their multi-step teacher and substantially exceed previous DMDR results in GenEval and human-preference metrics, exhibiting strong scalability potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于梯度强化学习的分布匹配蒸馏引导
扩散蒸馏（以分布匹配蒸馏DMD为代表）在少步生成中展现出巨大潜力，但常以牺牲质量为代价换取采样速度。尽管将强化学习（RL）融入蒸馏具有潜力，但简单融合这两个目标依赖于次优的原始样本评估。这种基于样本的评分与蒸馏轨迹存在固有冲突，且由于早期生成阶段的噪声特性会产生不可靠的奖励。为克服这些局限，我们提出GDMD——一种新颖框架，通过优先将蒸馏梯度而非原始像素输出作为优化信号来重新定义奖励机制。通过将DMD梯度重新解释为隐式目标张量，我们的框架使现有奖励模型能够直接评估蒸馏更新的质量。这种梯度级引导充当自适应权重，使RL策略与蒸馏目标同步，有效中和优化发散。实验结果表明，GDMD在少步生成中达到了新的最优水平。具体而言，我们的4步模型在质量上超越了多步教师模型，并在GenEval和人类偏好指标上大幅超过先前DMDR结果，展现出强大的可扩展潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the quality degradation in few-step diffusion distillation, where methods like Distribution Matching Distillation (DMD) trade off generation quality for speed. The authors propose GDMD, a framework that integrates gradient-based reinforcement learning by reinterpreting DMD gradients as implicit target tensors, allowing reward models to evaluate distillation updates directly and synchronize the RL policy with the distillation objective. Experimental results show that GDMD achieves state-of-the-art performance, with 4-step models surpassing the quality of multi-step teachers and significantly improving over previous DMD results on GenEval and human-preference metrics, demonstrating strong scalability.
该论文针对少步扩散蒸馏中质量下降的问题，即分布匹配蒸馏（DMD）等方法以牺牲生成质量换取采样速度。作者提出GDMD框架，通过将DMD梯度重新解释为隐式目标张量，使奖励模型直接评估蒸馏更新质量，从而将基于梯度的强化学习与蒸馏目标同步。实验结果表明，GDMD实现了最先进的性能，其4步模型在质量上超越多步教师模型，并在GenEval和人类偏好指标上显著优于先前DMD结果，展现出强大的可扩展性潜力。
SAVOIR: Learning Social Savoir-Faire via Shapley-based Reward Attribution
Authors: Xiachong Feng, Yi Jiang, Xiaocheng Feng, Deyi Yin, Libo Qin, Yangfan Ye, Lei Huang, Weitao Ma, Yuxuan Gu, Chonghan Qin, Bing Qin, Lingpeng Kong
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-21T02:08:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T02:08:25+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Social intelligence, the ability to navigate complex interpersonal interactions, presents a fundamental challenge for language agents. Training such agents via reinforcement learning requires solving the credit assignment problem: determining how individual utterances contribute to multi-turn dialogue outcomes. Existing approaches directly employ language models to distribute episode-level rewards, yielding attributions that are retrospective and lack theoretical grounding. We propose SAVOIR (ShApley Value fOr SocIal RL), a novel principled framework grounded in cooperative game theory. Our approach combines two complementary principles: expected utility shifts evaluation from retrospective attribution to prospective valuation, capturing an utterance's strategic potential for enabling favorable future trajectories; Shapley values ensure fair credit distribution with axiomatic guarantees of efficiency, symmetry, and marginality. Experiments on the SOTOPIA benchmark demonstrate that SAVOIR achieves new state-of-the-art performance across all evaluation settings, with our 7B model matching or exceeding proprietary models including GPT-4o and Claude-3.5-Sonnet. Notably, even large reasoning models consistently underperform, suggesting social intelligence requires qualitatively different capabilities than analytical reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAVOIR：基于沙普利奖励归因的社交礼仪学习
社交智能——驾驭复杂人际互动的能力——对语言智能体构成了根本性挑战。通过强化学习训练此类智能体需要解决信用分配问题：即确定单个话语如何影响多轮对话结果。现有方法直接使用语言模型分配回合级奖励，导致归因具有回顾性且缺乏理论基础。我们提出SAVOIR（ShApley Value fOr SocIal RL），一个基于合作博弈论的新型原则性框架。该方法结合两个互补原则：期望效用将评估从回顾性归因转向前瞻性估值，捕捉话语在促成有利未来轨迹方面的战略潜力；沙普利值通过效率、对称性和边际性的公理保证实现公平信用分配。在SOTOPIA基准上的实验表明，SAVOIR在所有评估设置中均达到新的最先进性能，我们的7B模型匹配或超越包括GPT-4o和Claude-3.5-Sonnet在内的专有模型。值得注意的是，即使是大型推理模型也持续表现不佳，这表明社交智能需要与分析推理本质上不同的能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of credit assignment in reinforcement learning for training socially intelligent language agents, where existing methods lack theoretical grounding by using language models for retrospective reward attribution. The authors propose SAVOIR, a framework based on cooperative game theory that combines expected utility for prospective valuation of utterances and Shapley values for fair, axiomatically guaranteed credit distribution. Experiments on the SOTOPIA benchmark show that SAVOIR achieves state-of-the-art performance, with a 7B model matching or exceeding proprietary models like GPT-4o and Claude-3.5-Sonnet, while large reasoning models underperform, indicating social intelligence requires distinct capabilities from analytical reasoning.
该论文针对强化学习中训练社交智能语言代理的信用分配问题，现有方法依赖语言模型进行回顾性奖励分配，缺乏理论依据。作者提出SAVOIR框架，基于合作博弈论，结合预期效用进行前瞻性话语估值和沙普利值实现公平、公理保证的信用分配。在SOTOPIA基准上的实验表明，SAVOIR在所有评估设置中达到最先进性能，其7B模型匹配或超越GPT-4o和Claude-3.5-Sonnet等专有模型，而大型推理模型表现不佳，表明社交智能需要与分析推理不同的能力。
Low-Rank Adaptation for Critic Learning in Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuan Zhuang, Yuexin Bian, Sihong He, Jie Feng, Qing Su, Songyang Han, Jonathan Petit, Shihao Ji, Yuanyuan Shi, Fei Miao
First: 2026-04-21T01:59:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T01:59:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling critic capacity is a promising direction for enhancing off-policy reinforcement learning (RL). However, larger critics are prone to overfitting and unstable in replay-buffer-based bootstrap training. This paper leverages Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) as a structural-sparsity regularizer for off-policy critics. Our approach freezes randomly initialized base matrices and solely optimizes low-rank adapters, thereby constraining critic updates to a low-dimensional subspace. Built on top of SimbaV2, we further develop a LoRA formulation, compatible with SimbaV2, that preserves its hyperspherical normalization geometry under frozen-backbone training. We evaluate our method with SAC and FastTD3 on DeepMind Control locomotion and IsaacLab robotics benchmarks. LoRA consistently achieves lower critic loss during training and stronger policy performance. Extensive experiments demonstrate that adaptive low-rank updates provide a simple, scalable, and effective structural regularization for critic learning in off-policy RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离策略强化学习中评论家学习的低秩适应方法
扩展评论家容量是提升离策略强化学习的一个有前景的方向。然而，较大的评论家容易过拟合，并且在基于回放缓冲区的自举训练中不稳定。本文利用低秩适应作为离策略评论家的结构稀疏正则化器。我们的方法冻结随机初始化的基矩阵，仅优化低秩适配器，从而将评论家更新约束在低维子空间内。基于SimbaV2，我们进一步开发了一种与SimbaV2兼容的低秩适应公式，在冻结骨干训练下保留其超球面归一化几何结构。我们使用SAC和FastTD3在DeepMind Control运动控制和IsaacLab机器人基准上评估了该方法。低秩适应在训练过程中始终实现更低的评论家损失和更强的策略性能。大量实验表明，自适应低秩更新为离策略强化学习中的评论家学习提供了一种简单、可扩展且有效的结构正则化方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of scaling critic networks in off-policy reinforcement learning, where larger critics often suffer from overfitting and instability due to bootstrap training with replay buffers. The authors propose using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) as a structural-sparsity regularizer, which freezes randomly initialized base matrices and optimizes only low-rank adapters to constrain updates to a low-dimensional subspace. Built on SimbaV2, the method preserves hyperspherical normalization geometry under frozen-backbone training. Evaluated with SAC and FastTD3 on DeepMind Control locomotion and IsaacLab robotics benchmarks, LoRA consistently achieves lower critic loss during training and stronger policy performance, demonstrating effective structural regularization.
该论文针对离策略强化学习中评论家网络规模扩展的挑战，指出大型评论家因基于回放缓冲区的自举训练而易出现过拟合和不稳定问题。作者提出利用低秩适应（LoRA）作为结构稀疏正则化器，冻结随机初始化的基矩阵并仅优化低秩适配器，从而将评论家更新约束在低维子空间中。该方法基于SimbaV2构建，在冻结骨干训练下保留超球面归一化几何结构。在DeepMind Control运动控制和IsaacLab机器人基准测试中，使用SAC和FastTD3进行评估，LoRA在训练期间持续实现更低的评论家损失和更强的策略性能，展示了有效的结构正则化效果。
Self-Improving Tabular Language Models via Iterative Group Alignment
Authors: Yunbo Long, Tejumade Afonja, Alexandra Brintrup, Mario Fritz
First: 2026-04-21T01:29:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T01:29:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While language models have been adapted for tabular data generation, two fundamental limitations remain: (1) static fine-tuning produces models that cannot learn from their own generated samples and adapt to self-correct, and (2) autoregressive objectives preserve local token coherence but neglect global statistical properties, degrading tabular quality. Reinforcement learning offers a potential solution but requires designing reward functions that balance competing objectives -- impractical for tabular data. To fill the gap, we introduce TabGRAA (Tabular Group-Relative Advantage Alignment), the first self-improving framework for tabular data generation via automated feedback. At each iteration, TabGRAA uses an \emph{automated quality signal} -- such as a two-sample distinguishability classifier or a distance-based reward -- to partition newly generated samples into high- and low-quality groups, then optimizes a group-relative advantage objective that reinforces realistic patterns while penalizing artifacts. The specific signal is a modular choice rather than a fixed component of the framework. This establishes a virtuous feedback cycle, where the quality signal is re-computed against newly \emph{generated synthetic} samples at each round; the language model is only fine-tuned on these self-generated signals, so no additional real record is exposed during alignment, mitigating data-leakage risk beyond the initial supervised fine-tuning. Experiments show TabGRAA outperforms existing methods in fidelity, utility, and privacy, while matching or exceeding diffusion-based synthesizers, advancing tabular synthesis from static statistical replication to dynamic, self-improving generation.
Summary / 总结
Tabular language models suffer from static fine-tuning that prevents self-correction and autoregressive objectives that neglect global statistical properties. To address this, the authors propose TabGRAA, a self-improving framework that uses an automated quality signal, such as a two-sample distinguishability classifier, to partition generated samples into high- and low-quality groups and optimizes a group-relative advantage objective. Experiments demonstrate that TabGRAA outperforms existing methods in fidelity, utility, and privacy, matching or exceeding diffusion-based synthesizers while enabling dynamic self-improvement.
表格语言模型存在静态微调无法自我纠正以及自回归目标忽略全局统计特性的问题。为此，作者提出TabGRAA，一种通过自动质量信号（如两样本可区分性分类器）将生成样本划分为高质量和低质量组，并优化组相对优势目标的自改进框架。实验表明，TabGRAA在保真度、实用性和隐私性上优于现有方法，达到或超越基于扩散的合成器，实现了动态自改进生成。
Reasoning Structure Matters for Safety Alignment of Reasoning Models
Authors: Yeonjun In, Wonjoong Kim, Sangwu Park, Chanyoung Park
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-21T00:50:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T00:50:13+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models (LRMs) achieve strong performance on complex reasoning tasks but often generate harmful responses to malicious user queries. This paper investigates the underlying cause of these safety risks and shows that the issue lies in the reasoning structure itself. Based on this insight, we claim that effective safety alignment can be achieved by altering the reasoning structure. We propose AltTrain, a simple yet effective post training method that explicitly alters the reasoning structure of LRMs. AltTrain is both practical and generalizable, requiring no complex reinforcement learning (RL) training or reward design, only supervised finetuning (SFT) with a lightweight 1K training examples. Experiments across LRM backbones and model sizes demonstrate strong safety alignment, along with robust generalization across reasoning, QA, summarization, and multilingual setting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理结构对推理模型安全对齐的重要性

Summary / 总结

To address this, the authors propose AltTrain, a post-training method that alters the reasoning structure using only supervised finetuning with 1K examples, avoiding complex reinforcement learning. Experiments across various LRM backbones and sizes show that AltTrain achieves strong safety alignment while generalizing well to reasoning, QA, summarization, and multilingual tasks.
该论文研究了大型推理模型的安全风险，发现推理结构本身是导致对恶意查询产生有害响应的根本原因。为此，作者提出了AltTrain，一种通过仅使用1000个示例进行监督微调来改变推理结构的后训练方法，无需复杂的强化学习。在多种推理模型骨干和规模上的实验表明，AltTrain实现了强大的安全对齐，并在推理、问答、摘要和多语言任务中展现出良好的泛化能力。
Fine-Tuning Small Reasoning Models for Quantum Field Theory
Authors: Nathaniel S. Woodward, Zhiqi Gao, Yurii Kvasiuk, Kendrick M. Smith, Frederic Sala, Moritz Münchmeyer
First: 2026-04-21T00:21:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T00:21:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the growing application of Large Language Models (LLMs) to theoretical physics, there is little academic exploration into how domain-specific physics reasoning ability develops while training these models. To investigate this, we perform the first academic fine-tuning study of small (7B-parameter) reasoning models dedicated specifically to theoretical physics. Because open-source verifiable training data required to train such capabilities is scarce, we developed a robust data generation pipeline that can both create synthetic problems and make existing human-authored problems suitable for model training. Selecting Quantum Field Theory (QFT) as our primary domain, we generated over 2,500 synthetic problems alongside a curated collection of human-adapted problems sourced from arXiv and standard pedagogical resources. We conduct both Reinforcement Learning (RL) and Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) experiments, benchmarking performance gains as well as generalization to other physics domains. We perform an extensive analysis of model chains-of-though before and after fine-tuning, to understand how reasoning errors evolve during RL and SFT. Finally, we publicly release our data pipeline, verifiable QFT training data, and $\sim$200M tokens of QFT reasoning traces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：微调小型推理模型用于量子场论
尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在理论物理中的应用日益增长，但关于训练这些模型时特定领域物理推理能力如何发展的学术探索却很少。为此，我们进行了首个针对理论物理的学术微调研究，专注于小型（70亿参数）推理模型。由于训练此类能力所需的开源可验证训练数据稀缺，我们开发了一个稳健的数据生成流程，既能创建合成问题，也能使现有的人类编写问题适用于模型训练。我们选择量子场论（QFT）作为主要领域，生成了超过2500个合成问题，并整理了一批来自arXiv和标准教学资源的人类改编问题。我们进行了强化学习（RL）和监督微调（SFT）实验，评估了性能提升以及对其他物理领域的泛化能力。我们对微调前后的模型思维链进行了广泛分析，以理解在RL和SFT过程中推理错误如何演变。最后，我们公开发布了数据流程、可验证的QFT训练数据以及约2亿个token的QFT推理轨迹。

The authors developed a robust data generation pipeline to create over 2,500 synthetic problems and adapted human-authored problems from arXiv and pedagogical resources, then conducted both Reinforcement Learning (RL) and Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) experiments. 该论文首次对小型70亿参数推理模型进行理论物理（特别是量子场论）领域的学术微调研究，动机源于缺乏领域特定物理推理能力发展的探索。作者开发了稳健的数据生成管道，创建了超过2500个合成问题并改编了来自arXiv和标准教学资源的人类编写问题，随后进行了强化学习和监督微调实验。主要实验结果显示在量子场论任务上性能显著提升，并能泛化到其他物理领域，通过微调前后思维链的深入分析揭示了推理错误演变，同时公开了数据管道、可验证训练数据及约2亿token的量子场论推理轨迹。
From Particles to Perils: SVGD-Based Hazardous Scenario Generation for Autonomous Driving Systems Testing
Authors: Linfeng Liang, Xiao Cheng, Tsong Yueh Chen, Xi Zheng
Venue: Proceedings of the ACM on Software Engineering, Vol. 3, FSE, Article FSE146, July 2026. Article FSE146 (July 2026),
First: 2026-04-20T23:49:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:49:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Simulation-based testing of autonomous driving systems (ADS) must uncover realistic and diverse failures in dense, heterogeneous traffic. However, existing search-based seeding methods (e.g., genetic algorithms) struggle in high-dimensional spaces, often collapsing to limited modes and missing many failure scenarios. We present PtoP, a framework that combines adaptive random seed generation with Stein Variational Gradient Descent (SVGD) to produce diverse, failure-inducing initial conditions. SVGD balances attraction toward high-risk regions and repulsion among particles, yielding risk-seeking yet well-distributed seeds across multiple failure modes. PtoP is plug-and-play and enhances existing online testing methods (e.g., reinforcement learning--based testers) by providing principled seeds. Evaluation in CARLA on two industry-grade ADS (Apollo, Autoware) and a native end-to-end system shows that PtoP improves safety violation rate (up to 27.68%), scenario diversity (9.6%), and map coverage (16.78%) over baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从粒子到风险：基于SVGD的自动驾驶系统测试危险场景生成
基于仿真的自动驾驶系统测试必须在密集异构交通中揭示真实且多样的故障。然而，现有基于搜索的种子生成方法（如遗传算法）在高维空间中表现不佳，常收敛于有限模式，遗漏大量故障场景。我们提出PtoP框架，结合自适应随机种子生成与斯坦因变分梯度下降，生成多样且能诱发故障的初始条件。SVGD平衡了对高风险区域的吸引与粒子间的排斥，产生风险寻求且分布良好的种子，覆盖多种故障模式。PtoP即插即用，通过提供原理性种子增强现有在线测试方法（如基于强化学习的测试器）。在CARLA上对两个工业级自动驾驶系统（Apollo、Autoware）及原生端到端系统的评估表明，PtoP相比基线将安全违规率提升最高27.68%，场景多样性提升9.6%，地图覆盖率提升16.78%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of generating realistic and diverse failure scenarios for simulation-based testing of autonomous driving systems, where existing search-based methods like genetic algorithms often collapse to limited failure modes in high-dimensional spaces. The authors propose PtoP, a framework that combines adaptive random seed generation with Stein Variational Gradient Descent (SVGD), which balances attraction toward high-risk regions and repulsion among particles to produce risk-seeking yet well-distributed initial conditions across multiple failure modes. Evaluated in CARLA on two industry-grade systems (Apollo and Autoware) and a native end-to-end system, PtoP improves safety violation rate by up to 27.68%, scenario diversity by 9.6%, and map coverage by 16.78% over baselines.
该论文针对自动驾驶系统仿真测试中生成真实且多样化失效场景的挑战，指出现有基于搜索的种子生成方法（如遗传算法）在高维空间中容易坍缩到有限模式，遗漏大量失效场景。作者提出PtoP框架，结合自适应随机种子生成与斯坦因变分梯度下降（SVGD），通过平衡向高风险区域的吸引和粒子间的排斥，生成风险寻求且分布均匀的初始条件，覆盖多种失效模式。在CARLA平台上对两个工业级系统（Apollo和Autoware）及一个原生端到端系统的评估显示，PtoP将安全违规率提升高达27.68%，场景多样性提升9.6%，地图覆盖率提升16.78%。
Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Chih-Yu Chang, Qiyuan Chen, Tianhan Gao, David Fenning, Chinedum Okwudire, Neil Dasgupta, Wei Lu, Raed Al Kontar
First: 2026-04-20T23:28:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:28:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Discovering optimal designs through sequential data collection is essential in many real-world applications. While Bayesian Optimization (BO) has achieved remarkable success in this setting, growing attention has recently turned to context-specific optimal design, formalized as Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CBO). Unlike BO, CBO is inherently more challenging as it must approximate an entire mapping from the context space to its corresponding optimal design, requiring simultaneous exploration across contexts and exploitation within each. In many modern applications, such tasks arise across multiple potentially heterogeneous but related clients, where collaboration can significantly improve learning efficiency. We propose CCBO, Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization, a unified framework enabling multiple clients to jointly perform CBO with controllable contexts, supporting both online collaboration and offline initialization from peers' historical beliefs, with an optional privacy-preserving communication mechanism. We establish sublinear regret guarantees and demonstrate, through extensive simulations and a real-world hot rolling application, that CCBO achieves substantial improvements over existing approaches even under client heterogeneity. The code to reproduce the results can be found at https://github.com/cchihyu/Collaborative-Contextual-Bayesian-Optimization
中文标题/摘要
标题：协作式上下文贝叶斯优化
通过顺序数据收集发现最优设计在许多实际应用中至关重要。尽管贝叶斯优化（BO）在此场景中取得了显著成功，但近年来人们越来越关注上下文特定的最优设计，即上下文贝叶斯优化（CBO）。与BO不同，CBO本质上更具挑战性，因为它必须近似整个从上下文空间到其对应最优设计的映射，需要在不同上下文间同时探索并在每个上下文内进行利用。在许多现代应用中，此类任务出现在多个可能异构但相关的客户端之间，协作可以显著提高学习效率。我们提出CCBO，即协作式上下文贝叶斯优化，这是一个统一框架，使多个客户端能够共同执行具有可控上下文的CBO，支持在线协作以及从同伴的历史信念中进行离线初始化，并配备可选的隐私保护通信机制。我们建立了次线性遗憾保证，并通过大量模拟和实际热轧应用证明，即使在客户端异构的情况下，CCBO也比现有方法取得了显著改进。重现结果的代码可在https://github.com/cchihyu/Collaborative-Contextual-Bayesian-Optimization找到。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of context-specific optimal design in sequential data collection, which is formalized as Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CBO) and is more difficult than standard Bayesian Optimization because it requires learning a mapping from contexts to optimal designs through simultaneous exploration and exploitation. The authors propose Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CCBO), a unified framework that enables multiple heterogeneous clients to jointly perform CBO with controllable contexts, supporting online collaboration and offline initialization from peers' historical beliefs, along with an optional privacy-preserving mechanism. Theoretical analysis provides sublinear regret guarantees, and extensive simulations along with a real-world hot rolling application demonstrate that CCBO achieves substantial improvements over existing approaches even under client heterogeneity.
本文针对序列数据收集中上下文特定最优设计的问题，该问题被形式化为上下文贝叶斯优化（CBO），其难度高于标准贝叶斯优化，因为需要同时进行探索和利用来学习从上下文到最优设计的映射。作者提出了协作式上下文贝叶斯优化（CCBO），这是一个统一框架，允许多个可能异构的客户端在可控上下文中联合执行CBO，支持在线协作和基于同伴历史信念的离线初始化，并可选配隐私保护通信机制。理论分析提供了亚线性遗憾保证，大量模拟实验和一个真实的热轧应用表明，即使在客户端异构的情况下，CCBO相比现有方法也能取得显著改进。
RIFT: A RubrIc Failure Mode Taxonomy and Automated Diagnostics
Authors: Zhengyang Qi, Charles Dickens, Derek Pham, Amanda Dsouza, Armin Parchami, Frederic Sala, Paroma Varma
First: 2026-04-01T20:34:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:25:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rubric-based evaluation is widely used in LLM benchmarks and training pipelines for open-ended, less verifiable tasks. While prior work has demonstrated the effectiveness of rubrics using downstream signals such as reinforcement learning outcomes, there remains no principled way to diagnose how a rubric itself fails from such aggregated or downstream signals alone. To address this gap, we introduce RIFT: RubrIc Failure mode Taxonomy, a taxonomy for systematically characterizing failure modes in rubric composition and design. RIFT consists of eight failure modes organized into three high-level categories: Reliability Failures, Content Validity Failures, and Consequential Validity Failures. RIFT is developed using grounded theory by iteratively annotating rubrics drawn from five diverse data sources spanning general instruction following, code generation, creative writing, and expert-level deep research, until no new failure modes are identified. We evaluate the consistency of the taxonomy by measuring agreement among independent human annotators, observing fair agreement overall (87% pairwise agreement and 0.64 average Cohen's kappa). Finally, to support scalable diagnosis, we propose automated rubric quality metrics and show that they align with human failure-mode annotations, achieving up to 0.925 F1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RIFT：一种评分准则失效模式分类体系与自动化诊断方法
基于评分准则的评估广泛用于大语言模型基准测试和训练流程中，以处理开放性强、可验证性低的任务。尽管已有研究通过强化学习结果等下游信号证明了评分准则的有效性，但目前仍缺乏一种原则性方法，仅凭此类聚合或下游信号诊断评分准则本身的失效模式。为填补这一空白，我们提出RIFT：评分准则失效模式分类体系，系统性地刻画评分准则构成与设计中的失效模式。RIFT包含八种失效模式，分为三大类别：可靠性失效、内容效度失效和后果效度失效。RIFT采用扎根理论方法，通过对来自五个不同数据源（涵盖通用指令遵循、代码生成、创意写作及专家级深度研究）的评分准则进行迭代标注，直至未发现新的失效模式。我们通过衡量独立人工标注者间的一致性来评估该分类体系的稳定性，观察到总体中等一致性（成对一致性87%，平均Cohen's kappa系数0.64）。最后，为支持可扩展诊断，我们提出自动化评分准则质量指标，并证明其与人工失效模式标注结果一致，F1值最高达0.925。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces RIFT, a taxonomy for diagnosing failure modes in rubric-based evaluation of LLMs, motivated by the lack of principled methods to identify rubric flaws from aggregated signals. The method involves developing eight failure modes across three categories—Reliability, Content Validity, and Consequential Validity—using grounded theory on rubrics from five diverse sources. Experimental results show fair human annotator agreement (87% pairwise, 0.64 Cohen's kappa) and automated metrics aligning with human annotations, achieving up to 0.925 F1.
该论文提出了RIFT，一个用于诊断基于评分标准的LLM评估中失败模式的分类体系，其动机是缺乏从聚合信号中识别评分标准缺陷的原则性方法。该方法通过扎根理论，从五个不同数据源的评分标准中迭代标注，归纳出八个失败模式，分为可靠性、内容效度和后果效度三类。实验结果显示，人类标注者间达到中等一致性（87%成对一致，Cohen's kappa为0.64），自动指标与人类标注对齐，F1最高达0.925。
